> 2025 年 4 月

Abstract

> **中文：** 摘要

This paper documents a new stylized fact: the cross-sectional variation in CEO pay levels has declined precipitously in recent years. We offer one explanation for this decline: firms are increasingly benchmarking CEO compensation to industry peers closest in size, thereby creating pay clusters. Our empirical tests provide support for this explanation and suggest that the rise of industry-size benchmarking is driven by the combination of three institutional factors: the mandatory disclosure of compensation peer groups, proxy advisory influence, and Say on Pay regulation. Our findings highlight a consequence of adopting a one-size-fits-all standard in the pay-setting process.  
(JEL: G3, G34, G38, M12, M52)

> **中文：** 本文记录了一个新的典型事实：近年来，CEO 薪酬水平的横截面差异急剧下降。我们为这一降幅提供了一种解释：公司越来越多地以规模最接近的行业同业公司作为 CEO 薪酬基准，从而形成薪酬集群。我们的实证检验支持这一解释，并表明行业-规模基准比较的兴起是三个制度因素共同作用的结果：薪酬同业组的强制披露、代理投票顾问的影响以及薪酬话语权投票（Say on Pay）监管。我们的研究结果揭示了在薪酬设定过程中采用“一刀切”标准所产生的一项后果。  
> （JEL：G3, G34, G38, M12, M52）

Keywords: Variation in executive pay; pay dispersion; compensation benchmarking; industry-size benchmarking; pay transparency; pay disclosure; proxy advisers; say on pay

> **中文：** 关键词：高管薪酬差异；薪酬离散度；薪酬基准比较；行业-规模基准比较；薪酬透明度；薪酬披露；代理投票顾问；薪酬话语权投票

We also thank two anonymous reviewers, the AE and the Editors, Philip Bond and Antoinette Schoar. Finally, in compliance with the Journal of Finance disclosure policy, the authors declare that they have nothing to disclose.

> **中文：** \*我们感谢 Eli Fich、Nickolay Gantchev、Peter Iliev、Tomislav Ladika、Paige Ouimet、Shawn Thomas、Vladimir Vladimirov、Alexander Wagner、Su Wang、Jun Yang、Ke Yang，以及 AFA、AAA、SFS Cavalcade、德雷塞尔公司治理会议（早期构想专场）、波士顿学院高管薪酬与公司治理午餐研讨系列的讨论人和研讨会参与者，以及 BI Oslo、布里斯托尔大学、伊拉斯姆斯大学、埃克塞特大学、KEDGE 商学院、兰卡斯特大学、曼彻斯特大学、NHH 挪威经济学院和阿姆斯特丹大学的研讨会参与者。我们还感谢两位匿名审稿人、副主编以及编辑 Philip Bond 和 Antoinette Schoar。最后，根据《Journal of Finance》的披露政策，作者声明无任何事项需要披露。

## Source Page 3

> **中文：** 原文第 3 页

1 . Introduction

> **中文：** 1．引言

This paper documents a new stylized fact: over the last decade, the cross-sectional variation in CEO pay levels has declined precipitously (see Figure 1). Using a wide sample of publicly listed U.S. firms, spanning from 1996 to 2023, we document a decline of almost 40 percent in the cross-sectional variation in CEO pay from 2007 until recent times. The decline in cross-sectional variation in CEO pay levels (henceforth “pay variation” or “pay dispersion”) is due to convergence in pay towards the median in both tails of the pay distribution and holds not only at the economy level but also within industries and industry-size groups. The pattern is empirically robust. The downward trend is also observable in demanding regression analyses using different degrees of data granularity (industry-size-year and firm-year) to control for potential confounding effects. The lower pay dispersion is neither due to a decline in the use of stock options nor due to an increase in the similarity of firm fundamentals; we find the same pattern when we exclude from total compensation the value of granted stock options and the portion of compensation associated with the main economic determinants of CEO pay (i.e., dispersion in “abnormal pay”).

> **中文：** 本文记录了一个新的典型事实：在过去十年间，CEO 薪酬水平的横截面差异急剧下降（见图 1）。我们使用涵盖 1996 年至 2023 年、范围广泛的美国上市公司样本，发现从 2007 年至近期，CEO 薪酬的横截面差异下降了近 40%。CEO 薪酬水平横截面差异的下降（下文称“薪酬差异”或“薪酬离散度”）源于薪酬分布两端均向中位数收敛；这一现象不仅存在于整体经济层面，也存在于行业内部和行业-规模组内部。这一模式在实证上具有稳健性。在使用不同数据粒度（行业-规模-年度和公司-年度）控制潜在混杂效应的严格回归分析中，也可以观察到这一下降趋势。薪酬离散度降低既不是因为股票期权使用减少，也不是因为公司基本面的相似程度提高；当我们从总薪酬中剔除授予股票期权的价值，以及与 CEO 薪酬主要经济决定因素相关的薪酬部分（即考察“异常薪酬”的离散度）时，仍然发现相同模式。

We offer one explanation for this secular decrease in pay variation: the rise of industry-size benchmarking caused by the increased scrutiny of CEO pay by regulators, shareholders, and proxy advisers. That is, compared to previous decades, firms are increasingly benchmarking CEO compensation to the industry peers closest in size. The adoption of such a uniform criterion across the economy can result in lower pay variation across firms to the extent that the policy generates “clusters” of compensation peers in which firms benchmark their pay to one another. As firms typically target pay at the median of their peers’ pay, the practice of pay targeting inevitably reduces pay variation within such clusters which, as we show below, can also reduce economy-wide pay dispersion.

> **中文：** 我们为薪酬差异的这一长期下降提供了一种解释：监管机构、股东和代理投票顾问对 CEO 薪酬的审查日益加强，推动了行业-规模基准比较的兴起。换言之，与此前数十年相比，公司越来越多地以规模最接近的行业同业公司作为 CEO 薪酬基准。在整个经济中采用这种统一标准可能降低公司之间的薪酬差异，因为该政策会形成若干薪酬同业公司的“集群”，集群内的公司相互参照来确定薪酬。由于公司通常将薪酬目标设定在同业公司薪酬的中位数，薪酬目标设定的做法必然会降低此类集群内部的薪酬差异；正如下文所示，这也可能降低整体经济范围内的薪酬离散度。

We examine the factors driving the growth of industry-size benchmarking and find that it is largely driven by three recent institutional developments: the 2006 SEC rule mandating the disclosure of peer groups used for compensation benchmarking, the growing influence of proxy advisors that favor industry-size benchmarks for CEO pay, and the introduction of

> **中文：** 我们考察了推动行业-规模基准比较发展的因素，发现其主要受到近期三项制度发展的推动：美国证券交易委员会（SEC）于 2006 年颁布的规则要求强制披露用于薪酬基准比较的同业组；偏好以行业-规模为 CEO 薪酬基准的代理投票顾问影响力日益增强；以及

1

> **中文：** 1

<!-- page:4 -->

## Source Page 4

> **中文：** 原文第 4 页

say on pay regulation. The confluence of these institutional developments—which enabled greater scrutiny of firms’ pay practices by shareholders and proxy advisors—increased pressure on boards to conform to a standardized pay-setting process. This, in turn, led to the adoption of uniform criteria such as industry-size benchmarking.

> **中文：** 薪酬话语权投票监管的引入。这些制度发展共同发挥作用，使股东和代理投票顾问能够更加严格地审查公司的薪酬实践，从而加大了董事会遵循标准化薪酬设定流程的压力。这进而促使公司采用行业-规模基准比较等统一标准。

Our findings highlight the implications of applying a uniform criterion—such as industry-size benchmarking—in the executive pay-setting process. On the one hand, increased transparency, coupled with standardized criteria, may facilitate the evaluation of pay practices and promote greater accountability. Moreover, uniformity in pay-setting may enhance perceptions of fairness in CEO compensation design, a key concern for directors and investors (Edmans, Gosling and Jenter, 2023). On the other hand, institutional pressure from regulators and investors to make CEO pay more transparent and standardized may lead boards to prioritize compliance over customization. As a result, firms may adopt a “one-size-fits-all” approach that sacrifices alignment with firm- and executive-specific needs, potentially leading to suboptimal incentive structures and inefficiencies. By documenting how adherence to standardized benchmarks contributes to a decline in cross-sectional pay variation, our results underscore the importance of better understanding how institutional and market pressures influence CEO pay—both in terms of overall pay levels and dispersion.

> **中文：** 我们的研究结果揭示了在高管薪酬设定过程中采用行业-规模基准比较等统一标准所产生的影响。一方面，提高透明度并辅以标准化准则，可能有助于评估薪酬实践并促进问责。此外，薪酬设定的统一性可能会增强人们对 CEO 薪酬设计公平性的认知，而公平性正是董事和投资者重点关注的问题（Edmans, Gosling and Jenter, 2023）。另一方面，监管机构和投资者要求提高 CEO 薪酬透明度和标准化程度的制度压力，可能导致董事会将合规置于定制化之上。因此，公司可能采用“一刀切”的方法，以牺牲与公司及高管特定需求的契合度为代价，并可能导致次优的激励结构和效率损失。通过记录遵循标准化基准如何促使薪酬横截面差异下降，我们的结果强调了更深入理解制度压力和市场压力如何影响 CEO 薪酬的重要性，这既包括对总体薪酬水平的影响，也包括对薪酬离散度的影响。

To examine the empirical validity of our proposed explanation for the documented decline in pay dispersion—namely, the widespread adoption of a uniform peer selection criterion based on industry affiliation and firm size—we conduct three sets of analyses. As a first step, we simulate the evolution of pay dispersion under the assumption that all firms adopt an industry-size-based benchmarking approach. We find that simulated pay dispersion declines substantially, lending support to the notion that industry-size benchmarking contributes to the observed reduction in pay dispersion. This simulation is informative because the effect of clustered compensation networks on economy-wide pay dispersion is not ex ante obvious: it depends on the number and size of benchmarking groups (e.g., industry-size groups), changes in the cross-sectional distribution of firm size and industry affiliation (which can be driven by entry, exit, growth, or other dynamics), and residual cross-group connections through

> **中文：** 为了检验我们对已记录的薪酬离散度下降所提出解释的实证有效性，即广泛采用以行业归属和公司规模为基础的统一同业公司选择标准，我们开展了三组分析。第一步，我们在假设所有公司均采用基于行业-规模的基准比较方法的前提下，模拟薪酬离散度的演变。我们发现，模拟得到的薪酬离散度显著下降，这支持了行业-规模基准比较促成实际观察到的薪酬离散度下降这一观点。这项模拟具有信息价值，因为集群化薪酬网络对整体经济薪酬离散度的影响在事前并不显而易见：它取决于基准比较组（例如行业-规模组）的数量和规模、公司规模与行业归属横截面分布的变化（这种变化可能由进入、退出、增长或其他动态因素推动），以及通过以下渠道形成的残余跨组联系：

2

> **中文：** 2

<!-- page:5 -->

## Source Page 5

> **中文：** 原文第 5 页

which pay shocks may propagate.

> **中文：** 薪酬冲击可能经由这些联系传播。

In our second set of tests, we use regression analyses to examine whether the decrease in pay dispersion goes hand in hand with the increasing tendency to benchmark CEO compensation to the industry peers closest in size. The results reveal that, over time, compensation peer groups exhibit less dispersion in size, are less likely to deviate from the industry-size criterion, and show greater compliance with the industry-size based peer selection methodology adopted by ISS (i.e., the largest proxy advisory firm). Critically, these patterns are strongly associated with our results on pay dispersion both in the time-series and the cross-section.

> **中文：** 在第二组检验中，我们使用回归分析考察薪酬离散度下降是否与越来越倾向于以规模最接近的行业同业公司作为 CEO 薪酬基准的趋势相伴发生。结果显示，随着时间推移，薪酬同业组内部的规模离散度有所降低，偏离行业-规模标准的可能性下降，并且更加符合 ISS（即规模最大的代理投票顾问公司）所采用的基于行业-规模的同业公司选择方法。关键在于，无论是在时间序列还是横截面上，这些模式都与我们关于薪酬离散度的结果密切相关。

In a third set of tests, we provide plausibly causal evidence on how three recent institutional developments—namely the 2006 SEC rule that mandated the disclosure of the peers used for compensation benchmarking, the influence of proxy advisors, and the introduction of say on pay regulation—have jointly contributed to the rise of industry-size benchmarking. Regarding the 2006 SEC pay disclosure mandate, we find that the decrease in pay dispersion starts after the implementation of the disclosure mandate that increased transparency about the pay setting process, not before. Also consistent with the disclosure mandate playing a role in the documented patterns, we observe that the increasing tendency to adopt industry-size benchmarking is stronger among firms whose compensation peer groups exhibit larger deviations from this criterion right before the introduction of the regulation (which was relatively unexpected). In a series of falsification tests, we do not find a decline in pay dispersion based on settings in which the 2006 SEC disclosure mandate plays a less prominent role: among non-US public firms, among private U.S. firms, and among senior executives outside the top 5 in public U.S. firms (whose pay is typically not determined via compensation benchmarking).

> **中文：** 在第三组检验中，我们就近期三项制度发展如何共同推动行业-规模基准比较的兴起，提供了具有合理因果解释的证据。这三项制度发展分别是：SEC 于 2006 年颁布的规则要求强制披露用于薪酬基准比较的同业公司、代理投票顾问的影响，以及薪酬话语权投票监管的引入。关于 2006 年 SEC 的薪酬披露要求，我们发现，薪酬离散度是在提高薪酬设定流程透明度的披露要求实施之后才开始下降，而非在此之前。与披露要求在所记录模式中发挥作用的解释一致，我们还观察到，在该项监管出台前夕（这项监管的出台相对出人意料），薪酬同业组对行业-规模标准偏离程度较大的公司，其采用行业-规模基准比较的趋势增强得更为明显。在一系列证伪检验中，对于 2006 年 SEC 披露要求作用相对较弱的情境，我们没有发现薪酬离散度下降；这些情境包括非美国上市公司、美国私营公司，以及美国上市公司中排名前 5 位之外的高级管理人员（其薪酬通常并非通过薪酬基准比较确定）。

Regarding the role of proxy advisers, we document that a firm’s probability of including a potential peer critically varies with the degree of conformity the peer has with ISS’s policy for compensation benchmarking, which we measure using peer rankings produced by ISS’s publicly disclosed methodology. But perhaps more importantly in terms of explaining the documented increase in industry-size benchmarking, we find that this association strengthens

> **中文：** 关于代理投票顾问的作用，我们发现，一家公司将某家潜在同业公司纳入同业组的概率，会显著地随该潜在同业公司符合 ISS 薪酬基准比较政策的程度而变化；我们使用依据 ISS 公开披露的方法生成的同业公司排名来衡量这种符合程度。不过，就解释已记录的行业-规模基准比较增长而言，或许更为重要的是，我们发现这种关联有所增强，

3

> **中文：** 3

<!-- page:6 -->

## Source Page 6

> **中文：** 原文第 6 页

significantly over the sample period. The association also shows a discontinuity around an arbitrary peer group size cutoff used in ISS’s peer selection methodology, reinforcing the causal role of ISS’s industry-size criterion. In placebo tests, this discontinuity is absent in years prior to the introduction of ISS’s policy. Further supporting proxy advisor influence, we find that firms are more likely to add or drop peers in line with ISS’s prior-year recommendations, including around the arbitrary cutoff where peers are otherwise similar. Finally, we show that industry-size benchmarking becomes more prevalent as passive ownership increases, consistent with the notion that passive investors—who face higher costs of active engagement—rely more heavily on proxy advisor guidance.

> **中文：** 并且这种增强在样本期内十分显著。这种关联还在 ISS 同业公司选择方法所采用的任意同业组规模阈值附近呈现不连续性，进一步强化了 ISS 行业-规模标准发挥因果作用的解释。在安慰剂检验中，ISS 政策出台之前的年份并不存在这种不连续性。进一步支持代理投票顾问具有影响力的是，我们发现，公司更有可能按照 ISS 上一年度的建议增加或剔除同业公司，包括在该任意阈值附近的情形，而在其他方面，这些同业公司彼此相似。最后，我们表明，随着被动投资者持股比例上升，行业-规模基准比较变得更加普遍；这与被动投资者因积极参与的成本更高而更加依赖代理投票顾问指导的观点一致。

Regarding the influence of Say on Pay (SOP) regulation, we find that, following weak SOP vote support, firms increase the conformity of their compensation peer groups with the industry-size benchmarking criterion.1 To sharpen identification, we exploit exogenous variation in the frequency of SOP voting; conceivably, a higher frequency of SOP votes puts more pressure on firms to accommodate compensation practices to standard governance criteria. We compare firms whose shareholders voted for a 1-year SOP vote frequency to those whose shareholders voted for a 3-year SOP vote frequency by a narrow margin in their first mandatory shareholder vote on the frequency of SOP voting. We find that firms whose shareholders narrowly voted for a 1-year frequency exhibit greater conformity in the years after the vote (but not before) with the industry-size benchmarking criterion than those in which the voting outcome was narrowly in favor of a 3-year frequency. These results support a causal role for SOP advisory votes in encouraging the adoption of industry-size benchmarking.

> **中文：** 关于薪酬话语权投票（SOP）监管的影响，我们发现，在 SOP 投票支持率较低之后，公司会提高其薪酬同业组对行业-规模基准比较标准的符合程度。1 为增强识别力度，我们利用 SOP 投票频率的外生差异；可以设想，更高的 SOP 投票频率会对公司施加更大压力，促使其薪酬实践适应标准化的治理准则。我们比较了两类公司：在首次就 SOP 投票频率举行的强制性股东投票中，一类公司的股东以微弱优势支持每 1 年举行一次 SOP 投票，另一类公司的股东则以微弱优势支持每 3 年举行一次 SOP 投票。我们发现，与投票结果以微弱优势支持每 3 年一次的公司相比，股东以微弱优势支持每 1 年一次的公司，在投票之后的年份中对行业-规模基准比较标准的符合程度更高，但投票之前并不存在这种差异。这些结果支持 SOP 咨询性投票在促进采用行业-规模基准比较方面发挥因果作用。

Our study contributes to the literature studying the evolution of compensation practices over time. This prior work focuses on the mean of the cross-sectional distribution of CEO pay levels (e.g., Jensen and Murphy, 1990; Hall and Liebman, 1998; Murphy, 1999; Bebchuk and Grinstein, 2005; Gabaix and Landier, 2008; Frydman and Jenter, 2010; Frydman and Saks, 2010; Shue and Townsend, 2017). Instead, we examine the variation in the cross-

> **中文：** 本研究对考察薪酬实践如何随时间演变的文献作出了贡献。既有研究主要关注 CEO 薪酬水平横截面分布的均值（例如 Jensen and Murphy, 1990; Hall and Liebman, 1998; Murphy, 1999; Bebchuk and Grinstein, 2005; Gabaix and Landier, 2008; Frydman and Jenter, 2010; Frydman and Saks, 2010; Shue and Townsend, 2017）。与之不同，我们考察的是 CEO 薪酬水平横截面

1To illustrate the dynamics between the board, shareholders, and proxy advisers around a weak SOP vote, we provide two anecdotes in the internet appendix in which boards discuss weak SOP vote outcomes, the subsequent changes to their compensation peer groups, and the underlying rationales thereof.

> **中文：** 1 为说明 SOP 投票支持率较低时董事会、股东与代理投票顾问之间的互动，我们在网络附录中提供了两个实例。在这些实例中，董事会讨论了较低的 SOP 投票支持率、随后对薪酬同业组作出的调整，以及这些调整背后的理由。

> **中文：** 4

> **中文：** 原文第 7 页

sectional distribution of CEO pay levels. In contrast to the secular increase in the mean of the cross-sectional distribution of CEO pay, we document a stark decline in the variation of this distribution in recent years. We propose one driver of the documented decrease in pay dispersion—industry-size benchmarking—but there could be others.

> **中文：** 分布的差异。与 CEO 薪酬横截面分布均值的长期上升形成对照的是，我们发现近年来这一分布的差异显著下降。我们提出了一个推动已记录薪酬离散度下降的因素，即行业-规模基准比较，但也可能存在其他因素。

Two notable recent contributions to this literature are Cabezon (2025) and Kalpathy, Nanda and Zhao (2024). Cabezon (2025) documents that the structure of compensation contracts has become more similar across firms since 2006, with companies relying on more similar compensation vehicles such as a similar fraction of pay in equity. However, greater similarity in the compensation vehicles does not imply less dispersion in pay levels. For example, firms could increase total compensation to offset utility losses associated with diminished flexibility in contract tailoring. Moreover, Cabezon’s analysis is not concerned with compensation peer groups but with the average similarity between a focal firm’s contract and the contracts of all other firms in the economy. In contrast, our study investigates the rise of industry-size benchmarking and the institutional forces behind its growing prevalence. Kalpathy, Nanda and Zhao (2024) provide complementary evidence that lower-profile, agency-prone firms tend to herd toward “star” peers in peer group selection to avoid shareholder scrutiny. While their focus is on opportunistic peer selection, our analysis highlights broader structural changes in peer benchmarking, emphasizing the influence of standardized criteria and the institutional pressures driving their adoption.

> **中文：** 该领域近期两项值得注意的研究是 Cabezon (2025) 和 Kalpathy, Nanda and Zhao (2024)。Cabezon (2025) 发现，自 2006 年以来，不同公司的薪酬合同结构变得更加相似，公司越来越依赖相似的薪酬工具，例如在薪酬中采用相近比例的权益薪酬。然而，薪酬工具更加相似并不意味着薪酬水平的离散度更低。例如，公司可能提高总薪酬，以抵消合同定制灵活性下降所带来的效用损失。此外，Cabezon 的分析关注的并非薪酬同业组，而是核心公司的合同与整体经济中所有其他公司合同之间的平均相似程度。相比之下，本研究考察行业-规模基准比较的兴起及其日益普及背后的制度力量。Kalpathy, Nanda and Zhao (2024) 提供了补充证据，表明知名度较低且更容易产生代理问题的公司，在选择同业组时往往会追随“明星”同业公司，以规避股东审查。他们关注的是机会主义同业公司选择，而我们的分析揭示了同业基准比较中更广泛的结构性变化，并强调标准化准则的影响以及推动公司采用这些准则的制度压力。

We also contribute to the broader discussion on the costs and benefits of increased transparency and scrutiny in corporate pay-setting processes (Mas, 2016; Baker et al., 2019; Bennedsen et al., 2022; Babenko, Bennett and Wang, 2025). Specifically, we show how regulations designed to enhance shareholder oversight can encourage the adoption of one-size-fits-all compensation practices, thereby highlighting a potential unintended consequence of well-intentioned governance reforms.

> **中文：** 我们还对有关提高公司薪酬设定流程透明度和审查强度之成本与收益的广泛讨论作出了贡献（Mas, 2016; Baker et al., 2019; Bennedsen et al., 2022; Babenko, Bennett and Wang, 2025）。具体而言，我们说明了旨在加强股东监督的监管规定如何可能促使公司采用“一刀切”的薪酬实践，从而揭示出善意治理改革可能产生的一项非预期后果。

Our study also adds to prior literature on compensation benchmarking. This literature examines the motivations underlying peer selection and finds evidence consistent with peer group choices reflecting economic forces in the market for managerial talent (Bizjak, Lemmon

> **中文：** 本研究还拓展了有关薪酬基准比较的既有文献。该文献考察同业公司选择背后的动机，并发现了与以下观点一致的证据：同业组选择反映了管理人才市场中的经济力量（Bizjak, Lemmon

and Naveen, 2008; Albuquerque, De Franco and Verdi, 2013; Cadman and Carter, 2014). However, other papers suggest that compensation benchmarking leads to pay inflation (Bizjak, Lemmon and Nguyen, 2011; Elson and Ferrere, 2013; Faulkender and Yang, 2010, 2013). We complement this literature by providing evidence that recent institutional developments have contributed to a decline in pay dispersion and a rise in industry-size benchmarking. While these trends make opportunistic peer selection more difficult, they may also result in less tailored and potentially suboptimal pay design.

> **中文：** and Naveen，2008；Albuquerque、De Franco and Verdi，2013；Cadman and Carter，2014）。然而，其他论文认为，薪酬基准比较会导致薪酬膨胀（Bizjak, Lemmon and Nguyen, 2011；Elson and Ferrere, 2013；Faulkender and Yang, 2010, 2013）。本文通过提供证据表明，近期的制度发展促使薪酬离散度下降，并推动行业-规模基准比较日益普及，从而补充了这一文献。尽管这些趋势增加了机会主义同业公司选择的难度，但也可能导致薪酬设计缺乏针对性，并可能偏离最优水平。

# 2. Background and hypothesis

> **中文：** 2. 背景与假设

To offer competitive pay to their executives, compensation committees routinely engage in compensation benchmarking, tying executives’ pay to that of their labor market competitors. One common benchmark is the median pay of industry peers closest in size, henceforth referred to as “industry-size benchmarking.” Anecdotal evidence suggests that industry-size benchmarking has significantly expanded in recent years (e.g., Lan, 2019; Equilar, 2023).

> **中文：** 为了向高管提供具有竞争力的薪酬，薪酬委员会通常会开展薪酬基准比较，将高管薪酬与其劳动力市场竞争者的薪酬挂钩。一种常见的基准是规模最为接近的行业同业公司的薪酬中位数，以下简称“行业-规模基准比较”。轶事证据表明，近年来行业-规模基准比较的应用显著扩大（例如，Lan, 2019；Equilar, 2023）。

## 2.1. The effect of industry-size benchmarking on pay dispersion

> **中文：** 2.1. 行业-规模基准比较对薪酬离散度的影响

The adoption of a uniform criterion to select compensation peers by firms across the economy—industry-size benchmarking being the case in point—likely increases the overlap of compensation peer groups. This uniformity can lead to the formation of “pay clusters,” where firms benchmark their CEO compensation against one another. As most firms usually target their peers’ median pay level, reciprocal referencing can result in a convergence of pay levels within these groups.

> **中文：** 整个经济体中的公司采用统一标准选择薪酬同业公司——行业-规模基准比较即为典型例子——可能会提高薪酬同业组之间的重叠程度。这种统一性可能导致“薪酬集群”的形成，其中各公司相互以对方的 CEO 薪酬为基准。由于大多数公司通常将同业公司的薪酬中位数作为目标，互惠参照可能导致这些群组内部的薪酬水平趋同。

Nonetheless, a convergence in pay levels within groups (e.g., within industry-size groups if industry and size became the popular benchmarking criteria) need not necessarily translate into an overall decrease in pay dispersion across the economy. While pay dispersion may decrease within groups, it could also increase across groups if within-group pay levels exhibited diverging pay growth trends. The net effect is difficult to predict and depends on

> **中文：** 尽管如此，群组内部薪酬水平的趋同（例如，当行业和规模成为普遍采用的基准比较标准时，行业-规模群组内部的趋同）并不一定会转化为整个经济体薪酬离散度的总体下降。虽然群组内部的薪酬离散度可能下降，但如果不同群组内部的薪酬水平呈现相互分化的增长趋势，群组之间的薪酬离散度也可能上升。因此，其净效应难以预测，并取决于

6

<!-- page:9 -->

## Source Page 9

multiple factors, such as the number of firms in an industry-size group and the number of across-group connections along which compensation changes can propagate.

> **中文：** 多种因素，例如一个行业-规模群组中的公司数量，以及薪酬变化能够沿其传播的跨群组连接数量。

## 2.2. Institutional factors contributing to industry-size benchmarking

> **中文：** 2.2. 推动行业-规模基准比较的制度因素

Understanding the institutional factors contributing to industry-size benchmarking requires an analysis of the potential costs and benefits of this practice for investors. On the cost side, the application of industry-size benchmarking across the economy likely introduces the usual disadvantages associated with one-size-fits-all approaches. Notably, to the extent that it constrains the selection of compensation peers, imposing such criterion limits boards’ discretion in tailoring pay policies to firm-specific needs, leading to deviations from optimal pay levels and potentially affecting hiring, retention, and incentives.

> **中文：** 理解推动行业-规模基准比较的制度因素，需要分析这种做法给投资者带来的潜在成本与收益。在成本方面，在整个经济体中应用行业-规模基准比较，可能会带来“一刀切”方法通常具有的弊端。尤其是，由于这一标准会约束薪酬同业公司的选择，强制采用该标准将限制董事会根据公司的特定需求定制薪酬政策的自由裁量权，进而导致薪酬水平偏离最优水平，并可能影响人才招聘、留任和激励。

On the benefit side, the universal application of industry-size benchmarking could offer several advantages to investors. It could reduce the scope for powerful CEOs to manipulate their own pay (the literature provides some evidence that firms choose compensation peers opportunistically).2 Moreover, even if industry-size benchmarking results in a deviation from optimal peer selection, the cost of such deviation could be lower for investors than the cost of monitoring the benchmarking practices of all portfolio companies. Thus, it is plausible that certain investors are better off with a universal application of industry-size benchmarking. Consistent with this possibility, this compensation assessment policy is often found in the guidelines of large asset managers (see, e.g., Blackrock, 2019, 2; T. Rowe Price, 2019, 6-7).

> **中文：** 在收益方面，普遍应用行业-规模基准比较可以为投资者带来若干好处。它可以缩小权势较大的 CEO 操纵自身薪酬的空间（已有文献提供了一些公司机会主义地选择薪酬同业公司的证据）。2 此外，即使行业-规模基准比较会导致同业公司选择偏离最优方案，这种偏离给投资者造成的成本也可能低于监督所有投资组合公司基准比较做法的成本。因此，对某些投资者而言，普遍应用行业-规模基准比较可能更为有利。与这种可能性一致，大型资产管理公司的指导方针经常纳入这种薪酬评估政策（例如，参见 Blackrock, 2019, 2；T. Rowe Price, 2019, 6-7）。

Boards and their compensation committees could give into investors’ request to use industry-size benchmarking due to reputational concerns (e.g., to avoid withhold votes at director elections or to avoid low say on pay vote outcomes). Further, explaining to investors a deviation from industry-size benchmarking might not be straightforward, as the optimal selection of the compensation peer group is often based on confidential information.

> **中文：** 出于声誉方面的顾虑，董事会及其薪酬委员会可能会接受投资者采用行业-规模基准比较的要求（例如，为避免在董事选举中遭遇保留票，或避免薪酬话语权投票获得较低支持率）。此外，由于薪酬同业组的最优选择通常以保密信息为依据，向投资者解释为何偏离行业-规模基准比较可能并非易事。

2Researchers have found mixed evidence on whether firms opportunistically select compensation peer groups. Bizjak, Lemmon and Nguyen (2011) and Faulkender and Yang (2010, 2013) provide evidence that compensation benchmarking contributes to pay inflation among poorly governed firms while Bizjak, Lemmon and Naveen (2008), Albuquerque, De Franco and Verdi (2013), and Cadman and Carter (2014) find that, on average, peer group choices reflect features of the managerial labor market and help with the design of pay packages to attract and retain talent.

> **中文：** 2关于公司是否会机会主义地选择薪酬同业组，研究人员得出了不一致的证据。Bizjak, Lemmon and Nguyen（2011）以及 Faulkender and Yang（2010, 2013）提供的证据表明，薪酬基准比较会加剧治理较差公司的薪酬膨胀；而 Bizjak, Lemmon and Naveen（2008）、Albuquerque, De Franco and Verdi（2013）以及 Cadman and Carter（2014）发现，平均而言，同业组选择反映了管理者劳动力市场的特征，并有助于设计能够吸引和留住人才的薪酬方案。

7

<!-- page:10 -->

## Source Page 10

Over recent decades, the costs and benefits of industry-size benchmarking for investors and directors have likely been shaped by key institutional developments. We consider three such developments: greater pay transparency due to the 2006 SEC rule mandating the disclosure of the peers used for compensation benchmarking, the growing influence of proxy advisors, and the introduction of the advisory (“say on pay”) vote on executive compensation. As discussed below, these institutional changes likely contribute to the increase in industry-size benchmarking in an interrelated and complementary way, with each development likely relying on the others to have an effect.

> **中文：** 近几十年来，行业-规模基准比较给投资者和董事带来的成本与收益很可能受到若干关键制度发展的影响。我们考察其中三项制度发展：2006 年 SEC 规则强制披露用于薪酬基准比较的同业公司，从而提高了薪酬透明度；代理投票顾问的影响力日益增强；以及针对高管薪酬引入咨询性投票，即“薪酬话语权投票”（say on pay）。如下文所述，这些制度变化可能以相互关联、相互补充的方式推动行业-规模基准比较日益普及，而且每一项制度发展可能都需要依赖其他制度发展才能产生影响。

### (i) The 2006 SEC rule on compensation disclosure

> **中文：** （i）2006 年 SEC 薪酬披露规则

The SEC issued in December 2006 new regulation that, among other things, mandated firms to disclose the identity of their compensation peers.3 The SEC rule thereby facilitated transparency about the CEO pay setting process and promoted greater scrutiny of firms’ compensation benchmarking practices by investors and third parties such as proxy advisors.4 Transparency and heightened scrutiny likely increased the costs for directors to deviate from the industry-size benchmarking criterion. These costs were likely amplified by other institutional factors that we discuss next.

> **中文：** SEC 于 2006 年 12 月发布了新规，其中包括强制公司披露其薪酬同业公司的身份。3 因此，SEC 规则提高了 CEO 薪酬设定过程的透明度，并促使投资者以及代理投票顾问等第三方更加严格地审查公司的薪酬基准比较做法。透明度的提高和审查力度的增强，很可能提高了董事偏离行业-规模基准比较标准的成本。我们接下来讨论的其他制度因素可能进一步放大了这些成本。

### (ii) Proxy advisors

> **中文：** （ii）代理投票顾问

As shown in prior literature, proxy advisors’ voting recommendations have a significant influence on vote outcomes (e.g., Ertimur, Ferri and Oesch, 2013; Iliev and Lowry, 2015; Malenko and Shen, 2016). This research also documents that—presumably in an attempt to avoid negative vote recommendations—corporate boards make compensation design choices in line with proxy advisors’ policies (e.g., Larcker, McCall and Ormazabal, 2013, 2015; Malenko and Shen, 2016 and Hayne and Vance, 2019). Adopting industry-size benchmarking is likely to

> **中文：** 既有文献表明，代理投票顾问的投票建议对投票结果具有显著影响（例如，Ertimur, Ferri and Oesch, 2013；Iliev and Lowry, 2015；Malenko and Shen, 2016）。这些研究还记录到，公司董事会会按照代理投票顾问的政策作出薪酬设计选择，这可能是为了避免收到负面的投票建议（例如，Larcker, McCall and Ormazabal, 2013, 2015；Malenko and Shen, 2016；Hayne and Vance, 2019）。采用行业-规模基准比较很可能

3Almost no firm voluntarily disclosed its compensation peers prior to 2007. Despite the mandate, some firms also ignored the mandate still in 2007 (see White, 2007, 2008).

> **中文：** 3在 2007 年以前，几乎没有公司自愿披露其薪酬同业公司。尽管存在这项强制要求，2007 年仍有一些公司未予遵守（参见 White, 2007, 2008）。

4Of course, transparency on compensation peers may have other, more complex effects. For example, Choi, Cicero and Mobbs (2022) report evidence that the compensation peer disclosure regulation by the SEC reveals information to executives about their outside opportunities and has led to pay increases and to a greater likelihood of accepting positions at firms included in the compensation peer group.

> **中文：** 4当然，薪酬同业公司的透明度也可能产生其他更为复杂的影响。例如，Choi, Cicero and Mobbs（2022）提供的证据表明，SEC 的薪酬同业公司披露规定向高管揭示了有关其外部就业机会的信息，并导致薪酬上升，同时提高了高管接受薪酬同业组内公司职位的可能性。

8

<!-- page:11 -->

## Source Page 11

be one of those choices, as proxy advisory firms typically justify their voting recommendations based on assessments of compensation practices that incorporate such a criterion (ISS, 2012a). For example, ISS (i.e., the largest proxy advisory firm) has developed its own industry- and size-based peer selection methodology. The methodology is used in its “multiple-of-median test,” which relates the level of a firm’s CEO pay to the median CEO pay of an industry- and size-matched set of firms.5

> **中文：** 就是这些选择之一，因为代理投票顾问公司通常依据对薪酬实践的评估来论证其投票建议，而这类评估纳入了该项标准（ISS, 2012a）。例如，ISS（即规模最大的代理投票顾问公司）制定了自己的行业和规模同业公司选择方法。该方法被用于其“中位数倍数检验”（multiple-of-median test），即将一家公司的 CEO 薪酬水平与一组在行业和规模上相匹配的公司的 CEO 薪酬中位数进行比较。5

Further, the rise in proxy advisor influence is frequently credited to the growth in passive investing that is driven by popular investment vehicles such as index funds and ETFs (e.g., Sushko and Turner, 2018). While passive investing vehicles offer significant advantages to investment clients (notably diversification and low management fees), such an investment strategy generates relatively weak incentives to monitor portfolio firms (Almazan, Hartzell and Starks, 2005). One way for fund managers of passive investment vehicles to reduce the cost of monitoring their portfolio is to rely on recommendations by proxy advisors. Consistent with this possibility, recent research suggests that fund managers’ reliance on proxy advisory advice is determined by their weighing of the costs and benefits of active voting (Iliev and Lowry, 2015).

> **中文：** 此外，代理投票顾问影响力的上升通常被归因于被动投资的增长，而指数基金和交易所交易基金（ETF）等广受欢迎的投资工具推动了这种增长（例如，Sushko and Turner, 2018）。虽然被动投资工具为投资客户带来了显著优势，尤其是分散化和较低的管理费用，但这种投资策略对监督投资组合公司的激励相对较弱（Almazan, Hartzell and Starks, 2005）。被动投资工具的基金经理降低投资组合监督成本的一种方式，是依赖代理投票顾问的建议。与这种可能性一致，近期研究表明，基金经理对代理投票顾问建议的依赖程度取决于其对主动投票成本与收益的权衡（Iliev and Lowry, 2015）。

### (iii) Say on pay

> **中文：** （iii）薪酬话语权投票

In 2011, the U.S. introduced “Say on Pay” (SOP) regulation. SOP stipulates that any publicly listed firm in the U.S. must regularly submit the compensation of its top executives to shareholders for an advisory vote. Firms are required to disclose the corresponding vote outcome and to report on their response to potential shareholder discontent.

> **中文：** 2011 年，美国引入了“薪酬话语权投票”（Say on Pay，SOP）规定。SOP 规定，任何在美国公开上市的公司都必须定期将其最高层高管的薪酬提交股东进行咨询性投票。公司必须披露相应的投票结果，并报告其如何回应股东可能表达的不满。

Prior literature provides evidence that boards make substantial changes to compensation practices after obtaining weak shareholder support in SOP proposals (e.g., Ferri and Maber, 2013; Ertimur, Ferri and Oesch, 2013; Correa and Lel, 2016; Denis, Jochem and Rajamani, 2020). There is also evidence that SOP has labor market consequences for directors. For

> **中文：** 既有文献提供的证据表明，当 SOP 提案获得的股东支持率较低后，董事会会对薪酬实践作出重大调整（例如，Ferri and Maber, 2013；Ertimur, Ferri and Oesch, 2013；Correa and Lel, 2016；Denis, Jochem and Rajamani, 2020）。还有证据表明，SOP 会对董事产生劳动力市场后果。例如，

5ISS uses this matched set of firms also as an input in several other pay screens that underpin pay-related vote recommendations; specifically, its quantitative pay-for-performance screen, relative degree of alignment screen, financial performance assessment, and qualitative review of the pay-for-performance analysis (see §15, 17, 19, 24 in ISS, 2019b).

> **中文：** 5ISS 还将这组匹配公司作为其他若干薪酬筛选指标的输入，而这些指标构成薪酬相关投票建议的依据；具体包括量化薪酬绩效筛选、相对一致程度筛选、财务绩效评估，以及对薪酬绩效分析的定性审查（参见 ISS, 2019b 中的 §15、17、19、24）。

9

<!-- page:12 -->

## Source Page 12

example, Badgett et al. (2022) find that directors at firms receiving low SOP support experience reductions in external directorships, compensation committee positions, and director compensation. Dey, Starkweather and White (2024) find that directors engage with shareholders about their pay policies after receiving low SOP support, and that the outreach is more substantive when directors face a greater risk of losing ISS support. As such, SOP could have increased the pressure on directors to adopt compensation practices favored by influential investors and proxy advisers, industry-size benchmarking being a notable example. The internet appendix provides two anecdotes consistent with this possibility.

> **中文：** Badgett et al.（2022）发现，SOP 支持率较低的公司，其董事所担任的外部董事职务、薪酬委员会职位以及董事薪酬均有所减少。Dey, Starkweather and White（2024）发现，在获得较低的 SOP 支持率后，董事会就其薪酬政策与股东进行沟通；当董事面临更高的失去 ISS 支持的风险时，这种沟通更具实质性。因此，SOP 可能加大了董事采用有影响力的投资者和代理投票顾问所偏好之薪酬实践的压力，行业-规模基准比较便是一个显著例子。网络附录提供了两个与这种可能性一致的轶事案例。

# 3. Evolution of pay dispersion over time

> **中文：** 3. 薪酬离散度随时间的演变

## 3.1. Sample and data

> **中文：** 3.1. 样本与数据

Our first sample includes the universe of firms covered by Execucomp between 1996 and 2023, which consists of a total of 3,976 distinct firms with an average of 1,975 firms per year (Execucomp backfills pay information for new entrants of the S&P 1500). In our later firm-level tests we restrict the sample to S&P 1500 firms and their compensation peers. We start in 1996 as the SEC phased in the EDGAR system for the electronic submission of public filings between 1993 and 1996 (Gao and Huang, 2020).6 In the tests using compensation peer data, the sample period starts in 2007, as there was no public disclosure of this information before that year.

> **中文：** 我们的第一个样本包括 1996 年至 2023 年期间 Execucomp 覆盖的全部公司，共计 3,976 家不同公司，平均每年包含 1,975 家公司（Execucomp 会回填新纳入 S&P 1500 公司此前的薪酬信息）。在后续的公司层面检验中，我们将样本限制为 S&P 1500 公司及其薪酬同业公司。样本期始于 1996 年，这是因为 SEC 在 1993 年至 1996 年期间分阶段推行了用于以电子方式提交公开申报文件的 EDGAR 系统（Gao and Huang, 2020）。6 在使用薪酬同业公司数据的检验中，样本期始于 2007 年，因为该信息在此前年份并未公开披露。

We obtain data on the identity of compensation peers from AuditAnalytics, Equilar, and ISS. To avoid that outliers or missing peer group data affect our inferences, we require that each peer group contains at least 5 and at most 76 peers (which are the 1st and 99th percentiles of peer group sizes, respectively). To maximize data coverage on compensation peers, we collect pay information from various sources including Execucomp, ISS’s Executive Compensation Analysis (ECA), Equilar, Capital IQ, and GMI, and exclude observations with insufficient data (i.e., when pay data is missing for more than 25 percent of compensation peers). We collect accounting information from Compustat, stock prices from CRSP,

> **中文：** 我们从 AuditAnalytics、Equilar 和 ISS 获取薪酬同业公司身份数据。为避免异常值或同业组数据缺失影响我们的推断，我们要求每个同业组至少包含 5 家、至多包含 76 家同业公司（分别对应同业组规模的第 1 和第 99 百分位数）。为了尽可能扩大薪酬同业公司数据的覆盖范围，我们从多个来源收集薪酬信息，包括 Execucomp、ISS 的 Executive Compensation Analysis（ECA）、Equilar、Capital IQ 和 GMI，并剔除数据不足的观测值（即超过 25% 的薪酬同业公司缺少薪酬数据的观测值）。我们从 Compustat 收集会计信息，从 CRSP 收集股票价格，

6Prior findings suggest that the staggered phase-in affected the dispersion of CEO pay levels between 1994 and 1996 as total CEO pay dropped significantly more in the upper tail of the compensation distribution following an increase in media coverage (Babenko, Bennett and Wang, 2025).

> **中文：** 6既有研究结果表明，这种分阶段推行影响了 1994 年至 1996 年间 CEO 薪酬水平的离散度，因为随着媒体报道增加，薪酬分布上尾的 CEO 总薪酬下降幅度显著更大（Babenko, Bennett and Wang, 2025）。

10

<!-- page:13 -->

## Source Page 13

institutional ownership information from Refinitiv, and shareholder vote outcomes and vote recommendations from ISS’s Voting Analytics and ECA databases. For our second sample, the firm-level dataset, these data requirements result in an average of 1,240 firms per year and 2,175 distinct firms between 2007 and 2023, using pay information for an average of 2,982 compensation peers per year with non-missing pay data. Table 1 provides further details on the characteristics of our two samples.

> **中文：** 从 Refinitiv 收集机构持股信息，并从 ISS 的 Voting Analytics 和 ECA 数据库收集股东投票结果与投票建议。对于我们的第二个样本，即公司层面数据集，这些数据要求使得 2007 年至 2023 年期间的样本平均每年包含 1,240 家公司，共计 2,175 家不同公司；我们使用的薪酬信息平均每年涵盖 2,982 家薪酬数据非缺失的薪酬同业公司。表 1 进一步提供了两个样本特征的详细信息。

## 3.2. Graphical analysis

> **中文：** 3.2. 图形分析

We first conduct a graphical analysis of the evolution of pay dispersion over our sample period. This analysis is conducted at the economy-, industry-size and firm-level. For each year, we measure pay dispersion as the standard deviation of Pay, computed as the CEO’s total compensation (TDC1 in Execucomp) scaled by its sample median in that year. A value of, say, 0.5 (1.5) for Pay hence implies that a CEO receives half (1.5 times) the median CEO pay level in that year. We scale TDC1 by its median because the level of executive pay measured in dollars is non-stationary (it increases over time) and because comparing dispersion across time requires a dimensionless measure (see, e.g., Cox and Lewis, 1966).7 We refer to the standard deviation of median-scaled TDC1 as Pay dispersion.

> **中文：** 我们首先对样本期内薪酬离散度的演变进行图形分析。该分析分别在经济体、行业-规模群组和公司层面开展。对于每一年，我们将薪酬离散度衡量为 `Pay` 的标准差，其中 `Pay` 的计算方式是用当年样本中位数对 CEO 总薪酬（Execucomp 中的 `TDC1`）进行缩放。因此，假设 `Pay` 的取值为 0.5（1.5），则意味着该 CEO 获得的薪酬为当年 CEO 薪酬中位数的一半（1.5 倍）。我们使用中位数对 `TDC1` 进行缩放，是因为以美元计量的高管薪酬水平是非平稳的（其随时间上升），并且跨期比较离散度需要使用无量纲指标（例如，参见 Cox and Lewis, 1966）。7 我们将经中位数缩放的 `TDC1` 的标准差称为 `Pay dispersion`。

Figure 1 plots the evolution of Pay dispersion over time computed at the economy-level (Panel A), at the industry-size group level (Panel B), and using firms’ compensation peer groups at the firm-level (Panel C). To control for potential confounding effects, the analysis adds two variants of Pay dispersion. First, we compute the dispersion of CEO compensation excluding stock options. We refer to this variant as Pay dispersion (ex-options). Stock options were prominent during the dot-com boom (1998-2002) when high equity valuations also

> **中文：** 图 1 绘制了分别在经济体层面（Panel A）、行业-规模群组层面（Panel B），以及使用各公司薪酬同业组计算的公司层面（Panel C）`Pay dispersion` 随时间的演变。为控制潜在的混杂影响，该分析还加入了 `Pay dispersion` 的两个变体。首先，我们计算不含股票期权的 CEO 薪酬离散度。我们将这一变体称为 `Pay dispersion (ex-options)`。在互联网泡沫时期（1998-2002），股票期权十分普遍，当时较高的股票估值也

7Standard deviation is not a dimensionless measure of dispersion; it increases mechanically with the magnitude of the underlying data (mathematically, SD(c · X) = c · SD(X)). Hence, while the standard deviation may be increasing due to larger magnitudes of the underlying values, actual dispersion declines if the standard deviation does not increase proportionately. For example, median CEO pay in our sample almost quadrupled between 1996 and 2023 (from $1.6 million in 1996 to $6.2 million in 2023 while the standard deviation of CEO pay increased by less than half (from $7.4 million in 1996 to $10.9 million in 2023). We use median pay rather than mean pay for scaling because we are interested in the ‘typical’ CEO’s pay level and not in the aggregate level of CEO pay (see Murphy, 2013, 9). Furthermore, firms often target the median of their compensation peer group and many of ISS’s executive pay screens relate a firm’s pay level to the median of a benchmark group.

> **中文：** 7标准差并不是无量纲的离散度指标；它会随机础数据量级的增大而机械性地上升（从数学上看，`SD(c · X) = c · SD(X)`）。因此，尽管标准差可能因基础数值的量级增大而上升，但如果标准差没有同比例上升，实际离散度便会下降。例如，1996 年至 2023 年间，我们样本中的 CEO 薪酬中位数接近增长至原来的四倍（从 1996 年的 160 万美元增至 2023 年的 620 万美元），而 CEO 薪酬的标准差增幅不足一半（从 1996 年的 740 万美元增至 2023 年的 1,090 万美元）。我们使用薪酬中位数而非平均数进行缩放，是因为我们关注的是“典型”CEO 的薪酬水平，而不是 CEO 薪酬的总量水平（参见 Murphy, 2013, 9）。此外，公司通常将其薪酬同业组的中位数作为目标，而且 ISS 的许多高管薪酬筛选指标都会将一家公司的薪酬水平与基准群组的中位数进行比较。

11

<!-- page:14 -->

---

## Source Page 14

inflated the value of stock option packages (Murphy, 2013), but lost much of their appeal after the introduction of FAS 123-R in 2005/2006. Second, we compute the CEO “abnormal” compensation as the residual from annual cross-sectional regressions of unscaled CEO pay on firm size, Tobin’s Q, sales growth, return on assets, stock return, and idiosyncratic volatility. We compute Pay dispersion (abnormal) as the standard deviation of the scaled residuals.

> **中文：** 这抬高了股票期权薪酬组合的价值（Murphy, 2013），但在 2005/2006 年引入 FAS 123-R 后，股票期权的吸引力大幅下降。其次，我们将未经缩放的 CEO 薪酬对公司规模、Tobin’s Q、销售增长率、资产收益率、股票收益率和特质波动率进行年度横截面回归，并以回归残差衡量 CEO“异常”薪酬。我们将缩放后残差的标准差计算为 Pay dispersion (abnormal)。

Figure 1A shows that Pay dispersion increased between 1996 and 2000, peaking during the dot-com boom in the late 1990s (solid line). The metric declines sharply after the dot-com bust (from 2.7 in 2000 to 2.1 in 2002), remaining relatively unchanged afterwards until 2007. After that year, we observe a gradual decline until recently (from 2.1 in 2007 to 1.3 in 2023; a decline of 38 percent). The dashed line shows that the secular decline post 2007 is similarly pronounced for Pay dispersion (ex-options) (i.e., when excluding stock options). The measure almost perfectly overlaps with pay dispersion after 2002, while the spike around the dot-com bubble largely disappears. We thus conclude that while the decline in the value of stock options may have contributed to the decline in pay dispersion in the early 2000s, it cannot explain the continued decline in pay dispersion between 2007 and 2023.8,9

> **中文：** 图 1A 显示，Pay dispersion 在 1996 年至 2000 年间上升，并在 20 世纪 90 年代末的互联网繁荣时期达到峰值（实线）。互联网泡沫破裂后，该指标大幅下降（从 2000 年的 2.7 降至 2002 年的 2.1），此后直至 2007 年基本保持不变。2007 年之后，我们观察到该指标逐渐下降并延续至近期（从 2007 年的 2.1 降至 2023 年的 1.3，降幅为 38%）。虚线显示，2007 年之后 Pay dispersion (ex-options)（即剔除股票期权后的薪酬离散度）的长期下降趋势同样显著。2002 年以后，该指标与薪酬离散度几乎完全重合，而互联网泡沫时期的尖峰则基本消失。因此，我们得出结论：尽管股票期权价值下降可能促成了 21 世纪初薪酬离散度的下降，但它无法解释 2007 年至 2023 年间薪酬离散度的持续下降。8,9

The decline in pay dispersion is also observable in Pay dispersion (abnormal) (i.e., when we repeat the analysis after adjusting for firm fundamentals). The timing and magnitude of the decline is similar to that in Pay dispersion (see dotted line in Figure 1A). This suggests that the decline in pay dispersion is not driven by a convergence in firm fundamentals which could have contributed to similar pay levels across firms.10

> **中文：** Pay dispersion (abnormal) 中同样可以观察到薪酬离散度的下降（即在对公司基本面进行调整后重复分析）。其下降的时间和幅度与 Pay dispersion 相似（见图 1A 中的点线）。这表明，薪酬离散度的下降并非由公司基本面趋同所驱动；公司基本面趋同原本可能导致不同公司之间的薪酬水平更加相近。10

8Another possibility is that FAS 123-R reduced stock option usage only gradually after 2006. This possibility is not supported by the data. Firms rapidly reduced their use of stock options: the median Execucomp firm had stock options as a fraction of total pay at 29 percent in 2003, reduced it to 11 percent in 2006, and had zero percent stock option pay from 2007 onwards. Between 2003 and 2007, Pay dispersion and Pay dispersion (ex-options) however remained steady between 2.0 and 2.1. Further, the irrelevance of stock option pay for the median firm as of 2007 is inconsistent with FAS 123-R explaining the continued decline that starts in 2008. In Figure IA.1 in the internet appendix, we further find that the post-2007 decline in Pay dispersion is identical for high and low option-use industries.

> **中文：** 8另一种可能性是，FAS 123-R 在 2006 年之后仅逐步降低了股票期权的使用。这种可能性并未得到数据支持。公司迅速减少了股票期权的使用：对于 Execucomp 中位数公司，股票期权占总薪酬的比例在 2003 年为 29%，到 2006 年降至 11%，并从 2007 年起降至零。尽管如此，2003 年至 2007 年间，Pay dispersion 和 Pay dispersion (ex-options) 均稳定在 2.0 至 2.1 之间。此外，截至 2007 年，股票期权薪酬对于中位数公司已经无关紧要，这与 FAS 123-R 能够解释始于 2008 年的持续下降并不一致。在网络附录图 IA.1 中，我们进一步发现，2007 年之后 Pay dispersion 的下降在股票期权使用程度较高和较低的行业中完全相同。

9We also consider the possibility that the decline in pay dispersion may be related to a decrease in the frequency of “mega grants” (i.e., large one-time equity grants). We find no support for this alternative explanation. In Panel A of Figure IA.2, we do not find evidence that mega grants have become less frequently used between 2007 and 2023. Further, Panel B shows that the pay dispersion decline is almost identical when excluding all firm-year observations with mega grants. As an alternative, we also exclude all stock- and option-based pay and continue to find a 34 percent decline in non-equity pay dispersion between 2007 and 2023.

> **中文：** 9我们还考虑了薪酬离散度下降可能与“巨额授予”（即大额一次性股权授予）频率降低有关的可能性。我们没有发现支持这一替代性解释的证据。在图 IA.2 的面板 A 中，我们未发现巨额授予在 2007 年至 2023 年间使用频率下降的证据。此外，面板 B 显示，在剔除所有存在巨额授予的公司—年度观测值后，薪酬离散度的降幅几乎完全相同。作为另一种检验，我们还剔除了所有基于股票和期权的薪酬，并仍然发现非股权薪酬离散度在 2007 年至 2023 年间下降了 34%。

10In Figure IA.3, we plot the dispersion of an extensive set of firm fundamentals across time. The figure

> **中文：** 当我们使用行业—规模组层面的平均离散度重复分析时（图 1B），以及在公司—年度层面计算所披露薪酬同业组内部的薪酬离散度并重复分析时（图 1C），均得到相似的薪酬离散度下降模式。11 最后，我们使用两种替代性的实际实现薪酬指标复现图 1 的分析。第一种指标采用 Execucomp 的 TOTAL ALT2，其中以已归属股票的价值和财政年度内行权所实现的价值，替代股票及期权奖励在授予日的公允价值。第二种指标采用 Carter and Pawliczek (2023) 提出的实际实现薪酬度量方法（详见变量附录）。网络附录图 IA.5 显示，自 2006 年起可获得的实际实现薪酬，其离散模式与图 1 报告的结果高度相似。

In Figure 2, we explore which tail of the pay distribution the decline originates from. We group sample observations by percentiles of CEO pay each year and, for each group, compute the fractional change in Pay between the start and the end of each of the periods before and after the SEC disclosure rule (i.e., 1996-2006 in Panel A and 2007-2023 in Panel B). For the highest percentiles, a negative (positive) change in Pay would suggest that CEO pay in that percentile is converging toward (moving away from) the median pay level. Conversely, for the lowest percentiles, a positive (negative) change would suggest that CEO pay in that percentile is converging to (moving away from) the median pay level.

> **中文：** 在图 2 中，我们考察薪酬离散度的下降源自薪酬分布的哪一端。我们每年按照 CEO 薪酬的百分位数对样本观测值进行分组，并针对每一组计算 SEC 披露规则实施前后各期间起点与终点之间 Pay 的比例变化（即面板 A 中的 1996—2006 年和面板 B 中的 2007—2023 年）。对于最高百分位组，Pay 的负向（正向）变化意味着该百分位上的 CEO 薪酬正在向中位数薪酬水平收敛（偏离）。相反，对于最低百分位组，Pay 的正向（负向）变化意味着该百分位上的 CEO 薪酬正在向中位数薪酬水平收敛（偏离）。

Figure 2B shows increases (decreases) in pay for the lower (higher) percentiles, suggesting that the distribution of pay has become narrower from 2007 to 2023. For example, the figure shows that pay of CEOs at the 25th percentile increased between 2007 and 2023 from 0.45 times median pay to 0.52 times median – an increase of 16 percent. During the same time period, CEOs at the 75th percentile saw their pay drop from 2.25 times median pay to 1.79 times median – a decline of 20 percent. In contrast, Figure 2A shows decreases in pay for the lower percentiles and minimal changes for the higher percentiles, suggesting that

> **中文：** 图 2B 显示，较低（较高）百分位组的薪酬有所上升（下降），表明 2007 年至 2023 年间薪酬分布趋于收窄。例如，该图显示，处于第 25 百分位的 CEO 薪酬在 2007 年至 2023 年间从中位数薪酬的 0.45 倍上升至 0.52 倍，增幅为 16%。同期，处于第 75 百分位的 CEO 薪酬从中位数薪酬的 2.25 倍降至 1.79 倍，降幅为 20%。相比之下，图 2A 显示，较低百分位组的薪酬下降，而较高百分位组的薪酬变化很小，这表明

shows no evidence that firms have become more similar over time along dimensions that typically determine pay levels.

> **中文：** 并未提供证据表明，公司在通常决定薪酬水平的各个维度上随时间推移变得更加相似。

11In Figure IA.4, we plot pay dispersion separately for each GICS2 industry and find substantial pay dispersion declines in all GICS2 industries (the min/avg/max decline is 38/48/59 percent since 1996 and 5/43/59 percent since 2007). We also plot in Figure IA.4 pay dispersion using alternative industry definitions and find that the decline does not depend on our choice for industry classification.

> **中文：** 11在图 IA.4 中，我们分别绘制了各 GICS2 行业的薪酬离散度，并发现所有 GICS2 行业的薪酬离散度均大幅下降（自 1996 年以来的最小/平均/最大降幅为 38/48/59%，自 2007 年以来则为 5/43/59%）。我们还在图 IA.4 中使用替代性行业定义绘制了薪酬离散度，结果发现，这一下降并不取决于我们对行业分类方法的选择。

there was no convergence of pay before the implementation of the SEC rule on compensation disclosures in 2006.12

> **中文：** 在 2006 年 SEC 薪酬披露规则实施之前，薪酬并未出现收敛。12

### 3.3. Regression analysis

> **中文：** 3.3. 回归分析

To explore the robustness of the previous patterns, we next conduct a regression analysis of the time variation in pay dispersion at the industry-size-year level and at the firm-year level. Consistent with Figure 1, models 1-3 in Table 2A shows that the secular decline during the last decades in pay dispersion is statistically significant at the industry-size group level. The result is robust to including industry-size fixed effects. The coefficient estimates suggest that the average annual decrease in pay dispersion within industry-size groups ranges from 0.015 to 0.051, depending on whether compensation is adjusted for option compensation or for firm fundamentals. Relative to their values in 2007, these coefficient estimates imply a cumulative decline between 22 and 74 percent in the respective pay dispersion measures between 2007 and 2023. We find similar results in models 4-6 when creating, for each firm, a separate group consisting of industry- and size-matched peers.13

> **中文：** 为了考察上述模式的稳健性，我们接下来分别在行业—规模—年度层面和公司—年度层面对薪酬离散度的时间变化进行回归分析。与图 1 一致，表 2A 的模型 1—3 显示，过去数十年薪酬离散度的长期下降在行业—规模组层面具有统计显著性。加入行业—规模固定效应后，结果依然稳健。系数估计表明，行业—规模组内部薪酬离散度的年均降幅介于 0.015 至 0.051 之间，具体取决于是否针对期权薪酬或公司基本面对薪酬进行调整。相对于这些指标在 2007 年的数值，上述系数估计意味着相应的薪酬离散度指标在 2007 年至 2023 年间累计下降了 22% 至 74%。当我们在模型 4—6 中为每家公司分别创建一个由行业和规模匹配的同业公司构成的组时，也得到相似结果。13

In Table 2B, we further corroborate these results by examining the dispersion of pay among the peer firms selected by our sample firms for compensation benchmarking (as disclosed in their public filings). Examining pay dispersion at the firm-level allows us to control for changes in firm characteristics and to add industry-by-size and firm fixed effects. Consistent with Figure 1, Table 2B shows a significant decline in pay dispersion within firms’ compensation peer groups.14

> **中文：** 在表 2B 中，我们通过考察样本公司为薪酬基准比较而选择的同业公司之间的薪酬离散度，进一步验证上述结果（这些同业公司披露于样本公司的公开申报文件中）。在公司层面考察薪酬离散度，使我们能够控制公司特征的变化，并加入行业×规模固定效应和公司固定效应。与图 1 一致，表 2B 显示，公司薪酬同业组内部的薪酬离散度显著下降。14

12Figure IA.6 in the internet appendix shows the trajectory of two alternative dispersion measures between 1996 and 2023 – the skewness and the median-scaled interquartile range of the CEO pay distribution. Consistent with Figure 2, the two dispersion measures show that the pay distribution narrowed only after the implementation of the SEC disclosure rule in 2006.

> **中文：** 12网络附录图 IA.6 展示了 1996 年至 2023 年间两种替代性离散度指标的变化轨迹，即 CEO 薪酬分布的偏度和经中位数缩放的四分位距。与图 2 一致，这两种离散度指标均显示，薪酬分布仅在 2006 年 SEC 披露规则实施后才开始收窄。

13The benefit of using firm-specific groups consisting of industry- and size-matched peers is that it avoids arbitrary size-quintile cutoffs. Further, as described in section 4, this resembles more closely the way in which firms pick peers for compensation benchmarking.

> **中文：** 13使用由行业和规模匹配的同业公司构成的公司特定组，其优点在于可以避免任意设定规模五分位数的截断点。此外，如第 4 节所述，这种方法更接近公司为薪酬基准比较选择同业公司的实际方式。

14In Table IA.1 in the internet appendix, we repeat the analysis in Table 2 while adding controls for the potentially confounding effect of compensation consultants: we include consultant fixed effects and the fraction of peers with the same compensation consultant as the focal firm. ### 3.4. Pay dispersion in other settings

> **中文：** 3.4. 其他情境下的薪酬离散度

To complete our exploratory analysis of the evolution of pay dispersion over time, it seems natural to examine whether the patterns in Figure 1 also hold in other settings. We repeat the analysis from Figure 1 for the following alternative groups: CEOs of non-U.S. public firms, CEOs of private U.S. firms, and non-top 5 senior executives in U.S. firms.

> **中文：** 为了完善我们对薪酬离散度随时间演变的探索性分析，自然有必要考察图 1 所示模式是否也存在于其他情境中。我们针对以下替代组重复图 1 的分析：非美国上市公司的 CEO、美国私营公司的 CEO，以及美国公司中薪酬排名不在前五位的高级管理人员。

Figure 3A compares pay dispersion among CEOs of public U.S. firms to pay dispersion among CEOs in public firms in other developed economies (the UK, continental Europe, Canada, Australia and the ‘rest-of-the-world’). The analysis starts in 2001 due to data limitations.15 Figure 3A reveals that, while at the start of the sample period the dispersion in CEO pay in the U.S. was much higher than in other regions, by 2023, it had dropped to average international levels. Remarkably, the figure also shows that the US is the only jurisdiction that has experienced such a decline in pay dispersion.

> **中文：** 图 3A 将美国上市公司 CEO 的薪酬离散度与其他发达经济体上市公司 CEO 的薪酬离散度进行比较，这些经济体包括英国、欧洲大陆、加拿大、澳大利亚以及“世界其他地区”。受数据限制，分析始于 2001 年。15 图 3A 显示，尽管在样本期初，美国 CEO 薪酬的离散程度远高于其他地区，但到 2023 年已降至国际平均水平。值得注意的是，该图还显示，美国是唯一经历了如此显著薪酬离散度下降的司法辖区。

Figure 3B compares pay dispersion among CEOs of public U.S. firms to pay dispersion among CEOs of private U.S. firms and to pay dispersion among non-top 5 senior executives in public U.S. firms.16 As shown in these figures, the evolution of pay dispersion in these two other placebo groups is very different from that among CEOs of public U.S. firms – dispersion has increased among the CEOs of private U.S. firms and has remained constant among non-top 5 senior U.S. executives.

> **中文：** 图 3B 将美国上市公司 CEO 的薪酬离散度与美国私营公司 CEO 的薪酬离散度，以及美国上市公司中薪酬排名不在前五位的高级管理人员的薪酬离散度进行比较。16 如这些图所示，另外两个安慰剂组的薪酬离散度演变与美国上市公司 CEO 的情况截然不同：美国私营公司 CEO 的薪酬离散度有所上升，而美国公司中薪酬排名不在前五位的高级管理人员的薪酬离散度则保持不变。

unique combination of institutional developments described in section 2. For example, the compensation of non-top 5 senior executives in U.S. firms is generally not determined by compensation benchmarking and is not subject to SOP voting. ## 4 . Industry-size benchmarking

> **中文：** 4 . 行业—规模基准比较

We next explore the empirical validity of our conjecture that the documented decrease in pay dispersion is driven by an increase in industry-size benchmarking. We explore this possibility by analyzing the evolution of the characteristics of firms’ compensation peer groups over the sample period.

> **中文：** 接下来，我们考察如下推测在经验上的有效性：本文记录的薪酬离散度下降是由行业—规模基准比较使用增加所驱动的。我们通过分析样本期内公司薪酬同业组特征的演变来考察这一可能性。

### 4.1. Simulation analysis

> **中文：** 4.1. 模拟分析

As a first step to explore whether industry-size benchmarking could cause a decrease in pay dispersion in our sample, we conduct a simulation exercise. We start from actual data on CEO pay and compensation peer groups for the cross-section of sample firms in 2007 (i.e., the first year of mandatory disclosure of compensation peer groups). For subsequent years we create for each firm a synthetic compensation peer group replicating the methodology published by ISS to assess compensation practices, which is based on industry and size (ISS is the largest proxy advisory firm and its peer selection methodology is publicly disclosed). The methodological details are shown in Appendix B. We then set each firm’s compensation for year t + 1 at a randomized target percentile of the pay distribution within the firm’s synthetic peer group in year t. We use randomized target percentiles to allow for the possibility that not all firms use the median peer pay level as their benchmark.17 As previously

> **中文：** 作为考察行业—规模基准比较是否可能导致样本中薪酬离散度下降的第一步，我们开展了一项模拟分析。我们以 2007 年样本公司的横截面 CEO 薪酬和薪酬同业组实际数据为起点（即强制披露薪酬同业组的第一年）。对于后续年份，我们依据 ISS 公布的薪酬实践评估方法，为每家公司构建一个基于行业和规模的合成薪酬同业组（ISS 是规模最大的代理投票顾问公司，其同业公司选择方法已公开披露）。具体方法详见附录 B。随后，我们将每家公司在 t + 1 年的薪酬设定为该公司 t 年合成同业组薪酬分布中的一个随机目标百分位数。我们采用随机目标百分位数，以允许并非所有公司都以同业公司薪酬中位数作为基准的可能性。17 如前所述，

17The target percentiles are drawn from a normal distribution with mean 60 and standard deviation of 10 so that 95 percent of these random numbers lie between 40 and 80, which is the range of pay target percentiles we observe in the data. In Figure IA.7 in the internet appendix, we show similar results if all firms were to use the identical target percentiles (e.g., the median or the 60th percentile). Further, we find that a higher average target percentile matters for the evolution in the first moment of pay (i.e., average pay) and leads

> **中文：** 17目标百分位数从均值为 60、标准差为 10 的正态分布中抽取，从而使这些随机数中的 95% 位于 40 至 80 之间，这与我们在数据中观察到的薪酬目标百分位数范围一致。在网络附录图 IA.7 中，我们表明，如果所有公司均采用相同的目标百分位数（例如中位数或第 60 百分位数），也会得到相似结果。此外，我们发现，较高的平均目标百分位数会影响薪酬一阶矩（即平均薪酬）的演变，并导致

16

> **中文：** 来源第 19 页

explained, the outcome of the simulation is difficult to predict because, while industry-size benchmarking mechanically decreases variation within compensation peer groups, it could also result in more variation across such groups.

> **中文：** 如前所述，模拟结果难以预测，因为尽管行业-规模基准比较会机械性地减少薪酬同业组内部的差异，但也可能导致这些同业组之间出现更大的差异。

Figure 4 plots the simulated pay dispersion across all firms over the sample period alongside actual pay dispersion. Similar to Figure 1, simulated pay dispersion declines significantly from the start to the end of the period. The magnitude of the decrease is similar in both data series (45 percent in the simulated data versus 38 percent in the actual data). The simulation hence suggests that an increase in industry-size benchmarking has the potential to explain the observed decline in pay dispersion since 2007.

> **中文：** 图 4 同时绘制了样本期内所有公司的模拟薪酬离散度和实际薪酬离散度。与图 1 类似，从样本期初至期末，模拟薪酬离散度显著下降。两个数据序列的降幅相近（模拟数据中为 45%，实际数据中为 38%）。因此，模拟结果表明，行业-规模基准比较的增加有可能解释自 2007 年以来观察到的薪酬离散度下降。

4.2. Graphical analysis

> **中文：** 4.2. 图形分析

We next explore whether industry-size benchmarking leads to a decrease in pay dispersion in our sample. To do so, we examine whether industry-size benchmarking has increased over time, in parallel to the decline in pay dispersion documented in the previous section. Figure 5A plots five measures of the extent to which a firm’s compensation peers are selected based on industry and size: (i) the standard deviation of peers’ relative book value of assets, (ii) the standard deviation of peers’ relative market value of assets, (iii) the number of GICS6 industries from which a firm draws compensation peers, (iv) the fraction of compensation peers that are significantly different in size (i.e., a peer is much larger (>200%) or much smaller (<50%) than the focal firm in terms of book value of assets and market value of assets), and (v) the fraction of compensation peers from a different GICS1-industry and with a significantly different size (defined as before). For clarity, we rescale the data relative to the start of the sample period. As shown in Figure 5A, we find a decline in all five metrics over time, supporting the notion that firms increasingly include compensation peers of similar industry and size.

> **中文：** 接下来，我们考察行业-规模基准比较是否会导致样本中的薪酬离散度下降。为此，我们检验行业-规模基准比较是否随着时间推移而增加，并与上一节所记录的薪酬离散度下降同步发生。图 5A 绘制了衡量公司在多大程度上依据行业和规模选择薪酬同业公司的五项指标：(i) 同业公司相对资产账面价值的标准差；(ii) 同业公司相对资产市场价值的标准差；(iii) 公司选取薪酬同业公司所涉及的 GICS6 行业数量；(iv) 规模存在显著差异的薪酬同业公司占比（即按资产账面价值和资产市场价值衡量，同业公司的规模远大于核心公司（>200%）或远小于核心公司（<50%））；以及 (v) 来自不同 GICS1 行业且规模存在显著差异（定义同前）的薪酬同业公司占比。为清晰起见，我们以样本期初为基准对数据进行了重新缩放。如图 5A 所示，全部五项指标均随时间推移而下降，这支持了公司日益倾向于纳入行业和规模相似的薪酬同业公司这一观点。

Table IA.2 confirms that compensation peer groups have not increased in size over time; hence, less similar peers are replaced with firms more similar in industry and size. Further-

> **中文：** 表 IA.2 证实，薪酬同业组的规模并未随时间推移而扩大；因此，相似度较低的同业公司被行业和规模更为相似的公司所取代。此

to escalating pay (also known as the “pay ratcheting effect” in the literature; see e.g., Elson and Ferrere, 2013) but does not matter for pay dispersion that we are concerned with in this study.

> **中文：** 会推高薪酬（文献中亦称为“薪酬棘轮效应”；例如参见 Elson and Ferrere, 2013），但与本研究所关注的薪酬离散度无关。

17

> **中文：** 17

<!-- page:20 -->

## Source Page 20

> **中文：** 来源第 20 页

more, since firms typically experience greater shareholder scrutiny when benchmarking their CEO pay against that of larger firms, we also examine the relative size of replaced peers. Figure IA.8 in the internet appendix shows that the decline in size dispersion is entirely due to the replacement of larger peers, which suggests a deliberate choice by boards, potentially due to heightened shareholder scrutiny.

> **中文：** 外，由于公司以规模更大的公司作为 CEO 薪酬比较基准时通常会受到更严格的股东监督，我们还考察了被替换同业公司的相对规模。网络附录中的图 IA.8 显示，规模离散度的下降完全源于对规模较大同业公司的替换。这表明董事会是有意作出这一选择的，其潜在原因可能是股东监督的加强。

We next explore whether, along with the increase in industry-size benchmarking, there is a parallel increase in the formation of clusters of firms that benchmark pay against one another. Such a finding would support the idea that an increase in industry-size benchmarking decreases pay dispersion via reciprocal benchmarking (see section 2.1).

> **中文：** 接下来，我们考察随着行业-规模基准比较的增加，相互参照薪酬的公司集群是否也同步增多。若发现这一现象，则将支持如下观点：行业-规模基准比较的增加通过互惠基准比较降低薪酬离散度（参见第 2.1 节）。

Figure 5B plots the values of several network measures based on compensation peer data over the sample period. Based on the literature on networks (Newman, 2010, Ch. 7), we construct three such measures at the firm-year level.18 Reciprocity is the fraction of existing network linkages that are bilateral (i.e., point in both directions). Transitivity is the number of triangles divided by the number of triads that exist in a graph (triads are groups of three nodes that are connected in some way while triangles are triads that are completely connected). Cluster coefficient is the number of triangles divided by the number of possible triads (intuitively, it measures how close a network is to a complete graph). To address potential limitations of the network measures, we also include Fraction of reciprocal references, defined as the fraction of a firm’s compensation peers that reference back the focal firm.19

> **中文：** 图 5B 绘制了样本期内基于薪酬同业公司数据计算的若干网络指标。依据网络研究文献（Newman, 2010, Ch. 7），我们在公司-年度层面构建了三项此类指标。18 互惠性（Reciprocity）是现有网络连接中双向连接（即同时指向两个方向）所占的比例。传递性（Transitivity）是图中三角形数量除以现有三元组数量（三元组是以某种方式相互连接的三个节点所组成的群组，而三角形则是完全连接的三元组）。聚类系数（Cluster coefficient）是三角形数量除以可能形成的三元组数量（直观而言，该指标衡量网络与完全图的接近程度）。为应对这些网络指标可能存在的局限性，我们还纳入了互惠参照比例（Fraction of reciprocal references），其定义为将核心公司反向列入自身薪酬同业组的同业公司占该公司薪酬同业公司的比例。19

As in previous analyses, we rescale the data relative to the start of the sample period. The results, shown in Figure 5B, suggest that compensation peer groups have become significantly more clustered over time. This supports the notion that industry-size benchmarking induces less pay dispersion through an increase in reciprocal benchmarking.20

> **中文：** 与之前的分析相同，我们以样本期初为基准对数据进行了重新缩放。图 5B 所示的结果表明，薪酬同业组随时间推移呈现出显著增强的集群化趋势。这支持了行业-规模基准比较通过增加互惠基准比较来降低薪酬离散度的观点。20

18As the goal is to measure how interconnected a group of firms is, each measure is computed for a firm’s network of its compensation peers that includes not only the base firm’s peer connections but also the connections among the peers (established via their respective peer groups).

> **中文：** 18由于研究目的是衡量一组公司的相互连接程度，因此，每项指标均基于一家公司及其薪酬同业公司组成的网络计算。该网络不仅包括基准公司与其同业公司的连接，还包括同业公司之间通过各自同业组建立的连接。

19On average, firms select 18 compensation peers while industry-size groups are typically larger than 18. Hence, all potential linkages among a firm’s peers cannot be realized. This creates practical upper limits for some of the clustering measures.

> **中文：** 19平均而言，公司选择 18 家薪酬同业公司，而行业-规模组通常包含超过 18 家公司。因此，一家公司各同业公司之间所有潜在的连接不可能全部实现。这对某些集群化指标形成了实际上的上限。

20In Figure IA.9 in the internet appendix, we repeat the analysis in Figure 5B for alternative aggregation levels: the economy-level and several industry levels (GICS2, GICS4, GICS6). That is, for each year, we create a network of all firms in the economy (all firms in a given industry) along with all their peer group

> **中文：** 20在网络附录的图 IA.9 中，我们在其他汇总层级重复了图 5B 的分析，包括总体经济层面和若干行业层面（GICS2、GICS4、GICS6）。具体而言，对于每一年，我们构建一个由经济体内所有公司（某一特定行业内的所有公司）及其全部同业组

4.3. Regression analysis

> **中文：** 4.3. 回归分析

In parallel to our previous tests, we next conduct a regression analysis of the time variation of the industry-size similarity measures in Figure 5A and the network measures in Figure 5B. The analysis is conducted at the firm-year level. As before, we include controls for the focal firm, industry-size, and firm fixed effects.

> **中文：** 与之前的检验相对应，我们接下来对图 5A 中行业-规模相似性指标和图 5B 中网络指标的时间变化进行回归分析。该分析在公司-年度层面进行。与之前一样，我们纳入核心公司的控制变量、行业-规模固定效应和公司固定效应。

We include four metrics of the conformity of the peer group with industry-size benchmarking. Dispersion in relative book values and Dispersion in relative market values are the standard deviations of peers’ relative book value of assets (BVA) or market value of assets (MVA). Deviation from industry-size benchmarking refers to the fraction of peers with a different GICS1 code or that are much larger (>200%) or much smaller (<50%) than the focal firm (in terms of BVA or MVA). ISS conformity refers to the fraction of a firm’s compensation peers that are included in the list of the firm-specific synthetic compensation peers generated by ISS’s peer selection methodology, which is based on size and industry affiliation (see Appendix B for details).21

> **中文：** 我们纳入四项指标，以衡量同业组与行业-规模基准比较的一致程度。相对账面价值离散度（Dispersion in relative book values）和相对市场价值离散度（Dispersion in relative market values）分别是同业公司相对资产账面价值（BVA）或资产市场价值（MVA）的标准差。偏离行业-规模基准比较（Deviation from industry-size benchmarking）是指 GICS1 代码不同，或按 BVA 或 MVA 衡量远大于（>200%）或远小于（<50%）核心公司的同业公司占比。ISS 一致度（ISS conformity）是指一家公司的薪酬同业公司中，被纳入依据 ISS 同业公司选择方法生成的公司特定合成薪酬同业公司名单的比例；该选择方法以规模和行业归属为基础（详见附录 B）。21

The results are presented in Table 3. Table 3A analyzes the conformity of peer groups to industry-size benchmarking. The results in models 1 to 4 corroborate that there is a significant decrease in the dispersion of firm size within compensation peer groups.22 The results in models 5 and 6 show a significant decrease in the fraction of peers that clearly deviate from industry-size benchmarking. Consistently, models 7 and 8 show that the likelihood of including peers that conform with ISS’s peer selection methodology increases significantly over time. Table 3B analyzes network clustering measures. In parallel to Figure 5B, the results reveal a statistically significant trend in all four metrics.

> **中文：** 结果列于表 3。表 3A 分析了同业组与行业-规模基准比较的一致程度。模型 1 至模型 4 的结果进一步证实，薪酬同业组内部公司规模的离散度显著下降。22 模型 5 和模型 6 的结果显示，明显偏离行业-规模基准比较的同业公司占比显著下降。与此一致，模型 7 和模型 8 显示，纳入符合 ISS 同业公司选择方法的同业公司的可能性随时间推移显著提高。表 3B 分析了网络集群化指标。与图 5B 相呼应，结果表明全部四项指标均呈现统计显著的趋势。

> **中文：** 参照关系所组成的网络，随后计算集群化指标。图 IA.9 显示，薪酬网络在所有汇总层级上的集群化程度均有所提高，这支持了上市公司之间逐渐形成更为封闭的薪酬基准比较集群。

21We construct synthetic peer groups because we do not have data on ISS’s peer groups. > **中文：** 来源第 22 页

Finally, we test whether there is a statistical association between pay dispersion and the tendency to select compensation peers based on industry-size benchmarking. That is, we test whether the trends documented in section 3 and in this section go hand in hand not only in the time-series, but also in the cross-section (i.e., after including industry x year fixed effects) and at more granular levels. For this purpose, the analysis is conducted at the firm level and the specification includes firm controls, industry-year fixed effects, and firm fixed effects. As shown in Table 4, pay dispersion is significantly and positively associated with dispersion in size as well as with deviations from industry-size benchmarking. The results also show a statistically strong significant negative association of pay dispersion with the fraction of peers that meet proxy advisors’ selection criteria and with the fraction of reciprocal peers that include the focal firm in their own compensation peer groups.23

> **中文：** 最后，我们检验薪酬离散度与依据行业-规模基准比较选择薪酬同业公司的倾向之间是否存在统计关联。也就是说，我们检验第 3 节和本节记录的趋势是否不仅在时间序列上同步变化，而且在横截面上（即纳入行业 × 年度固定效应后）以及更细的层级上同样如此。为此，该分析在公司层面进行，模型设定包括公司控制变量、行业-年度固定效应和公司固定效应。如表 4 所示，薪酬离散度与规模离散度以及对行业-规模基准比较的偏离均存在显著正相关关系。结果还显示，薪酬离散度与符合代理投票顾问选择标准的同业公司占比，以及将核心公司纳入自身薪酬同业组的互惠同业公司占比之间，均存在统计上高度显著的负相关关系。23

5 . Institutional developments driving peer group selection

> **中文：** 5. 推动同业组选择的制度发展

We next examine the potential drivers of the rise in industry-size benchmarking. As previously explained, we consider the following institutional developments: (i) the SEC’s mandate to disclose compensation peer groups, (ii) the growing influence of proxy advisers, and (iii) the introduction of “say on pay”.

> **中文：** 接下来，我们考察行业-规模基准比较日益普及的潜在驱动因素。如前所述，我们考虑以下制度发展：(i) SEC 强制披露薪酬同业组的规定；(ii) 代理投票顾问影响力的增强；以及 (iii)“薪酬话语权投票（Say on Pay）”制度的引入。

5.1. The 2006 SEC rule on compensation disclosure

> **中文：** 5.1. 2006 年 SEC 薪酬披露规则

We first focus on the 2006 SEC rule mandating public disclosure of compensation peers. We start by testing whether the decline in pay dispersion documented in section 3 occurs after the implementation of the rule in 2007, not before. Table 5A presents results of the analysis at the industry-size level. As shown in models 1-2, we find no significant evidence of

> **中文：** 我们首先关注 SEC 于 2006 年颁布的强制公开披露薪酬同业公司的规则。我们首先检验第 3 节所记录的薪酬离散度下降是否发生在该规则于 2007 年实施之后，而非此前。表 5A 列出了行业-规模层面的分析结果。如模型 1-2 所示，我们没有发现显著证据表明

23We note the potential for interesting heterogeneity in this effect based on the number of firms in an industry: When an industry has many firms, firms that only match on industry have many potential peers to pick from. Hence, initially, there is a lower likelihood for reciprocal benchmarking and therefore greater pay dispersion. However, with industry-size benchmarking, firms are required to select peers that are also similar in size. This then shrinks the number of permissible peers within the industry and results in larger increases in reciprocal benchmarking and hence bigger declines in pay dispersion in such industries. We investigate this idea in Table IA.3 in the internet appendix. We indeed find that industries and industry-size groups with a larger number of firms have initially higher levels of CEO pay dispersion. However, as industry-size benchmarking becomes more prominent over the years, pay dispersion then drops faster in these industries / industry-size groups.

> **中文：** 23我们注意到，这一效应可能因行业内公司数量不同而呈现出值得关注的异质性：当一个行业拥有较多公司时，仅依据行业进行匹配的公司可以从许多潜在同业公司中作出选择。因此，起初形成互惠基准比较的可能性较低，薪酬离散度也因而较高。然而，在采用行业-规模基准比较后，公司还必须选择规模相似的同业公司。这会缩小行业内可选择同业公司的范围，从而使互惠基准比较增幅更大，并因此使这些行业的薪酬离散度降幅更大。我们在网络附录的表 IA.3 中考察了这一观点。我们确实发现，公司数量较多的行业和行业-规模组最初具有更高的 CEO 薪酬离散度。然而，随着行业-规模基准比较逐年变得更加普遍，这些行业／行业-规模组的薪酬离散度随后下降得更快。

Tests based on pooling data from both subsamples reveal that the differences between the 2003-2006 and 2007-2010 subperiods are statistically significant (models 5-6). > **中文：** 薪酬离散度在披露前时期（即 2003-2006 年）有所下降。相比之下，在披露后时期（即 2007-2010 年），我们发现薪酬离散度逐年显著下降（模型 3-4）。基于合并两个子样本数据的检验表明，2003-2006 年与 2007-2010 年两个子时期之间的差异在统计上显著（模型 5-6）。这一结果与图 1B 所示 2007 年前后的单变量趋势一致。

As an alternative way of analyzing the effect of the 2006 SEC disclosure rule, we test whether the post-2007 patterns documented in the previous sections are concentrated among firms with a higher degree of deviation from industry-size benchmarking.24 We measure such degree of deviation using the first disclosures on compensation peers published in 2007. As explained by Faulkender and Yang (2013, 809), the regulatory process of the 2006 SEC rule was relatively quick, leaving no time to modify compensation peer groups in anticipation of the rule. As such, the 2007 disclosures likely reflect ex-ante (i.e., absent the disclosure requirement) choices of compensation peers.25

> **中文：** 作为分析 2006 年 SEC 披露规则影响的另一种方式，我们检验前述各节记录的 2007 年后模式是否集中出现在对行业-规模基准比较偏离程度较高的公司中。24 我们利用 2007 年首次公布的薪酬同业公司披露信息衡量这种偏离程度。正如 Faulkender and Yang (2013, 809) 所解释的，2006 年 SEC 规则的监管制定过程相对迅速，公司没有时间为预先应对该规则而修改薪酬同业组。因此，2007 年的披露信息很可能反映了事前的薪酬同业公司选择，即不存在披露要求时的选择。25

The results in Table 5B suggest that the patterns documented in the previous sections for the period immediately after the introduction of the SEC rule – the decline in pay dispersion, the decline in deviations from industry-size benchmarking, and the increase in conformity with ISS – are concentrated among firms with lower initial conformity with the industry-size criterion in the selection of their compensation peers. 5.2. Proxy adviser influence

> **中文：** 5.2. 代理投票顾问的影响

We next examine the role of proxy advisers in the documented increase in industry-size benchmarking. We conduct three sets of tests. First, we study the influence of ISS’s policy in the composition of the compensation peer groups. Second, we study the influence of ISS’s policy in the exclusion/inclusion of a firm from/in the focal firm’s compensation peer group. Third, we study the role of passive investing since fund managers of passive investing vehicles are more likely to rely on proxy adviser recommendations.

> **中文：** 接下来，我们考察代理投票顾问在前文所记录的行业-规模基准比较增加中所发挥的作用。我们进行三组检验。第一，我们研究 ISS 的政策对薪酬同业组构成的影响。第二，我们研究 ISS 的政策对一家公司被排除在核心公司的薪酬同业组之外或被纳入其中的影响。第三，我们研究被动投资的作用，因为被动投资工具的基金经理更有可能依赖代理投票顾问的建议。

5.2.1. Composition of compensation peer groups and ISS policy

> **中文：** 5.2.1. 薪酬同业组的构成与 ISS 政策

Our first set of tests examine whether the composition of firms’ compensation peer groups is related to ISS’s peer selection methodology for compensation benchmarking. As previously explained, ISS ranks all potential peers based on whether they are in the same industry and of similar size. It then selects the first n peers in the ranking, where n varies from 14 to 24 depending on the number of firms in the industry of the subject firm (in most cases, n=24; see Appendix B for details).

> **中文：** 第一组检验考察公司薪酬同业组的构成是否与 ISS 用于薪酬基准比较的同业公司选择方法有关。如前所述，ISS 根据所有潜在同业公司是否处于同一行业以及规模是否相近对其进行排名。随后，ISS 选择排名最靠前的 n 家同业公司，其中 n 根据被评估公司所在行业的公司数量而在 14 至 24 之间变化（在大多数情况下，n=24；详见附录 B）。

To gauge the potential effect of this policy, we conduct two tests. We start by examining whether the position in the ranking generated by ISS’s policy is associated with the likelihood that a given firm is included by the focal firm in its compensation peer group. For each focal firm, we include all potential peers from the same GICS2 industry and rank them based on ISS’s publicly disclosed methodology. We refer to firms’ position in this ranking as ISS rank (where ISS rank equal to 1 implies the most closely matched peer and higher ranks indicate a lower fit). We then test the association between this variable and Included in peer group, which equals one if the firm is included in the focal firm’s compensation peer group, and zero otherwise. We restrict the analysis to the period 2012-2023, as ISS published its methodology

> **中文：** 为评估该政策的潜在影响，我们进行两项检验。首先，我们考察由 ISS 政策生成的排名位置是否与某家公司被核心公司纳入其薪酬同业组的可能性相关。对于每一家核心公司，我们纳入同一 GICS2 行业中的所有潜在同业公司，并依据 ISS 公开披露的方法对其进行排名。我们将公司在该排名中的位置称为 ISS rank（ISS rank 等于 1 表示匹配程度最高的同业公司，排名数值越大则表示匹配程度越低）。随后，我们检验该变量与 Included in peer group 之间的关联；如果该公司被纳入核心公司的薪酬同业组，该变量等于 1，否则等于 0。由于 ISS 公布其方法的时间是

22

> **中文：** 22

<!-- page:25 -->

## Source Page 25

> **中文：** 来源第 25 页

in December 2011. The specification includes a host of fixed effects that fully exploit the granularity of the data, including firm-by-year and peer-by-year fixed effects (which control for unobserved time-varying firm and peer characteristics such as factors leading both ISS and firms to independently include or exclude a peer).26 We further add variables to account for the relative differences in firm characteristics between a focal firm and each of its potential peers.

> **中文：** 2011 年 12 月，因此我们将分析限制在 2012-2023 年期间。模型设定包含一系列充分利用数据细粒度特征的固定效应，包括公司×年份固定效应和同业公司×年份固定效应（这些固定效应控制不可观测且随时间变化的公司及同业公司特征，例如同时促使 ISS 和公司各自独立纳入或排除某家同业公司的因素）。26 我们还加入若干变量，以控制核心公司与其每一家潜在同业公司之间在公司特征方面的相对差异。

Table 6A presents the results. The negative coefficient on ISS rank confirms the predictive power of the ISS rankings: a higher ISS rank for a potential peer (indicating a lower fit with ISS’s criteria) decreases the probability that the firm includes the peer into its peer group. Panel A also examines whether ISS’s peer selection policy has become more influential over time (ISS’s influence could have increased due to the growth of passive investing and the introduction of SOP). The negative and significant coefficients on the interaction variable ISS rank × Trend confirms the increasing importance of ISS’s policy on peer selection over time. With each passing year, the probability that a potential peer is chosen after improving its rank in ISS’s methodology by one increases by 0.5 percentage points (models 1-3). This is an economically large effect considering that the unconditional average probability of selection for any given peer is 0.75 percent. These results hold in univariate tests as well as in multivariate tests that include demanding fixed effects.

> **中文：** 表 6A 报告了结果。ISS rank 的负系数证实了 ISS 排名的预测能力：潜在同业公司的 ISS rank 越高（表明其与 ISS 标准的匹配程度越低），公司将该同业公司纳入其同业组的概率就越低。面板 A 还考察 ISS 的同业公司选择政策是否随时间推移产生了更大的影响（被动投资的发展和 SOP 的引入可能增强了 ISS 的影响力）。交互变量 ISS rank × Trend 的系数显著为负，证实 ISS 政策对同业公司选择的重要性随时间推移而提高。每过一年，潜在同业公司在 ISS 方法中的排名每改善一位，其被选中的概率便增加 0.5 个百分点（模型 1-3）。考虑到任意一家同业公司被选中的无条件平均概率为 0.75%，这一效应在经济意义上相当大。无论是在单变量检验中，还是在包含严格固定效应的多变量检验中，这些结果均成立。

To mitigate the concern that using the universe of potential GICS2-peers could result in inflated significance levels (as it increases the sample size), we repeat the analysis while focusing only on the top-ranked 18 peers (which is the size of the average peer group; see Table IA.2). The signs of the coefficients in models 4-6 are consistent with those in models 1-3. In sum, the results in Table 6A suggest that the conformity with the industry-size peer benchmarking criteria used by ISS matters for peer selection and has become increasingly important over time.

> **中文：** 为缓解使用全部潜在 GICS2 同业公司可能因扩大样本量而夸大显著性水平的担忧，我们仅以排名最高的 18 家同业公司为研究对象重复上述分析（18 是同业组的平均规模；见表 IA.2）。模型 4-6 中的系数符号与模型 1-3 一致。总之，表 6A 的结果表明，是否符合 ISS 采用的行业-规模同业基准比较标准会影响同业公司选择，而且其重要性随时间推移而不断提高。

varies from 14 to 24 (see Appendix B for details).27 For each focal firm, we first compute the number of potential peers in conformity with the ISS criterion (which depends on the number of similar-sized firms in the same industry) and then rank these potential peers from 1 up to 100 following ISS’s methodology. We then plot in Figure 6 the probability that a potential peer is included in the focal firm’s actual compensation peer group based on the distance between the peer’s position in the ranking with respect to the cutoff used by ISS (i.e., between 14 and 24). For example, for a focal firm with an ISS recommended peer group consisting of 24 peers, a potential peer ranked 23rd (25th) would have a relative rank of -1 (1). For each focal firm, the sample consists of potential peers that were ranked just below, at, or just above the ISS size threshold – i.e., potential peers with relative ranks -1, 0 or 1. We regress Included in peer group (as previously defined) on indicator variables for whether a potential peer firm is just at ISS’s threshold (e.g., the 24th ranked firm) or just above it (e.g., 25th ranked firm).29 The coefficients on the indicator variables capture the incremental probability that a potential peer at or just above the ISS size threshold is included in the focal firm’s actual compensation peer group relative to a potential peer ranked just below the ISS size threshold for the firm. > **中文：** 表 6B 报告了该检验的多变量版本。对于每一家核心公司，样本由排名恰好位于 ISS 规模阈值之下、正好处于该阈值或恰好位于该阈值之上的潜在同业公司组成，即相对排名为 -1、0 或 1 的潜在同业公司。我们将 Included in peer group（定义同前）对若干指示变量进行回归，这些指示变量分别表示潜在同业公司是否恰好处于 ISS 的阈值位置（例如排名第 24 位的公司）或恰好高于该阈值所涵盖的范围（例如排名第 25 位的公司）。29 这些指示变量的系数衡量：相对于排名恰好位于该公司 ISS 规模阈值之下的潜在同业公司，处于或恰好超出 ISS 规模阈值的潜在同业公司被纳入核心公司实际薪酬同业组的增量概率。我们进一步将样本期扩展至包括 2007 年至 2011 年。这样做是为了利用研究情境中的另一项制度特征：ISS 首次公布其同业公司选择方法是在

28We note that ISS publishes annually for each firm a “proxy advisory report” in which it names all the peers that it considers appropriate for a firm as given by its methodology. > **中文：** 28需要指出的是，ISS 每年都会针对每家公司发布一份“代理投票顾问报告”，并在其中列出依据其方法认定适合该公司的所有同业公司。薪酬委员会及其顾问很可能知悉这些报告，从而提高报告中所列同业公司被选中的可能性。
