the first time in its “U.S. Corporate Governance Policy 2012 Update” on December 20, 2011 (see Gibson, 2011). The specific timing of this policy change allows us to analyze whether the discontinuity appears only as of 2012 – i.e., the first year in which ISS implemented the change in peer selection methodology. Table 6B shows that this is indeed the case: we do not find that the ranking relative to the size cutoff matters prior to ISS’s policy change in 2012 (see models 1-5). > **中文：** 2011 年 12 月 20 日发布的《U.S. Corporate Governance Policy 2012 Update》中（见 Gibson，2011）。这一政策变更的具体时点使我们能够分析上述不连续变化是否仅从 2012 年开始出现，即 ISS 实施同业公司选择方法变更的第一年。表 6B 表明，实际情况确实如此：在 ISS 于 2012 年改变政策之前，我们并未发现相对于规模截点的排名会产生影响（见模型 1-5）。相比之下，2012 年之后，当潜在同业公司的排名恰好位于 ISS 推荐同业组规模之外时，其被选中的可能性会出现统计上显著的下降（见模型 6-10）。

5.2.2. Peer group additions/exclusions and ISS policy

> **中文：** 5.2.2. 同业组的新增与排除及 ISS 政策

Our second set of tests examines whether exclusion/addition of a potential peer from/to the ISS recommended peer group is associated with an exclusion/addition of that firm from/to the focal firm’s disclosed compensation peer group in the following year. The analysis, shown in Table 7, is conducted at the firm-peer-year level.

> **中文：** 第二组检验考察某家潜在同业公司被排除出 ISS 推荐同业组或被加入该同业组，是否与该公司在下一年被排除出核心公司披露的薪酬同业组或被加入该同业组相关。表 7 报告的分析在公司-同业公司-年份层面进行。

We first focus on exclusions. The dependent variable, Dropped peer is an indicator  
t+1  
variable for whether a peer in year t is excluded from the focal firm’s compensation peer group in year t+1. On the right-hand side, Dropped by ISS in t is an indicator variable that equals one if ISS had included a peer in year t − 1 in its peer group but dropped it from its recommended peer group in year t. The specification includes a host of control variables to control for the most common reasons for which firms are usually excluded.30 Like in Table 6, we again add firm-by-year and peer-by-year fixed effects to control for unobserved time-varying firm and peer characteristics.

> **中文：** 我们首先关注同业公司的排除。因变量 Dropped peer  
> t+1  
> 是一个指示变量，表示年份 t 的某家同业公司是否在年份 t+1 被排除出核心公司的薪酬同业组。在回归式右侧，Dropped by ISS in t 是一个指示变量；如果 ISS 在年份 t − 1 将某家同业公司纳入其同业组，但在年份 t 将其排除出推荐同业组，则该变量等于 1。模型设定包含一系列控制变量，用以控制公司通常排除同业公司的最常见原因。30 与表 6 一样，我们再次加入公司×年份固定效应和同业公司×年份固定效应，以控制不可观测且随时间变化的公司及同业公司特征。

To further tighten identification, in model 4 we focus the analysis on a narrow window around the peer group size cutoff used by ISS. Specifically, we define Just dropped below ISS

> **中文：** 为进一步加强识别，在模型 4 中，我们将分析集中于 ISS 所采用同业组规模截点附近的一个狭窄窗口。具体而言，我们将 Just dropped below ISS

30The vector of control variables is as follows. In ISS peer group at t-1 is an indicator variable for whether the firm met ISS peer selection criteria in the previous period. Peer delisted at t is an indicator variable which is equal to 1 if the peer firm was delisted from the stock exchange in year t (e.g., as a result of a merger, bankruptcy or liquidation). Change in relative market value is the annual change (from year t−1 to year t) in the relative market value of the peer (i.e., peer’s market value scaled by focal firm’s market value). Similarly, Change in relative sales is the annual change (from year t − 1 to year t) in the relative sales of the peer. Finally, Total assets, Tobin’s Q, Sales growth, Stock return, and Idiosyncratic volatility are the usual controls for firm characteristics as in Table 2B (see Appendix A for definitions).

> **中文：** 30控制变量向量如下。In ISS peer group at t-1 是一个指示变量，表示该公司在上一期是否符合 ISS 的同业公司选择标准。Peer delisted at t 是一个指示变量；如果同业公司在年份 t 从证券交易所退市（例如因合并、破产或清算而退市），则该变量等于 1。Change in relative market value 是同业公司相对市场价值的年度变化（从年份 t−1 至年份 t），其中相对市场价值是同业公司的市场价值除以核心公司的市场价值。类似地，Change in relative sales 是同业公司相对销售额的年度变化（从年份 t − 1 至年份 t）。最后，Total assets、Tobin’s Q、Sales growth、Stock return 和 Idiosyncratic volatility 是与表 2B 相同的常用公司特征控制变量（定义见附录 A）。

> **中文：** 25

## Source Page 28

> **中文：** 来源第 28 页

cutoff as an indicator variable for whether the peer was inside ISS’s peer group size cutoff in t − 1 (i.e., relative rank -4 to 0) and just outside the cutoff in year t (i.e., relative rank 1 to 5).31 Firms in the vicinity of the size cutoff should be almost identical in firm characteristics and therefore should have – absent any ISS influence – a similar probability of being included in the focal firm’s compensation peer group.

> **中文：** cutoff 定义为一个指示变量，表示某家同业公司在 t − 1 年位于 ISS 同业组规模截点以内（即相对排名为 -4 至 0），但在年份 t 恰好位于该截点之外（即相对排名为 1 至 5）。31 位于规模截点附近的公司在公司特征方面应当几乎完全相同。因此，在不存在 ISS 影响的情况下，它们被纳入核心公司薪酬同业组的概率应当相近。

In parallel to the previous tests, we also analyze whether a firm is more likely to add a peer to its benchmark group after ISS policy adds the peer to ISS’s recommended peer group in the prior year. Because it relates to additions (rather than exclusions), we include for each focal firm the universe of potential peers with non-missing data (which results in a much higher number of observations). In parallel to the above tests on deletions, we also define an indicator variable Just rose above ISS cutoff.

> **中文：** 与前述检验相对应，我们还分析：在 ISS 的政策于上一年将某家同业公司加入 ISS 推荐同业组后，公司是否更有可能将该同业公司加入其基准组。由于该分析涉及新增而非排除，我们针对每一家核心公司纳入数据非缺失的全部潜在同业公司，因而产生了数量多得多的观测值。与上述排除检验相对应，我们还定义了指示变量 Just rose above ISS cutoff。

Table 7 presents the results of the two sets of analysis. Models 1-3 show that firms are more likely to exclude a peer from their benchmark groups when the peer is excluded from their corresponding ISS peer groups in the prior year. Using the narrow subset of peers in the vicinity of the ISS rank cutoff, we find that peers that fall just below the ISS cutoff are also more likely to be excluded from firms’ compensation peer group (model 4). This is consistent with the notion that firms exclude peers that do not conform with ISS’s selection criteria. Models 5-8 show consistent patterns for additions (rather than exclusions) into compensation peer groups. In model 8, a potential peer that was ranked just outside ISS’s recommended peer group in year t − 1 (i.e., relative rank 1-5) but ranked just inside ISS’s peer group in year t (i.e., relative rank -4 to 0) is more likely to be added by the focal firm to its peer group in the following year. This further supports the idea that ISS’s industry-sized based rankings play a causal role in firms’ adoption of industry-size benchmarking policies.

> **中文：** 表 7 报告了这两组分析的结果。模型 1-3 表明，如果某家同业公司在上一年被排除出相应的 ISS 同业组，公司就更有可能将其排除出自身的基准组。使用 ISS 排名截点附近的狭窄同业公司子样本时，我们发现，刚刚跌至 ISS 截点之外的同业公司也更有可能被排除出公司的薪酬同业组（模型 4）。这一结果与公司会排除不符合 ISS 选择标准的同业公司这一观点一致。模型 5-8 显示，将同业公司加入而非排除出薪酬同业组时也存在一致的模式。在模型 8 中，如果某家潜在同业公司在年份 t − 1 的排名恰好位于 ISS 推荐同业组之外（即相对排名为 1-5），但在年份 t 的排名恰好进入 ISS 同业组以内（即相对排名为 -4 至 0），则核心公司更有可能在下一年将其加入自身的同业组。这进一步支持了如下观点：ISS 基于行业和规模的排名在公司采用行业-规模基准比较政策的过程中发挥了因果作用。

5.2.3. ISS and role of passive investing

> **中文：** 5.2.3. ISS 与被动投资的作用

In our final test on proxy advisor influence, we analyze whether the increased conformity to the industry-size benchmarking criterion we document in previous tests is more pronounced

> **中文：** 在关于代理投票顾问影响的最后一项检验中，我们分析前述检验所记录的对行业-规模基准比较标准的遵循程度上升是否在某些情况下更为显著

31We take a window of ±5 ranks around the cutoff, to which we refer as “relative rank 0”. We choose a window of ±5 ranks since reducing it further leaves too few instances in which a potential peer was ranked just inside the cutoff in one year and ranked just outside of it the next year.

> **中文：** 31我们在截点附近选取 ±5 个排名位置的窗口，并将该截点称为“相对排名 0”。之所以选择 ±5 个排名位置的窗口，是因为如果进一步缩小窗口，潜在同业公司在某一年排名恰好位于截点以内、而在下一年排名恰好位于截点之外的情形就会过少。

26

> **中文：** 26

<!-- page:29 -->

---

## Source Page 29

among firms exposed to more passive investing. Due to large, dispersed portfolios and low-fee services, passive investors are more likely to economize on their monitoring of portfolio firms and are therefore more likely to vote along proxy advisor recommendations. We therefore expect boards of firms with greater levels of passive investors to adopt peer selection practices that show greater conformity with the industry-size benchmarking criterion.

> **中文：** 在被动投资敞口更高的公司中，情况尤其如此。由于投资组合规模庞大且较为分散，同时提供低费率服务，被动投资者更有可能节省对投资组合公司的监督成本，因此也更有可能按照代理投票顾问的建议进行投票。因此，我们预期，被动投资者持股水平较高的公司，其董事会采用的同业公司选择实践将更符合行业-规模基准比较标准。

The analysis is conducted at the firm-year level using the same dependent variables as in previous tests, namely Size dispersion (size measured as BVA and MVA), Deviation from industry-size benchmarking, and ISS conformity. Our measures of the influence of passive investing on a given firm are grounded in prior literature showing that such influence is a function of investors’ level of ownership and based on their incentives to monitor. Fraction shares owned by institutional investors is the fraction of shares owned by institutional investors in a given firm-year. Fraction shares owned by quasi-indexers is the fraction of shares in a firm-year owned by quasi-indexers (as classified by Bushee and Noe, 2000 and Bushee, 2001). Fraction shares owned by index mutual funds is the fraction of shares owned by mutual funds that follow index investing (as defined in Appel, Gormley and Keim, 2016). Finally, to more directly measure proxy advisory influence on firm investors, Propensity to vote with ISS is the fraction of shares owned by mutual funds that in prior years voted following ISS’s advice when ISS and the firm’s management gave conflicting voting advice (Larcker, McCall and Ormazabal, 2013, 2015). Similar to Table 4, we include Industry-by-year fixed effects in all models so that the analysis examines cross-sectional associations.

> **中文：** 本文在公司-年度层面开展分析，使用与前述检验相同的因变量，即 Size dispersion（规模离散度，规模分别以 BVA 和 MVA 衡量）、Deviation from industry-size benchmarking（偏离行业-规模基准比较）以及 ISS conformity（ISS 一致性）。我们对被动投资对特定公司影响的衡量以既有文献为基础；这些文献表明，这种影响取决于投资者的持股水平，并以其监督激励为基础。Fraction shares owned by institutional investors（机构投资者持股比例）是指在特定公司-年度中由机构投资者持有的股份比例。Fraction shares owned by quasi-indexers（准指数投资者持股比例）是指在特定公司-年度中由准指数投资者持有的股份比例（分类依据为 Bushee and Noe, 2000 和 Bushee, 2001）。Fraction shares owned by index mutual funds（指数共同基金持股比例）是指遵循指数投资策略的共同基金所持有的股份比例（定义依据为 Appel, Gormley and Keim, 2016）。最后，为了更直接地衡量代理投票顾问对公司投资者的影响，Propensity to vote with ISS（与 ISS 一致投票的倾向）是指由共同基金持有的股份比例，且这些共同基金在以往年份中，当 ISS 与公司管理层提出相互冲突的投票建议时，曾按照 ISS 的建议进行投票（Larcker, McCall and Ormazabal, 2013, 2015）。与 Table 4 类似，我们在所有模型中均纳入 Industry-by-year fixed effects（行业×年度固定效应），从而使分析考察横截面关联。

Table 8 presents the results. Models 1-4 show that firms with greater ownership by institutional investors also engage in more industry-size benchmarking and have greater compliance with ISS’s peer selection methodology. Consistently, industry-size benchmarking is also significantly and positively correlated with ownership by quasi-indexers (models 5-8), with ownership by index mutual funds (models 9-12), and with the propensity of a firm’s mutual fund owners to vote alongside ISS recommendations (models 13-16). We note that the coefficients tend to increase in magnitude as the proxies for passive investing become more focused on passive investing and a greater likelihood of voting alongside ISS. While

> **中文：** Table 8 报告了检验结果。模型 1-4 表明，机构投资者持股比例较高的公司也更多地采用行业-规模基准比较，并且更加符合 ISS 的同业公司选择方法。与此一致，行业-规模基准比较还与准指数投资者持股比例（模型 5-8）、指数共同基金持股比例（模型 9-12），以及公司共同基金股东按照 ISS 建议进行投票的倾向（模型 13-16）呈显著正相关。我们注意到，随着被动投资的代理变量更加聚焦于被动投资以及更高的与 ISS 一致投票概率，相关系数的绝对值往往随之增大。尽管

descriptive, the results of these tests are consistent with the notion that passive investing promotes the adoption of industry-size benchmarking through proxy advisory influence.

> **中文：** 这些检验结果属于描述性证据，但与以下观点一致：被动投资通过代理投票顾问的影响，促进了行业-规模基准比较的采用。

### 5.3. Say on pay

> **中文：** 5.3. 薪酬话语权投票（Say on Pay）

To empirically identify the role of “say on pay” (SOP) in the documented increase in industry-size benchmarking, we exploit two sources of variation: (i) weak SOP votes and (ii) close shareholder votes on SOP vote frequency.

> **中文：** 为了从实证上识别“薪酬话语权投票”（say on pay，SOP）在前文所记录的行业-规模基准比较增加过程中所发挥的作用，我们利用两种变异来源：(i) 较低的 SOP 投票支持率；以及 (ii) 关于 SOP 投票频率的结果接近的股东投票。

### 5.3.1. Weak SOP votes

> **中文：** 5.3.1. 较低的 SOP 投票支持率

In the first set of tests, we examine whether firms receiving a weak SOP vote are more likely to subsequently select peers based on the industry-size criterion. We conduct the analysis at the firm-year level. To avoid confounding effects, we focus on firms’ first say on pay votes in 2011 or 2012.32 We take a three-year window around each firm’s first SOP vote. The “treatment” group includes firms with weak SOP vote support. The control group includes firms without weak SOP votes. Control firms are matched to treated firms based on industry and stock returns (performance is a frequent determinant of say on pay vote outcomes). This results in 139 and 199 firms in the treatment and control groups, respectively.

> **中文：** 在第一组检验中，我们考察获得较低 SOP 投票支持率的公司，随后是否更有可能依据行业-规模标准选择同业公司。我们在公司-年度层面开展分析。为避免混杂效应，我们聚焦于公司在 2011 年或 2012 年进行的首次薪酬话语权投票。32 我们以每家公司首次 SOP 投票为中心，选取一个三年窗口。“处理组”包括 SOP 投票支持率较低的公司；控制组则包括未获得较低 SOP 投票支持率的公司。我们依据行业和股票收益率，将控制组公司与处理组公司进行匹配（公司业绩通常是薪酬话语权投票结果的重要决定因素）。最终，处理组和控制组分别包含 139 家和 199 家公司。

The dependent variables are as in section 3 and 4, namely Size dispersion (size measured as BVA and MVA), Deviation from industry-size benchmarking, and ISS conformity. On the right-hand side, Weak SOP support is an indicator variable for whether the firm ranks in the lowest decile of the SOP vote distribution (in our sample, the lowest decile includes SOP votes that received less than 75 percent support).33 Given the delay between shareholder voting and compensation contracting, we interact this variable with annual indicator variables for the first, second, and third year following the weak SOP vote support (Post Year

> **中文：** 因变量与第 3 节和第 4 节相同，即 Size dispersion（规模离散度，规模分别以 BVA 和 MVA 衡量）、Deviation from industry-size benchmarking（偏离行业-规模基准比较）以及 ISS conformity（ISS 一致性）。在等式右侧，Weak SOP support（较低的 SOP 支持率）是一个指示变量，用于表示公司是否位于 SOP 投票分布的最低十分位数（在我们的样本中，最低十分位数包括支持率低于 75% 的 SOP 投票）。33 鉴于股东投票与薪酬契约订立之间存在时滞，我们将该变量分别与获得较低 SOP 投票支持率之后第一年、第二年和第三年的年度指示变量进行交互（Post Year

32SOP regulation became mandatory for the first annual shareholder meeting after January 1, 2011. Since SOP votes are backwards looking, the first vote concerned pay policies for fiscal years 2010 or 2011.

> **中文：** 32 SOP 监管规定自 2011 年 1 月 1 日之后召开的首次年度股东大会起成为强制性要求。由于 SOP 投票具有回顾性，首次投票涉及的是 2010 或 2011 财政年度的薪酬政策。

33Vote support in SOP proposals is highly skewed. However, proxy advisory firms and compensation consultants consider vote support below 70 percent already as a negative view of firms’ compensation practices. ISS, for example, adopted a policy in November 2011 to provide case-by-case voting recommendations on compensation committee members if a company’s prior year say on pay vote outcome was below 70 percent. In 2016, Glass Lewis and ISS established so-called “red zones” that trigger greater scrutiny when opposition votes exceed 20-25 percent.

> **中文：** 33 SOP 提案的投票支持率呈高度偏斜分布。在涵盖超过 13,000 次此类投票的样本中，平均（中位数）支持率为 90.9%（95.8%），仅有 2% 的 SOP 提案获得的支持率低于 50%。然而，代理投票顾问公司和薪酬顾问已将低于 70% 的投票支持率视为对公司薪酬实践的负面评价。例如，ISS 于 2011 年 11 月实施了一项政策：如果一家公司上一年度的薪酬话语权投票支持率低于 70%，则针对其薪酬委员会成员逐案提出投票建议。2016 年，Glass Lewis 和 ISS 设立了所谓的“红区”；当反对票比例超过 20-25% 时，将触发更严格的审查。

### 5.3.2. SOP vote frequency

> **中文：** 5.3.2. SOP 投票频率

To further sharpen identification, Table 10 presents a variant of the previous tests that exploits plausibly exogenous variation in the frequency of SOP voting. Specifically, at the introduction of SOP voting, firms were required to also vote on the frequency of future SOP consultations (the choices were every 1, 2, or 3 years). In the majority of firms, shareholders supported an annual SOP vote (77%) while shareholders in most remaining firms (22%) supported having SOP voting at a 3-year frequency (only 1% approved a 2-year frequency). However, in 67 cases of the Russell 3000, investor support was almost equally distributed among the two options. Following prior research (Cuñat, Gine and Guadalupe, 2012), we exploit the quasi-random variation in the close votes of those firms to enhance the empirical identification of the effect of SOP voting on industry-size benchmarking.35

> **中文：** 为了进一步增强识别，Table 10 给出了前述检验的一种变体，该检验利用 SOP 投票频率中可被合理视为外生的变异。具体而言，在引入 SOP 投票时，公司还必须就未来 SOP 咨询投票的频率进行表决（可选择每 1 年、2 年或 3 年进行一次）。在大多数公司中，股东支持每年进行一次 SOP 投票（77%）；在其余大多数公司中（22%），股东支持每三年进行一次 SOP 投票（仅有 1% 的公司批准每两年进行一次）。然而，在 Russell 3000 指数成分公司中，有 67 家公司的投资者支持票几乎均等地分布于这两个选项。依循既有研究（Cuñat, Gine and Guadalupe, 2012），我们利用这些公司在结果接近的投票中产生的准随机变异，增强对 SOP 投票影响行业-规模基准比较这一效应的实证识别。35

We compare firms whose shareholders narrowly voted in favor of a 1-year SOP vote frequency with those whose shareholders narrowly voted for a 3-year SOP vote. Conceivably, a higher frequency of SOP voting puts more pressure on firms to accommodate compensation

> **中文：** 我们将股东以微弱优势投票支持每年进行一次 SOP 投票的公司，与股东以微弱优势投票支持每三年进行一次 SOP 投票的公司进行比较。可以设想，更高的 SOP 投票频率会给公司带来更大压力，促使其调整薪酬

34Table IA.5 in the internet appendix shows that firms with weak SOP vote support also exhibit higher pay dispersion which then decreases significantly in the years after the weak vote.

> **中文：** 34 网络附录中的 Table IA.5 表明，SOP 投票支持率较低的公司还表现出更高的薪酬离散度，而该离散度在较低支持率投票之后的数年中显著下降。

35To increase the power of the test (close SOP frequency votes are rare), we expand the sample in this test from S&P1500 firms to R3000 firms. Of the 67 firms with close say on pay votes (defined as cases where the difference between the support for a 1-year SOP vote frequency and the support for a 3-year SOP vote frequency is within ±5 percentage points) 31 firms are part of the S&P1500. In 35 firms (32 firms), shareholders voted for SOP votes each year (every three years).

> **中文：** 35 为提高检验功效（结果接近的 SOP 频率投票较为罕见），我们在该项检验中将样本从 S&P1500 公司扩展至 R3000 公司。在薪酬话语权投票结果接近的 67 家公司中（定义为支持每年进行一次 SOP 投票与支持每三年进行一次 SOP 投票的比例之差在 ±5 个百分点以内），有 31 家属于 S&P1500 公司。在 35 家公司（32 家公司）中，股东投票支持每年（每三年）进行一次 SOP 投票。

practices to standard governance criteria, notably industry-size benchmarking. We take a narrow 3-year post window after the first SOP frequency vote event in firms (which occurred in calendar years 2011-2013) so that firms with a 3-year SOP vote frequency have benchmarking policies that are affected only by a single (their first) SOP vote whereas firms with an annual SOP vote frequency have held several SOP votes during that period. Focusing on firms with close SOP vote events allows us to maximize randomness in the voting outcome. As shown in Table IA.6 in the internet appendix, the sample firms with 1- and 3-year SOP vote schedules are identical in firm characteristics.

> **中文：** 实践以适应标准治理准则，尤其是行业-规模基准比较。我们选取公司首次 SOP 频率投票事件（发生于 2011-2013 日历年度）之后一个较窄的三年窗口，从而使每三年进行一次 SOP 投票的公司，其基准比较政策仅受到一次 SOP 投票（即首次投票）的影响，而每年进行一次 SOP 投票的公司则在此期间已经举行了数次 SOP 投票。聚焦于 SOP 投票结果接近的公司，使我们能够最大限度地提高投票结果的随机性。如网络附录中的 Table IA.6 所示，采用一年期和三年期 SOP 投票安排的样本公司在公司特征方面相同。

The dependent variables are as in Table 9. On the right-hand side, Annual SOP vote frequency is an indicator for whether a 1-year SOP vote frequency was narrowly chosen over a 3-year SOP vote frequency. Post is an indicator variable for the fiscal years after a firm’s first SOP frequency vote. The multivariate specifications include firm controls (as in sections 3 and 4) and industry-year fixed effects.36

> **中文：** 因变量与 Table 9 相同。在等式右侧，Annual SOP vote frequency（年度 SOP 投票频率）是一个指示变量，用于表示每年进行一次 SOP 投票是否以微弱优势击败每三年进行一次 SOP 投票而获选。Post 是一个指示变量，表示公司首次 SOP 频率投票之后的财政年度。多变量模型设定包括公司层面的控制变量（与第 3 节和第 4 节相同）以及行业-年度固定效应。36

The results, presented in Table 10, are in line with those in Table 9. Relative to firms whose shareholders narrowly opted for a 3-year SOP vote frequency, firms with annual SOP votes exhibit larger declines in their peer group size dispersion and greater conformity with the industry-size benchmarking criterion after the vote. As shown in Figure 7, we do not find such patterns in the period prior to the implementation of SOP in 2010 (i.e., the parallel trends assumption seems to hold). This evidence supports a causal relationship between SOP voting and industry-size benchmarking.

> **中文：** Table 10 所报告的结果与 Table 9 的结果一致。与股东以微弱优势选择每三年进行一次 SOP 投票的公司相比，每年进行 SOP 投票的公司在投票之后表现出更大幅度的同业组规模离散度下降，并且与行业-规模基准比较标准的一致性更高。如 Figure 7 所示，在 2010 年实施 SOP 之前的时期，我们并未发现这种模式（即平行趋势假设似乎成立）。这一证据支持 SOP 投票与行业-规模基准比较之间存在因果关系。

## 6 . Conclusion

> **中文：** 6. 结论

Using a wide sample of public U.S. firms spanning from 1996 to 2023, this paper documents a new stylized fact; over the last decade, the cross-sectional variation in CEO pay levels has declined precipitously. The decline in pay dispersion is very robust empirically and cannot be explained by a decline in the use of stock options and/or by an increased similarity in firm fundamentals. We propose one explanation for this secular decrease in pay variation,

> **中文：** 本文使用涵盖 1996 年至 2023 年的大规模美国上市公司样本，记录了一个新的典型事实：在过去十年中，CEO 薪酬水平的横截面差异急剧下降。薪酬离散度下降这一现象在实证上非常稳健，无法由股票期权使用减少和／或公司基本面相似性提高来解释。我们针对薪酬差异的这种长期下降提出了一种解释，

36We use GICS1 industries for the fixed effects given the low number of firms per industry in the sample.

> **中文：** 36 鉴于样本中每个行业的公司数量较少，我们使用 GICS1 行业设置固定效应。

30

<!-- page:33 -->

## Source Page 33

the rise of industry-size benchmarking. That is, firms are increasingly likely to benchmark CEO compensation to the industry peers closest in size.

> **中文：** 即行业-规模基准比较的兴起。换言之，公司越来越有可能以规模最为接近的行业同业公司为基准来确定 CEO 薪酬。

We show that the decrease in pay dispersion goes hand in hand with an increasing tendency to benchmark CEO compensation to the industry peers closest in size. We provide evidence consistent with the notion that three institutional developments have contributed to the rise of industry-size benchmarking; the 2006 SEC disclosure rule mandating disclosure of the peers used for compensation benchmarking that increased transparency on the pay setting process, the growing influence of proxy advisors, and shareholder advisory votes on executives’ compensation packages (“say on pay”).

> **中文：** 我们表明，薪酬离散度的下降与公司越来越倾向于以规模最为接近的行业同业公司为基准确定 CEO 薪酬这一趋势相伴而生。我们提供的证据与以下观点一致：三项制度发展促成了行业-规模基准比较的兴起，包括 2006 年 SEC 披露规则强制要求披露用于薪酬基准比较的同业公司，从而提高薪酬设定过程的透明度；代理投票顾问的影响力日益增强；以及股东针对高管薪酬方案进行的咨询性投票（“薪酬话语权投票”）。

Our results inform the regulatory debate on pay transparency (e.g., Mas, 2016; Babenko, Bennett and Wang, 2025; Baker et al., 2019; Bennedsen et al., 2022). Our evidence suggests that the disclosure of compensation peers may promote a one-size-fits-all approach to the selection of these peers, resulting in a decline of CEO pay dispersion. Further, our results speak to the ongoing debate on the influence of proxy advisors and passive investors on the evolution of executive compensation practices and, more broadly, on their role in the economy (e.g., Posner, 2018; Financial Times, 2019).

> **中文：** 我们的研究结果为有关薪酬透明度的监管争论提供了参考（例如 Mas, 2016；Babenko, Bennett and Wang, 2025；Baker et al., 2019；Bennedsen et al., 2022）。我们的证据表明，薪酬同业公司的披露可能会推动采用“一刀切”的同业公司选择方法，从而导致 CEO 薪酬离散度下降。此外，我们的研究结果也回应了当前有关代理投票顾问和被动投资者如何影响高管薪酬实践演变的争论，以及更广泛意义上有关它们在经济中所发挥作用的争论（例如 Posner, 2018；Financial Times, 2019）。

We hope that our analysis helps promote an academic debate on the causes and consequences of the documented decline in pay dispersion, a phenomenon about which – to the best of our knowledge – there is currently little awareness. Our evidence suggests that the increase in industry-size benchmarking is one plausible driver of such decline, yet there could be others. Less variation in executive pay could have a wide range of consequences. Most evidently, to the extent that it is driven by a one-size-fits-all rule, the decline in pay dispersion might reflect a deviation from optimal pay levels, which potentially affects hiring and/or retention. Other consequences could be less obvious. For example, the need to conform to the benchmarked pay level could induce changes in the characteristics of the compensation contract, thereby affecting incentives. Moreover, when pay levels are relatively similar, external tournament incentives are low. Based on prior literature (e.g., Coles, Li and Wang, 2018) a decrease in such incentives could affect corporate risk-taking, firm performance, and

> **中文：** 我们希望，本研究能够推动学术界讨论本文所记录的薪酬离散度下降现象的成因与后果。据我们所知，目前人们对这一现象的认识仍然有限。我们的证据表明，行业-规模基准比较的增加是导致这种下降的一个合理因素，但也可能存在其他因素。高管薪酬差异缩小可能产生广泛的后果。最明显的是，如果薪酬离散度下降是由“一刀切”规则所驱动，那么这种下降可能反映薪酬水平偏离最优水平，进而可能影响人员聘用和／或留任。其他后果可能并不那么明显。例如，遵循基准薪酬水平的要求可能会引起薪酬契约特征的变化，从而影响激励。此外，当薪酬水平较为相似时，外部锦标赛激励较弱。根据既有文献（例如 Coles, Li and Wang, 2018），此类激励的减弱可能影响公司的风险承担、公司业绩以及

31

<!-- page:34 -->

## Source Page 34

product market competition. Consequently, stock return synchronicity may increase within industry groups (Roll, 1988; Chen, Goldstein and Jiang, 2007; Wurgler, 2000).

> **中文：** 产品市场竞争。因此，行业组内部的股票收益同步性可能会上升（Roll, 1988；Chen, Goldstein and Jiang, 2007；Wurgler, 2000）。

## Source Page 39

Appendix A: Variable appendix

> **中文：** 附录 A：变量附录

Variable | Definition | Source

> **中文：** 变量 | 定义 | 数据来源

I. Pay variables

> **中文：** I. 薪酬变量

Pay dispersion (economy-, industry- or industry-size level)

> **中文：** 薪酬离散度（经济总体、行业或行业-规模层面）

Standard deviation of Pay where Pay is defined as CEO pay (TDC1 in Execucomp) scaled by its median value in that year and winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles. When computed at the economy-level, pay dispersion is computed across all sample firms in a given year. When computed at the industry-level, pay dispersion is computed across firms within the same GICS6-industry in a given year. When computed at the industry-size level, pay dispersion is computed across firms that are in the same GICS6 × Size quintile group, where size quintiles are based on firms’ lagged market values.

> **中文：** Pay 的标准差，其中 Pay 定义为 CEO 薪酬（Execucomp 中的 TDC1）除以该年度的中位数，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。在经济总体层面计算时，薪酬离散度基于给定年度全部样本公司计算。在行业层面计算时，薪酬离散度基于给定年度同一 GICS6 行业内的公司计算。在行业-规模层面计算时，薪酬离散度基于属于同一 GICS6 × Size 五分位数组的公司计算，其中规模五分位数依据公司的滞后市场价值划分。

Execucomp; Compustat

> **中文：** Execucomp；Compustat

Pay dispersion (firm-level)

> **中文：** 薪酬离散度（公司层面）

Standard deviation of Pay for S&P 1500 firms where Pay is defined as the CEO’s pay scaled by its median value in that year and winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles. At the firm-level, pay dispersion is computed across a firm’s compensation peers (compensation peers are the firms disclosed by a focal firm in its proxy statement for the purpose of benchmarking pay levels). Data on the identity of compensation peers is obtained from AuditAnalytics, Equilar, and ISS IncentiveLab. We require that each peer group contains at least 5 and at most 76 peers (the 1st and 99th percentiles of peer group sizes, respectively). Pay information is obtained first from Execucomp (TDC1) and supplemented for non-Execucomp firms from ISS’s Executive Compensation Analysis (ECA) database, Equilar, Capital IQ, and GMI. Observations with missing pay data for more than 25 percent of compensation peers are excluded.

> **中文：** S&P 1500 公司的 Pay 标准差，其中 Pay 定义为 CEO 薪酬除以该年度的中位数，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。在公司层面，薪酬离散度基于一家公司的薪酬同业公司计算（薪酬同业公司是核心公司为进行薪酬水平基准比较而在其代理权声明中披露的公司）。薪酬同业公司身份数据来自 AuditAnalytics、Equilar 和 ISS IncentiveLab。我们要求每个同业组至少包含 5 家、至多包含 76 家同业公司，分别对应同业组规模的第 1 和第 99 百分位数。薪酬信息首先取自 Execucomp（TDC1）；对于未被 Execucomp 覆盖的公司，则使用 ISS 的 Executive Compensation Analysis（ECA）数据库、Equilar、Capital IQ 和 GMI 进行补充。如果超过 25% 的薪酬同业公司缺少薪酬数据，则剔除该观测值。

Execucomp; ISS ECA; Equilar; AuditAnalytics; GMI

> **中文：** Execucomp；ISS ECA；Equilar；AuditAnalytics；GMI

Pay dispersion (abnormal)

> **中文：** 薪酬离散度（异常）

Standard deviation of Abnormal pay. Abnormal pay is computed as the residual from the following cross-sectional regression (estimated for each year separately):

CEO pay<sub>i,t</sub> = α<sub>t</sub> + β<sub>t</sub> ∗ firm characteristics<sub>i,t−1</sub> + γ<sub>s,t</sub> + ϵ<sub>i,t</sub>

where CEO pay is the unscaled reported pay, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles. The suffixes i, t, s refer to firm i, year t and industry-size quintile s. The vector of firm characteristics includes firm size, stock return, sales growth, Tobin’s Q, and idiosyncratic return volatility. The residuals from the annual regressions are then scaled by the median CEO pay in the year. The dispersion is computed as the standard deviation of the scaled residuals (depending on the level of aggregation - i.e., either across all firms in the economy, across all firms in an industry-size group, or across all compensation peers of a firm).

> **中文：** Abnormal pay 的标准差。Abnormal pay 按照以下横截面回归的残差计算（每年分别估计）：
>
> CEO pay<sub>i,t</sub> = α<sub>t</sub> + β<sub>t</sub> ∗ firm characteristics<sub>i,t−1</sub> + γ<sub>s,t</sub> + ϵ<sub>i,t</sub>
>
> 其中，CEO pay 是未经缩放的报告薪酬，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。下标 i、t、s 分别表示公司 i、年份 t 和行业-规模五分位数组 s。公司特征向量包括公司规模、股票收益率、销售增长率、Tobin’s Q 和特质收益波动率。随后，将年度回归所得残差除以该年度 CEO 薪酬的中位数。离散度计算为缩放后残差的标准差，具体取决于汇总层面，即基于经济总体中的全部公司、某个行业-规模组中的全部公司，或者一家公司的全部薪酬同业公司计算。

Execucomp; Compustat; CRSP; ISS ECA; Equilar; AuditAnalytics; GMI

> **中文：** Execucomp；Compustat；CRSP；ISS ECA；Equilar；AuditAnalytics；GMI

Pay dispersion (ex-options)

> **中文：** 薪酬离散度（不含期权）

Standard deviation of Pay (ex-options). Pay (ex-options) is computed as TDC1 minus the value of stock options granted (either the Black-Scholes option value or, if missing, as the grant date fair value) scaled by its median value in that year and winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles. Pay dispersion is computed as the standard deviation of scaled values depending on the level of aggregation (i.e., either across all firms in the economy, across all firms in an industry-size group, or across all compensation peers of a firm in a given year).

> **中文：** Pay (ex-options) 的标准差。Pay (ex-options) 等于 TDC1 减去授予的股票期权价值（采用 Black-Scholes 期权价值；如果该数据缺失，则采用授予日公允价值），再除以该年度的中位数，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。薪酬离散度计算为缩放后数值的标准差，具体取决于汇总层面，即基于经济总体中的全部公司、某个行业-规模组中的全部公司，或者给定年度一家公司的全部薪酬同业公司计算。

Execucomp

> **中文：** Execucomp

Realized pay (v1)

> **中文：** 已实现薪酬（v1）

Realized pay as defined by Execucomp in item TOTAL_ALT2. TOTAL_ALT2 is defined as TOTAL_SEC (i.e., total compensation as reported to SEC in that year) except that stock and option awards are valued using their realized values – i.e., the value of options exercised in the year and the value of stocks vested during the year. The measure is winsorized at the 5th and 95th percentiles.

> **中文：** Execucomp 在 TOTAL_ALT2 项目中定义的已实现薪酬。TOTAL_ALT2 的定义与 TOTAL_SEC（即该年度向 SEC 报告的薪酬总额）相同，但股票和期权奖励使用其已实现价值计量，即该年度已行权期权的价值以及该年度已归属股票的价值。该指标在第 5 和第 95 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。

Execucomp

> **中文：** Execucomp

Realized pay (v2)

> **中文：** 已实现薪酬（v2）

Realized pay following a definition developed by Carter and Pawliczek (2023). As described in Carter and Pawliczek (2023), we make the following adjustments to the pay reported to SEC:

Realized pay (v2) = Non-equity pay + End-of-year value of stock and option grants made in the year + Change in the value of outstanding and unvested equity grants from prior years + Change in the value of stock grants vested during the year

where non-equity pay is the total reported pay minus the fair value of stock and option grants reported to the SEC. The measure is winsorized at the 5th and 95th percentiles.

> **中文：** 依据 Carter and Pawliczek (2023) 提出的定义计算已实现薪酬。按照 Carter and Pawliczek (2023) 的说明，我们对向 SEC 报告的薪酬进行以下调整：
>
> Realized pay (v2) = Non-equity pay + End-of-year value of stock and option grants made in the year + Change in the value of outstanding and unvested equity grants from prior years + Change in the value of stock grants vested during the year
>
> 其中，Non-equity pay 等于报告薪酬总额减去向 SEC 报告的股票和期权授予的公允价值。该指标在第 5 和第 95 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。

Execucomp; CRSP

> **中文：** Execucomp；CRSP

Cumul. pay growth

> **中文：** 累计薪酬增长率

Cumulative CEO pay growth between first year in sample and current year.

> **中文：** 从样本首年到当前年度的 CEO 薪酬累计增长率。

Execucomp

> **中文：** Execucomp

37

> **中文：** 37

## Source Page 40

> **中文：** 来源第 40 页

Appendix A: Variable appendix (cont’d)

> **中文：** 附录 A：变量附录（续）

Variable Definition Source

> **中文：** 变量　定义　来源

II. Compensation peer / peer group variables

> **中文：** II. 薪酬同业公司／同业组变量

Dispersion in relative book values  
Standard deviation of the relative book values in a focal firm’s compensation peer group. Relative book value is the ratio of a peer’s total book value of assets to the total book value of assets of the focal firm. The measure is winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 相对账面价值离散度  
> 核心公司薪酬同业组中相对账面价值的标准差。相对账面价值是同业公司的资产账面总值与核心公司的资产账面总值之比。该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

Dispersion in relative market values  
Standard deviation of the relative market values in a focal firm’s compensation peer group. Relative market value is the ratio of peer’s market value of assets (defined as total book value of assets minus book value of equity plus market value of equity at fiscal year end) to the market value of assets of the focal firm. The measure is winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 相对市场价值离散度  
> 核心公司薪酬同业组中相对市场价值的标准差。相对市场价值是同业公司的资产市场价值与核心公司的资产市场价值之比，其中资产市场价值定义为资产账面总值减去权益账面价值，再加上财政年度末的权益市场价值。该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

Deviation from industry-size benchmarking  
Fraction of compensation peers that are from outside the GICS1 industry or that are much larger (>200%) or much smaller (<50%) than the focal firm in book or market value of assets. The measure is winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 偏离行业-规模基准比较  
> 薪酬同业公司中不属于同一 GICS1 行业，或者其资产账面价值或市场价值远大于（>200%）或远小于（<50%）核心公司的公司占比。该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

ISS conformity  
Fraction of firm’s actual compensation peers that are included in a synthetic compensation peer group for the firm based on ISS’s peer selection methodology (see Appendix B for details). The measure is winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
AuditAnalytics; ISS IncentiveLab; Equilar; Compustat, CRSP

> **中文：**  
> ISS 一致度  
> 公司实际薪酬同业公司中，按照 ISS 的同业公司选择方法被纳入该公司合成薪酬同业组的公司占比（详见附录 B）。该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> AuditAnalytics；ISS IncentiveLab；Equilar；Compustat；CRSP

Fraction of reciprocal peers  
Fraction of compensation peers that reference back the focal firm, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
AuditAnalytics; ISS IncentiveLab; Equilar

> **中文：**  
> 互惠同业公司占比  
> 反向将核心公司列为参照对象的薪酬同业公司占比，在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> AuditAnalytics；ISS IncentiveLab；Equilar

Peer group reciprocity  
The fraction of the existing network linkages that are bilateral (i.e., point in both directions). At the firm-level, the network for a given firm is created by first adding the focal firm and all its compensation peers as nodes, and then by adding all the references between the focal firm and all its peers and the references among the peers as defined in their respective compensation peer groups. The measure is winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
AuditAnalytics; ISS IncentiveLab; Equilar

> **中文：**  
> 同业组互惠性  
> 现有网络连接中双向连接（即指向两个方向）所占的比例。在公司层面，首先将核心公司及其所有薪酬同业公司添加为节点，然后根据各自薪酬同业组的定义，添加核心公司与其所有同业公司之间的全部参照关系以及同业公司之间的参照关系，由此构建给定公司的网络。该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> AuditAnalytics；ISS IncentiveLab；Equilar

Peer group transitivity  
The number of triangles divided by the number of triads that exist in a network. Triads are groups of three nodes that are connected in some way; triangles are triads that are completely connected. A higher number indicates a greater connectivity among the members of the network. The measure is winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
AuditAnalytics; ISS IncentiveLab; Equilar

> **中文：**  
> 同业组传递性  
> 网络中的三角形数量除以现有三元组数量。三元组是以某种方式相互连接的三个节点组成的集合；三角形则是完全连接的三元组。数值越高，表示网络成员之间的连接程度越高。该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> AuditAnalytics；ISS IncentiveLab；Equilar

Peer group cluster coefficient  
The number of triangles divided by the number of possible triads. A higher number indicates a more complete graph. The measure is winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
AuditAnalytics; ISS IncentiveLab; Equilar

> **中文：**  
> 同业组聚类系数  
> 三角形数量除以可能形成的三元组数量。数值越高，表示网络图越完整。该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> AuditAnalytics；ISS IncentiveLab；Equilar

Low initial conformity  
An indicator variable that is one for firms with below-median conformity with the industry-size peer benchmark in 2007, else 0. Conformity with the industry-size benchmark is measured as the fraction of compensation peers that are from the same GICS2 industry and that are within 50-200% of a firm’s relative market value of assets.  
Compustat; CRSP; AuditAnalytics; ISS IncentiveLab; Equilar

> **中文：**  
> 初始一致度较低  
> 指示变量：若公司在 2007 年与行业-规模同业基准的一致度低于中位数，则取值为 1，否则为 0。与行业-规模基准的一致度，以薪酬同业公司中属于同一 GICS2 行业且资产市场价值处于该公司资产市场价值 50%—200% 范围内的公司占比衡量。  
> Compustat；CRSP；AuditAnalytics；ISS IncentiveLab；Equilar

ISS rank  
Rank that ISS assigns to all potential same-GICS2 industry peers based on its peer selection methodology (see Appendix B for details).  
Compustat; CRSP

> **中文：**  
> ISS 排名  
> ISS 根据其同业公司选择方法对属于同一 GICS2 行业的所有潜在同业公司赋予的排名（详见附录 B）。  
> Compustat；CRSP

Included in peer group  
Indicator variable that is one if a firm is part of the actual compensation peer group of a given firm.  
Compustat; AuditAnalytics; ISS IncentiveLab; Equilar

> **中文：**  
> 纳入同业组  
> 指示变量：若某公司是给定公司实际薪酬同业组的成员，则取值为 1。  
> Compustat；AuditAnalytics；ISS IncentiveLab；Equilar

Relative market value  
Market value of assets of peer scaled by focal firm’s market value of assets, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 相对市场价值  
> 同业公司的资产市场价值除以核心公司的资产市场价值，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

Relative Tobin’s Q  
Tobin’s Q of peer scaled by focal firm’s Tobin’s Q, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 相对 Tobin’s Q  
> 同业公司的 Tobin’s Q 除以核心公司的 Tobin’s Q，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

Relative sales  
Total sales of peer scaled by focal firm’s total sales, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 相对销售额  
> 同业公司的总销售额除以核心公司的总销售额，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

38

> **中文：** 38

## Source Page 41

> **中文：** 来源第 41 页

Appendix A: Variable appendix (cont’d)

> **中文：** 附录 A：变量附录（续）

Variable Definition Source

> **中文：** 变量　定义　来源

Different industry  
Indicator variable that is one if potential peer is from a different GICS4 industry.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 不同行业  
> 指示变量：若潜在同业公司属于不同的 GICS4 行业，则取值为 1。  
> Compustat

At threshold  
Indicator variable that is equal to one for the potential peer that has the highest ISS rank and that is still included in ISS’s recommended peer group for a given focal firm in a given year, else 0. (E.g., when ISS’s recommended peer group has 24 peers, then it is coded 1 for the potential peer that is ranked 24th in ISS’s methodology, else 0.)  
Compustat, CRSP

> **中文：**  
> 位于阈值处  
> 指示变量：对于给定核心公司和给定年度，在仍被纳入 ISS 推荐同业组的潜在同业公司中，若其 ISS 排名最低，则取值为 1，否则为 0。（例如，当 ISS 推荐同业组包含 24 家同业公司时，按照 ISS 方法排名第 24 位的潜在同业公司取值为 1，否则为 0。）  
> Compustat；CRSP

Above threshold  
Indicator variable that is equal to one for the potential peer whose ISS rank is just above the peer group size of ISS’s recommended peer group for a given focal firm in a given year, else 0. (E.g., when ISS’s recommended peer group has 24 peers, then it is coded 1 for the potential peer that is ranked 25th in ISS’s methodology, else 0).  
Compustat, CRSP

> **中文：**  
> 位于阈值之上  
> 指示变量：对于给定核心公司和给定年度，若潜在同业公司的 ISS 排名刚好超出 ISS 推荐同业组的规模，则取值为 1，否则为 0。（例如，当 ISS 推荐同业组包含 24 家同业公司时，按照 ISS 方法排名第 25 位的潜在同业公司取值为 1，否则为 0。）  
> Compustat；CRSP

Dropped peer (t+1)  
Indicator variable that is one if a firm is a compensation peer for a given focal firm in year t but is no longer a compensation peer for the focal firm in year t+1.  
AuditAnalytics; ISS IncentiveLab; Equilar

> **中文：**  
> 被剔除的同业公司（t+1）  
> 指示变量：若某公司在 t 年是给定核心公司的薪酬同业公司，但在 t+1 年不再是该核心公司的薪酬同业公司，则取值为 1。  
> AuditAnalytics；ISS IncentiveLab；Equilar

Added peer (t+1)  
Indicator variable that is one if a firm is not a compensation peer for a given focal firm in year t but is added as a compensation peer for the focal firm in year t+1.  
AuditAnalytics; ISS IncentiveLab; Equilar

> **中文：**  
> 新增的同业公司（t+1）  
> 指示变量：若某公司在 t 年不是给定核心公司的薪酬同业公司，但在 t+1 年被新增为该核心公司的薪酬同业公司，则取值为 1。  
> AuditAnalytics；ISS IncentiveLab；Equilar

Dropped (added) by ISS at t  
Indicator variable that is one for a potential peer that was dropped from (added to) ISS’s recommended peer group for a given focal firm in year t.  
Compustat; CRSP

> **中文：**  
> 在 t 年被 ISS 剔除（新增）  
> 指示变量：若某潜在同业公司在 t 年被 ISS 从给定核心公司的推荐同业组中剔除（新增至该组），则取值为 1。  
> Compustat；CRSP

Just dropped below ISS cutoff  
An indicator variable that is equal to one if a firm’s potential peer was just included in its ISS recommended peer group (i.e. relative rank between -4 and 0) in year t − 1 but was just excluded from its ISS recommended peer group in year t (i.e., relative rank between 1 and 5).  
Compustat; CRSP

> **中文：**  
> 刚降至 ISS 截止点以下  
> 指示变量：若一家公司的潜在同业公司在 t − 1 年刚好被纳入其 ISS 推荐同业组（即相对排名介于 -4 和 0 之间），但在 t 年刚好被排除在其 ISS 推荐同业组之外（即相对排名介于 1 和 5 之间），则取值为 1。  
> Compustat；CRSP

Just rose above ISS cutoff  
An indicator variable that is equal to one if a firm’s potential peer was just excluded in its ISS recommended peer group (i.e. relative rank between 1 and 5) in year t − 1 but was just included from its ISS recommended peer group in year t (i.e., relative rank between -4 and 0).  
Compustat; CRSP

> **中文：**  
> 刚升至 ISS 截止点以上  
> 指示变量：若一家公司的潜在同业公司在 t − 1 年刚好被排除在其 ISS 推荐同业组之外（即相对排名介于 1 和 5 之间），但在 t 年刚好被纳入其 ISS 推荐同业组（即相对排名介于 -4 和 0 之间），则取值为 1。  
> Compustat；CRSP

In ISS peer group  
Indicator variable that is one if a potential peer was in ISS’s recommended peer group for a focal firm in a given year.  
Compustat; CRSP

> **中文：**  
> 位于 ISS 同业组中  
> 指示变量：若某潜在同业公司在给定年度属于核心公司的 ISS 推荐同业组，则取值为 1。  
> Compustat；CRSP

Peer delisted  
Indicator variable that is equal to one if a potential peer was delisted from the stock exchange in year t as a result of merger, bankruptcy or liquidation.  
Compustat; CRSP

> **中文：**  
> 同业公司退市  
> 指示变量：若某潜在同业公司因合并、破产或清算而在 t 年从证券交易所退市，则取值为 1。  
> Compustat；CRSP

Change in relative market value  
Change in the relative market value of assets for a given peer between year t−1 to year t. Relative market value of assets is defined as the market value of assets of the peer scaled by the market value of assets of the focal firm. The measure is winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 相对市场价值的变化  
> 给定同业公司的相对资产市场价值从 t−1 年至 t 年的变化。相对资产市场价值定义为同业公司的资产市场价值除以核心公司的资产市场价值。该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

Change in relative sales  
Change in relative sales is the change in the relative sales of the peer from year t − 1 to year t. Relative sales is defined as total sales of the peer scaled by total sales of the focal firm. The measure is winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 相对销售额的变化  
> 相对销售额的变化是指同业公司的相对销售额从 t − 1 年至 t 年的变化。相对销售额定义为同业公司的总销售额除以核心公司的总销售额。该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

Weak SOP support  
Indicator variable that is one for firms that receive voting support in their say on pay votes in the bottom decile of the SOP vote distribution (which corresponds to 75 percent vote support).  
ISS Voting Analytics

> **中文：**  
> 较低的 SOP 支持率  
> 指示变量：若公司在薪酬话语权投票中获得的投票支持率处于 SOP 投票分布的最低十分位数（对应 75% 的投票支持率），则取值为 1。  
> ISS Voting Analytics

Annual SOP vote frequency  
Indicator variable that is one if a firm has an annual say on pay voting frequency and zero if a firm has a say on pay vote frequency of every three years.  
ISS Voting Analytics

> **中文：**  
> 年度 SOP 投票频率  
> 指示变量：若公司每年举行一次薪酬话语权投票，则取值为 1；若公司每三年举行一次薪酬话语权投票，则取值为 0。  
> ISS Voting Analytics

Fraction shares owned by institutional investors  
The fraction of a firm’s shares that are owned by institutional investors. The measure is winsorized at the 5th and 95th percentiles.  
Refinitiv 13F holdings

> **中文：**  
> 机构投资者持股比例  
> 机构投资者持有的公司股份占比。该指标在第 5 和第 95 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Refinitiv 13F holdings

Fraction shares owned by quasi indexers  
The fraction of a firm’s shares that are owned by mutual funds that are classified as quasi-indexers per Bushee and Noe (2000); Bushee (2001). The measure is winsorized at the 5th and 95th percentiles.  
Refinitiv 13F holdings; Brian Bushee’s investor classification

> **中文：**  
> 准指数投资者持股比例  
> 按照 Bushee and Noe (2000) 和 Bushee (2001) 的分类，被归类为准指数投资者的共同基金所持有的公司股份占比。该指标在第 5 和第 95 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Refinitiv 13F holdings；Brian Bushee’s investor classification

39

> **中文：** 39

## Source Page 42

> **中文：** 来源第 42 页

Appendix A: Variable appendix (cont’d)

> **中文：** 附录 A：变量附录（续）

Variable Definition Source

> **中文：** 变量　定义　来源

Fraction shares owned by index mutual funds  
Defined as in Appel, Gormley and Keim (2016), p.116: The fraction of a firm’s shares that are owned by mutual funds that are flagged as passively managed. A mutual fund is flagged as passively managed if its fund name includes a string that identifies it as an index fund. The strings used to identify index funds are: Index, Idx, Indx, Ind (where indicates a space), Russell, S & P, S and P, S&P, SandP, SP, DOW, Dow, DJ, MSCI, Bloomberg, KBW, NASDAQ, NYSE, STOXX, FTSE, Wilshire, Morningstar, 100, 400, 500, 600, 900, 1000, 1500, 2000, and 5000. The measure is winsorized at the 5th and 95th percentiles.  
Refinitiv 13F holdings; CRSP mutual fund

> **中文：**  
> 指数共同基金持股比例  
> 按 Appel, Gormley and Keim (2016), p.116 的定义：被标记为被动管理型共同基金持有的公司股份占比。如果共同基金的基金名称包含能够识别其为指数基金的字符串，则将该基金标记为被动管理型。用于识别指数基金的字符串包括：Index、Idx、Indx、Ind（其中表示一个空格）、Russell、S & P、S and P、S&P、SandP、SP、DOW、Dow、DJ、MSCI、Bloomberg、KBW、NASDAQ、NYSE、STOXX、FTSE、Wilshire、Morningstar、100、400、500、600、900、1000、1500、2000 和 5000。该指标在第 5 和第 95 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Refinitiv 13F holdings；CRSP mutual fund

Propensity to vote with ISS  
The fraction of times that a firm’s mutual fund investors voted alongside ISS in prior years when ISS and the firm management disagreed on the vote recommendation, averaged across all shareholdings, with each fund weighted by the fraction of shares it owns in the firm. (Data availability starts in 2003 and ends in 2017.) The measure is winsorized at the 5th and 95th percentiles.  
Refinitiv 13F holdings; ISS voting analytics; ISS mutual fund voting

> **中文：**  
> 与 ISS 一致投票的倾向  
> 在以往年度 ISS 与公司管理层的投票建议不一致时，公司共同基金投资者与 ISS 一致投票的次数占比。该比例在全部持股中取加权平均，每只基金的权重为其持有的公司股份比例。（数据可得期间始于 2003 年，止于 2017 年。）该指标在第 5 和第 95 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Refinitiv 13F holdings；ISS voting analytics；ISS mutual fund voting

IV. Other firm characteristics

> **中文：** IV. 其他公司特征

Log total assets  
Natural logarithm of total book value of assets (rescaled to 2023 real USD).  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 总资产对数  
> 资产账面总值的自然对数（按 2023 年实际美元重新调整）。  
> Compustat

Tobin’s Q  
Total book value of assets minus book value of equity plus the market value of equity at the end of the fiscal year scaled by the total book value of assets, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> Tobin’s Q  
> 资产账面总值减去权益账面价值，再加上财政年度末的权益市场价值，所得结果除以资产账面总值；该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

Sales growth  
Change in total sales from year t−1 to year t divided by total sales in fiscal year t−1, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
Compustat

> **中文：**  
> 销售增长率  
> 从 t−1 年至 t 年的总销售额变化除以 t−1 财政年度的总销售额，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> Compustat

Stock return  
Daily stock returns compounded over a firm’s fiscal year, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
CRSP

> **中文：**  
> 股票收益率  
> 在公司财政年度内按复利计算的日股票收益率，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> CRSP

Idiosyncratic volatility  
Annualized standard deviation of the residuals of a firm’s returns from the Fama-French 4-factor model estimated using its daily returns over its fiscal year, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.  
CRSP

> **中文：**  
> 特质波动率  
> 使用公司财政年度内的日收益率估计 Fama-French 四因子模型，并计算公司收益率残差的年化标准差；该指标在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。  
> CRSP

40

> **中文：** 40

## Source Page 43

> **中文：** 来源第 43 页

Appendix B: ISS’s methodology for the selection of compensation peers

> **中文：** 附录 B：ISS 选择薪酬同业公司的方法

On December 20, 2011, ISS published a whitepaper that included a new approach to establish peer groups that are used for compensation analysis and pay-for-performance screens (Gibson, 2011). The whitepaper was republished with minor revisions on February 17, 2012 (ISS, 2012a).

> **中文：** 2011 年 12 月 20 日，ISS 发布了一份白皮书，其中提出了一种建立用于薪酬分析和薪酬绩效筛选的同业组的新方法（Gibson, 2011）。该白皮书经过小幅修订后，于 2012 年 2 月 17 日再次发布（ISS, 2012a）。

In that whitepaper, ISS disclosed its new methodology for the selection of a comparison peer group that consists of the following steps:

> **中文：** 在该白皮书中，ISS 披露了其选择比较同业组的新方法，该方法包括以下步骤：

1. Create an initial list of potential peers from the two-digit GICS universe as the subject company that satisfies the following two criteria:

> **中文：** 1. 从与被评估公司相同的两位数 GICS 行业范围内创建潜在同业公司的初始名单，并要求其满足以下两个标准：

(cid:136) potential peers are between 0.45 and 2.1 times the subject company’s annual sales (assets for financial firms).

> **中文：** (cid:136) 潜在同业公司的年度销售额应介于被评估公司年度销售额的 0.45 倍至 2.1 倍之间（金融公司采用资产衡量）。

(cid:136) potential peers have a market capitalization of between 0.2 times and 5 times the subject company’s market capitalization.

> **中文：** (cid:136) 潜在同业公司的市值应介于被评估公司市值的 0.2 倍至 5 倍之间。

2. Narrow down the initial list of potential peers to those companies that are in the subject company’s six-digit GICS category and rank them from 1 to N using the absolute relative distance in sales so that the subject company stays near the median of the selected group.

> **中文：** 2. 将潜在同业公司的初始名单缩小至与被评估公司属于同一六位数 GICS 类别的公司，并依据销售额的绝对相对距离将其从 1 排至 N，以使被评估公司保持在所选同业组中位数附近。

3. Take the top 24 potential peers for the subject firm’s peer group. If this peer group has fewer than 14 peers, then supplement peers by repeating step (ii) for firms in the subject firm’s four-digit GICS. If thereafter there are still fewer than 14 peers, repeat step (ii) for firms in the subject firm’s two-digit GICS.

> **中文：** 3. 选取排名前 24 位的潜在同业公司组成被评估公司的同业组。如果该同业组少于 14 家同业公司，则针对与被评估公司属于同一四位数 GICS 类别的公司重复步骤 (ii)，以补充同业公司。此后若同业公司仍少于 14 家，则针对与被评估公司属于同一两位数 GICS 类别的公司重复步骤 (ii)。

In some rare cases, firms do not end up with 14 peers. An example of this are companies that much larger than others in its industry (referred to as “super-mega non-financial companies” by ISS); in such cases, realizing the importance of firm size on CEO pay, ISS relaxes the industry criterion so to pair these firms with peers that are similar-sized.

> **中文：** 在少数情况下，公司最终无法获得 14 家同业公司。例如，有些公司远大于其所在行业的其他公司（ISS 将其称为“超巨型非金融公司”）；在这种情况下，鉴于公司规模对 CEO 薪酬的重要性，ISS 会放宽行业标准，以便将这些公司与规模相近的同业公司进行配对。

Over the years, ISS has made some modifications to its selection methodology. Some of the changes added complexity while not truly affecting the industry and size match outcomes. For example, one such change was to tighten the initial industry selection filter from GICS6 to GICS8 (if insufficient peers are identified, this was again relaxed to GICS6, GICS4 and GICS2 as described in step (iii) above). Another change allowed firms from the GICS8 industry of the subject firm’s own chosen compensation peers as potential peers with some priority given to what ISS calls “first-degree peers” (those that referenced back the subject firm) and those with numerous connections (i.e. those often chosen as a peer).

> **中文：** 多年来，ISS 对其选择方法进行了一些调整。部分调整增加了方法的复杂性，但并未实质性影响行业和规模匹配结果。例如，其中一项调整是将初始行业筛选条件从 GICS6 收紧至 GICS8（如果识别出的同业公司数量不足，则按照上述步骤 (iii) 的说明，依次放宽至 GICS6、GICS4 和 GICS2）。另一项调整允许将被评估公司自行选择的薪酬同业公司所属 GICS8 行业中的公司纳入潜在同业公司，并对 ISS 所称的“一级同业公司”（即反向将被评估公司列为参照对象的公司）以及拥有大量连接的公司（即经常被选为同业公司的公司）给予一定优先权。

Despite such changes, repeated disclosures by ISS describing analyses of their peer group method show that there are little effective changes to the tightness of the industry-size restrictions. For example, in 2012, ISS reports that for the 2013 proxy season, 90 percent of peer groups maintain the subject company within 20 percent of the peer group median size and no peer groups had 2-digit GICS peers (ISS, 2012b, 15). In 2019, ISS reports a 2017 analysis that there were still no 2-digit GICS peers and 85 percent of peer groups maintain the subject firm within 20 percent of the peer group median size (ISS, 2019a, 3). In 2023, it reports the same statistics as in 2019 (ISS, 2023, 4-5).

> **中文：** 尽管存在上述调整，ISS 多次披露的同业组方法分析结果表明，行业-规模限制的严格程度实际上几乎没有变化。例如，ISS 在 2012 年报告称，在 2013 年委托书季，90% 的同业组使被评估公司的规模保持在同业组规模中位数上下 20% 的范围内，并且没有任何同业组包含两位数 GICS 同业公司（ISS, 2012b, 15）。2019 年，ISS 报告了一项 2017 年的分析，结果显示仍然没有两位数 GICS 同业公司，并且 85% 的同业组使被评估公司的规模保持在同业组规模中位数上下 20% 的范围内（ISS, 2019a, 3）。2023 年，ISS 报告了与 2019 年相同的统计数据（ISS, 2023, 4-5）。

41

> **中文：** 41

Figure 1: Pay dispersion

> **中文：** 图 1：薪酬离散度

The figures show the trajectory of CEO pay dispersion at three levels of aggregation—for the overall economy between 1996 and 2023 (Figure 1A), for the average industry-size group between 1996 and 2023 (Figure 1B), and within the average compensation peer group between 2007 and 2023 (Figure 1C).

> **中文：** 各图展示了三个聚合层面上 CEO 薪酬离散度的变化轨迹：1996—2023 年的整体经济层面（图 1A）、1996—2023 年的平均行业-规模组层面（图 1B），以及 2007—2023 年的平均薪酬同业组内部（图 1C）。

Pay dispersion is measured as the standard deviation of Pay (defined as TDC1 in Execucomp scaled by its median value in the year).

> **中文：** 薪酬离散度以 Pay 的标准差衡量，其中 Pay 定义为 Execucomp 中的 TDC1 除以其当年中位数。

Pay dispersion (ex-options) is the standard deviation of CEO pay (defined as TDC1 minus the value of stock options granted) scaled by its median value in that year.

> **中文：** 薪酬离散度（不含期权）是 CEO 薪酬（定义为 TDC1 减去所授予股票期权的价值）除以其当年中位数后的标准差。

Pay dispersion (abnormal) is computed as the standard deviation of pay residuals that are scaled by the median CEO pay in the year; the pay residuals are obtained from annual cross-sectional regressions of unscaled CEO pay on the economic determinants of pay (see variable appendix for details).

> **中文：** 薪酬离散度（异常）计算为薪酬残差除以当年 CEO 薪酬中位数后的标准差；薪酬残差来自以未缩放的 CEO 薪酬为因变量、薪酬的经济决定因素为自变量进行的年度横截面回归（详见变量附录）。

In Figure 1B, industry is defined by GICS6 industry affiliation and size is based on quintiles of the market value of assets.

> **中文：** 在图 1B 中，行业根据 GICS6 行业归属界定，规模则依据资产市场价值的五分位数组确定。

## Source Page 46

Figure 3: Pay dispersion in different settings

> **中文：** 图 3：不同情境下的薪酬离散度

This figure plots CEO pay dispersion in different settings. Pay dispersion is measured as the standard deviation of Pay, which is defined as total CEO pay scaled by the median value of total CEO pay in that year within the corresponding group (i.e., country/region; public/private firms; or non-Top 5 senior employees).

> **中文：** 该图绘制了不同情境下的 CEO 薪酬离散度。薪酬离散度以 Pay 的标准差衡量；Pay 定义为 CEO 总薪酬除以对应组别（即国家/地区、上市/非上市公司或非前五名高级员工）当年的 CEO 总薪酬中位数。

Panel A shows CEO pay dispersion in several countries/regions. Data for U.S. firms is from Execucomp. U.K., European, Australian and Canadian firms are from BoardEx. “Rest-of-world” firms are from NRG Metrics (available for 2011–2019).

> **中文：** 面板 A 展示了若干国家或地区的 CEO 薪酬离散度。美国公司的数据来自 Execucomp；英国、欧洲、澳大利亚和加拿大公司的数据来自 BoardEx；“世界其他地区”公司的数据来自 NRG Metrics（数据可得期为 2011—2019 年）。

Panel B contrasts the pay dispersion among CEOs in public U.S. firms with the pay dispersion among CEOs in private U.S. firms and the pay dispersion among non-Top 5 senior employees.

> **中文：** 面板 B 对比了美国上市公司 CEO、美国非上市公司 CEO 以及非前五名高级员工之间的薪酬离散度。

Data for senior employee and private-firm CEO pay comes from Capital IQ People Intelligence.

> **中文：** 高级员工和非上市公司 CEO 薪酬数据来自 Capital IQ People Intelligence。

For each Capital IQ firm, we keep the CEO of private firms and their total executive compensation, as well as the employees with non-zero total senior employee compensation in public and private U.S. firms.

> **中文：** 对于 Capital IQ 中的每家公司，我们保留非上市公司的 CEO 及其高管总薪酬，同时保留美国上市和非上市公司中高级员工总薪酬非零的员工。

We remove employees whose title indicated that they are part of the board, that they belong to the C-suite (i.e., have a “Chief” title), or which have a “President” title (as the use of president and CEO overlaps in some organizations).

> **中文：** 我们剔除职位名称表明其属于董事会、属于最高管理层（即职位名称中含有“Chief”），或者职位名称中含有“President”的员工，因为在部分组织中，President 与 CEO 的称谓存在重叠。

The remaining most common titles in the senior employees sample (representing over 95 percent) are then, in order of frequency: senior key executive; other key executive; secretary; head of corporate development; head of sales; head of human resources; top key executives; head of marketing; other professional and operations professional; treasurer; controller.

> **中文：** 高级员工样本中剩余的最常见职位名称（合计占比超过 95%）按出现频率依次为：高级关键高管、其他关键高管、秘书、企业发展负责人、销售负责人、人力资源负责人、最高层关键高管、营销负责人、其他专业人员及运营专业人员、财务主管和财务总监。

The senior employees sample covers 37,000 distinct employees; data coverage for U.S. private-firm CEOs starts in 2006 and covers 2,954 distinct CEOs across 2,464 private U.S. firms.

> **中文：** 高级员工样本涵盖 37,000 名不同员工；美国非上市公司 CEO 的数据覆盖期始于 2006 年，涵盖 2,464 家美国非上市公司的 2,954 名不同 CEO。

## Source Page 47

Figure 4: Simulation

> **中文：** 图 4：模拟

This figure shows the simulated and observed CEO pay dispersion in the economy.

> **中文：** 该图展示了整体经济中模拟得到和实际观察到的 CEO 薪酬离散度。

Observed pay dispersion is defined as in Figure 1A.

> **中文：** 实际观察到的薪酬离散度定义与图 1A 相同。

Simulated pay dispersion is the economy-wide pay distribution when CEO pay is simulated under the assumption that all firms select compensation peers based on ISS’s compensation peer selection methodology (see Appendix B for details).

> **中文：** 模拟薪酬离散度是指在假设所有公司均依据 ISS 的薪酬同业公司选择方法选择薪酬同业公司的情况下，通过模拟 CEO 薪酬所得到的整体经济薪酬分布（详见附录 B）。

We target pay at a randomized target percentile of their peers’ pay.

> **中文：** 我们将薪酬设定在同业公司薪酬分布中随机确定的目标百分位数上。

That is, each year, each firm selects its compensation peers by following the industry- and size-based methodology developed by ISS and then sets its CEO pay level to a target percentile of this peer group pay distribution.

> **中文：** 也就是说，每年每家公司均按照 ISS 制定的基于行业和规模的方法选择薪酬同业公司，随后将其 CEO 薪酬水平设定为该同业组薪酬分布中的某一目标百分位数。

Size and industry data for each year is obtained from Compustat.

> **中文：** 各年度的规模和行业数据来自 Compustat。

Target percentiles are randomly drawn from a normal distribution with mean 0.6 and standard deviation 0.1.

> **中文：** 目标百分位数从均值为 0.6、标准差为 0.1 的正态分布中随机抽取。

Observed pay dispersion  
Simulated pay dispersion

> **中文：** 实际观察到的薪酬离散度  
> 模拟薪酬离散度

2007 2009 2011 2013 2015 2017 2019 2021 2023

> **中文：** 2007 2009 2011 2013 2015 2017 2019 2021 2023

## Source Page 48

Figure 5: Compensation peer choices

> **中文：** 图 5：薪酬同业公司的选择

This figure shows the composition of firms’ compensation peer groups across time.

> **中文：** 该图展示了公司薪酬同业组构成随时间的变化。

In Panel A, Frac. peers different in industry and size is defined as the fraction of compensation peers that are in a different GICS1 industry and outside of 50-200% of relative asset size and market values.

> **中文：** 在面板 A 中，行业和规模均不同的同业公司比例（Frac. peers different in industry and size）定义为以下薪酬同业公司所占的比例：其所属 GICS1 行业不同，并且相对资产规模和市场价值处于 50%—200% 区间之外。

Frac. peers different in size is defined as the fraction of compensation peers that are outside of 50-200% of relative asset size and market values.

> **中文：** 规模不同的同业公司比例（Frac. peers different in size）定义为相对资产规模和市场价值处于 50%—200% 区间之外的薪酬同业公司所占的比例。

Number of peer GICS6 industries is defined as the number of distinct GICS6 industries from which firms’ compensation peers are drawn.

> **中文：** 同业公司所属 GICS6 行业数量（Number of peer GICS6 industries）定义为公司薪酬同业公司来源所涉及的不同 GICS6 行业数量。

SD of peers’ relative book value (market value) is measured as the standard deviation of the ratio of peers’ sizes to that of the subject firm, where size is measured using the book value of assets (total market value of assets).

> **中文：** 同业公司相对账面价值（市场价值）的标准差，按照同业公司规模与被评估公司规模之比的标准差衡量，其中规模分别采用资产账面价值（资产总市场价值）衡量。

In Panel B, Fraction of reciprocal references is the fraction of compensation peers that reference back the subject firm in their respective peer groups.

> **中文：** 在面板 B 中，互惠参照比例（Fraction of reciprocal references）是指在各自同业组中反向将被评估公司列为同业公司的薪酬同业公司所占比例。

Peergroup reciprocity, Peergroup transitivity and Peergroup clustering coefficient further consider the connections among the peers: reciprocity is the fraction of connections in the network that are reciprocal; transitivity (clustering coefficient) is the fraction of triangles divided by the number of existing triad (divided by the number of possible triads) in the peer group network.

> **中文：** 同业组互惠性（Peergroup reciprocity）、同业组传递性（Peergroup transitivity）和同业组聚类系数（Peergroup clustering coefficient）进一步考虑了同业公司之间的连接关系：互惠性是网络中互惠连接所占的比例；传递性（聚类系数）是同业组网络中的三角形数量除以现有三元组数量（除以可能的三元组数量）所得的比例。

5A. Relative size and industry affiliation

> **中文：** 5A. 相对规模与行业归属

SD of peers' relative market values

Figure 6: The influence of ISS on peer selection

> **中文：** 图 6：ISS 对同业公司选择的影响

This figure shows the probability that a potential peer is chosen by a subject firm as its compensation peer as a function of the potential peer’s rank as per ISS’s ranking methodology.

> **中文：** 该图展示了某一潜在同业公司被被评估公司选为薪酬同业公司的概率，该概率是潜在同业公司依据 ISS 排名方法所得排名的函数。

In its methodology, ISS creates for each subject firm a ranking of appropriate compensation peers based on industry affiliation and relative-size criteria, and then chooses the highest-ranked 14-24 peers (see Appendix B for details).

> **中文：** 根据 ISS 的方法，ISS 针对每家被评估公司，依据行业归属和相对规模标准对适当的薪酬同业公司进行排名，随后选择排名最高的 14—24 家同业公司（详见附录 B）。

A lower ISS rank implies a more suitable peer.

> **中文：** ISS 排名越低，意味着该公司越适合作为同业公司。

The x-axis shows a potential peer’s relative rank per ISS methodology; the relative rank is defined as a potential peer’s ISS rank minus the size of the ISS recommended peer group for the subject firm.

> **中文：** 横轴表示潜在同业公司按照 ISS 方法计算的相对排名；相对排名定义为潜在同业公司的 ISS 排名减去 ISS 为被评估公司建议的同业组规模。

For example, for a subject firm with an ISS recommended peer group of 14 (24) peers, relative rank 1 indicates a 15th (25th) ranked potential peer and which is hence just outside of ISS’s peer group per ISS methodology.

> **中文：** 例如，对于 ISS 建议同业组包含 14（24）家同业公司的被评估公司，相对排名 1 表示排名第 15（25）位的潜在同业公司，因此按照 ISS 方法，该公司恰好位于 ISS 同业组之外。

Probability that potential peer is chosen by firm

> **中文：** 潜在同业公司被公司选中的概率

Rank relative to ISS's peer group size

> **中文：** 相对于 ISS 同业组规模的排名

-10 -5 0 5 10 15 20 25 30 35 40 45 50

> **中文：** -10 -5 0 5 10 15 20 25 30 35 40 45 50

Figure 7: The influence of SOP on peer selection

> **中文：** 图 7：SOP 对同业公司选择的影响

This figure shows the univariate dispersion of peers’ relative book values, dispersion of peers’ relative market values, deviation from industry-size benchmarking, and conformity with ISS’s peer selection policy in year [-3,+3] around firms’ first SOP frequency vote event.

> **中文：** 该图展示了公司首次薪酬话语权投票（SOP）频率投票事件前后 [-3,+3] 年期间，同业公司相对账面价值的单变量离散度、同业公司相对市场价值的离散度、相对于行业-规模基准比较的偏离程度，以及与 ISS 同业公司选择政策的一致程度。

The measures, normalized as of year 0 (i.e., the year of the first SOP frequency vote), are shown separately for the firms whose shareholders voted for a 1-year (3-year) SOP vote frequency in close shareholder votes.

> **中文：** 这些指标以第 0 年（即首次 SOP 频率投票发生的年份）为基准进行标准化，并分别展示在票数接近的股东投票中，股东选择每 1 年（每 3 年）举行一次 SOP 投票的公司。

Close votes are defined as those with less than a 5 percentage point difference in support for the 1-year versus 3-year SOP vote frequency in a firm.

> **中文：** 票数接近的投票定义为：在一家公司中，支持每 1 年举行一次 SOP 投票与支持每 3 年举行一次 SOP 投票的比例之差低于 5 个百分点。

The vertical lines around the point estimate show 95% confidence intervals.

> **中文：** 点估计值周围的垂直线表示 95% 置信区间。

## Source Page 52

**Table 2: CEO pay dispersion**

> **中文：** **表 2：CEO 薪酬离散度**

This table shows the trend in CEO pay dispersion within industry-size groups (Panel A) and within compensation peer groups (Panel B). In models 1-3 of Panel A, industry-size groups are based on GICS6-industry affiliation and size quintiles are based on market value of assets; the level of observation is hence industry-size-year. In models 4-6 of Panel A, we match to each firm its 18 closest-sized GICS6-peers in that year (since 18 is the average peer group size in the data) before computing the pay dispersion measures among the matched peers; the level of observation is hence firm-year. In Panel B, we compute pay dispersion measures among the firm’s disclosed compensation peers in a given year; the level of observation is hence firm-year. Annual trend is a linear time trend variable defined as the fiscal year minus the first year of the respective sample period. Pay dispersion is the standard deviation of Pay. Pay dispersion (abnormal) is the standard deviation of Pay (abnormal), computed as explained in Appendix A. Pay dispersion (ex-options) is the standard deviation of Pay (ex-options). Firm controls include lagged Total assets (logged), Tobin’s Q, Sales growth, Stock return, and Idiosyncratic volatility. In Panel A (Panel B) we also control for Cumulative pay growth between 2007 and the year of observation at the economy level (at the firm level). All variable definitions are described in the variable appendix. All models include a constant term. t-statistics in parentheses are based on standard errors clustered at the industry-size level (Panel A, models 1-3) or firm-level (Panel A, models 4-6 and Panel B). *, **, and *** denote significance at the 10%, 5%, and 1% levels, respectively.

> **中文：** 本表展示行业-规模组内（面板 A）以及薪酬同业组内（面板 B）CEO 薪酬离散度的变化趋势。在面板 A 的模型 1—3 中，行业-规模组依据 GICS6 行业归属划分，规模五分位组依据资产市场价值划分；因此，观测层级为行业-规模-年度。在面板 A 的模型 4—6 中，我们首先为每家公司匹配当年规模最为接近的 18 家 GICS6 同业公司（因为数据中的同业组平均规模为 18 家），然后计算匹配同业公司之间的薪酬离散度指标；因此，观测层级为公司-年度。在面板 B 中，我们计算公司在给定年度披露的薪酬同业公司之间的薪酬离散度指标；因此，观测层级为公司-年度。Annual trend 是一个线性时间趋势变量，定义为会计年度减去相应样本期的第一年。Pay dispersion 是 Pay 的标准差。Pay dispersion (abnormal) 是 Pay (abnormal) 的标准差，其计算方法见附录 A。Pay dispersion (ex-options) 是 Pay (ex-options) 的标准差。公司控制变量包括滞后一期的 Total assets（取对数）、Tobin’s Q、Sales growth、Stock return 和 Idiosyncratic volatility。在面板 A（面板 B）中，我们还控制经济总体层面（公司层面）从 2007 年至观测年度的 Cumulative pay growth。所有变量的定义均见变量附录。所有模型均包含常数项。括号内的 t 统计量基于在行业-规模层面（面板 A，模型 1—3）或公司层面（面板 A，模型 4—6 及面板 B）聚类的标准误。*、** 和 *** 分别表示在 10%、5% 和 1% 水平上显著。

## Source Page 53

**Table 3: Peer groups**

> **中文：** **表 3：同业组**

Panel A shows the time trend in the characteristics of firms’ chosen compensation peer groups since the introduction of the SEC pay disclosure rule (2007-2023). Dispersion in relative book values and Dispersion in relative market values are the standard deviations of peers’ relative book value of assets (BVA) and market value of assets (MVA), respectively. Deviation from industry-size benchmarking is the fraction of peers with a different GICS1 code or that are much larger (>200%) or much smaller (<50%) than the focal firm (in terms of BVA or MVA). ISS conformity refers to the fraction of peers included in a synthetic compensation peer group based on ISS’s peer selection methodology (see Appendix B for details). Panel B shows network measures that describe the connections between firms and their compensation peers (including among the peers) as defined via firms’ compensation peer groups. Annual trend is defined as the fiscal year minus 2007. Industry is defined as GICS6 affiliation. Firm controls are identical to those in Table 2B. All variable definitions are described in the variable appendix. All models include a constant term. t-statistics in parentheses are based on standard errors clustered at the firm level. *, **, and *** denote significance at the 10%, 5%, and 1% levels, respectively.

> **中文：** 面板 A 展示自 SEC 薪酬披露规则出台以来（2007—2023 年），公司所选薪酬同业组特征的时间趋势。Dispersion in relative book values 和 Dispersion in relative market values 分别为同业公司相对资产账面价值（BVA）和相对资产市场价值（MVA）的标准差。Deviation from industry-size benchmarking 是符合以下任一条件的同业公司所占比例：其 GICS1 代码与核心公司不同，或者按 BVA 或 MVA 衡量，其规模远大于（>200%）或远小于（<50%）核心公司。ISS conformity 是指根据 ISS 同业公司选择方法构建的合成薪酬同业组所包含的同业公司比例（详见附录 B）。面板 B 展示用于描述公司与其薪酬同业公司之间联系的网络指标，其中也包括同业公司彼此之间的联系；这些指标依据公司的薪酬同业组进行定义。Annual trend 定义为会计年度减去 2007。Industry 依据 GICS6 行业归属定义。公司控制变量与表 2B 中的控制变量相同。所有变量的定义均见变量附录。所有模型均包含常数项。括号内的 t 统计量基于在公司层面聚类的标准误。*、** 和 *** 分别表示在 10%、5% 和 1% 水平上显著。

## Source Page 55

**Table 5: SEC disclosure rule**

> **中文：** **表 5：SEC 披露规则**

This table shows the trend in Pay dispersion within industry-size groups (Panel A) and within compensation peer groups (Panel B) around the introduction of the SEC disclosure rule for compensation peers. Annual trend is a linear time trend variable defined as the fiscal year minus the first year of the respective sample period. Panel B shows results for Pay dispersion and several metrics characterizing compensation peer choices (see Table 3 or the variable appendix for definitions). Low initial conformity is an indicator variable that is one for firms with below-median conformity with the industry-size peer benchmark in 2007, else 0. Conformity with the industry-size benchmark is measured as the fraction of compensation peers that are from the same GICS2 industry and that are within 50-200% of a firm’s relative market value of assets. Firm controls are identical to those in Table 2B. All variable definitions are described in the variable appendix. All models include a constant term. t-statistics in parentheses are based on standard errors that are clustered at the industry-size level in Panel A and at the firm level in Panel B. *, **, and *** denote significance at the 10%, 5%, and 1% levels, respectively.

> **中文：** 本表展示 SEC 薪酬同业公司披露规则出台前后，行业-规模组内（面板 A）和薪酬同业组内（面板 B）Pay dispersion 的变化趋势。Annual trend 是一个线性时间趋势变量，定义为会计年度减去相应样本期的第一年。面板 B 报告 Pay dispersion 以及若干刻画薪酬同业公司选择的指标的结果（定义见表 3 或变量附录）。Low initial conformity 是一个指示变量：若公司 2007 年与行业-规模同业基准的一致性低于中位数，则取值为 1，否则为 0。与行业-规模基准的一致性采用符合以下两个条件的薪酬同业公司比例衡量：与该公司属于同一 GICS2 行业，并且其资产市场价值相对于该公司处于 50%—200% 的范围内。公司控制变量与表 2B 中的控制变量相同。所有变量的定义均见变量附录。所有模型均包含常数项。括号内的 t 统计量基于面板 A 中在行业-规模层面聚类、面板 B 中在公司层面聚类的标准误。*、** 和 *** 分别表示在 10%、5% 和 1% 水平上显著。

## Source Page 56

### Table 6: ISS rankings

> **中文：** 表 6：ISS 排名

This table examines firms’ decisions to include potential peers into their compensation peer groups. In Panel A, Models 1-3 include the top 100 potential peers ranked by ISS methodology (described in Appendix B). Models 4-6 limit the number of potential peers to 18, which is the average number of compensation peers (see Table IA.2). Panel B compares the likelihood of inclusion of potential peers that were ranked just at ISS’s firm-specific peer group size threshold relative to those potential peers that were ranked just above it.

> **中文：** 本表考察公司将潜在同业公司纳入其薪酬同业组的决策。在面板 A 中，模型 1-3 纳入依据 ISS 方法排名前 100 位的潜在同业公司（该方法见附录 B）。模型 4-6 将潜在同业公司的数量限制为 18 家，即薪酬同业公司的平均数量（见表 IA.2）。面板 B 比较排名恰好位于 ISS 针对特定公司设定的同业组规模阈值处和排名恰好高于该阈值的潜在同业公司被纳入的可能性。

At threshold is coded 1 for the peer with the highest rank per ISS methodology and that is still included in the ISS recommended peer group for the firm (i.e. relative rank 0 in Figure 6), else 0. Above threshold is coded 1 for the peer with relative rank +1 (i.e., ranked just outside ISS’s recommended peer group), else 0. The omitted category are potential peers at relative rank -1.

> **中文：** 对于依据 ISS 方法排名最低但仍被纳入 ISS 为该公司推荐的同业组的同业公司（即图 6 中相对排名为 0），At threshold 取值为 1，否则为 0。对于相对排名为 +1 的同业公司（即排名恰好位于 ISS 推荐同业组之外），Above threshold 取值为 1，否则为 0。省略类别为相对排名为 -1 的潜在同业公司。

Panel A uses data after 2012 when ISS published its peer selection methodology. Panel B restricts data to year(s) either prior to 2012 (models 1-5 as placebo tests) or to years after 2012 (models 6-10) when ISS had published its peer selection methodology. A lower ISS rank implies a more suitable peer.

> **中文：** 面板 A 使用 ISS 于 2012 年公布同业公司选择方法之后的数据。面板 B 将数据限制在 2012 年之前的年份（模型 1-5，作为安慰剂检验）或 ISS 公布同业公司选择方法之后的年份（模型 6-10）。ISS 排名越低，表示该公司越适合作为同业公司。

Both panels include controls about the relative size and industry differences between the subject firm and the potential peer: Relative assets, Relative market value, Relative Tobin’s Q, Relative sales as well as an indicator variable (Different industry) that is one if the potential peer is from a different GICS4-industry. All models include a constant term. t-statistics (in parentheses) are based on standard errors clustered at the firm level. *, **, and *** denote significance at the 10%, 5%, and 1% levels, respectively.

> **中文：** 两个面板均控制被评估公司与潜在同业公司之间的相对规模及行业差异，包括 Relative assets、Relative market value、Relative Tobin’s Q、Relative sales，以及指标变量 Different industry；若潜在同业公司来自不同的 GICS4 行业，该指标取值为 1。所有模型均包含常数项。括号内为基于公司层面聚类标准误计算的 t 统计量。*、** 和 *** 分别表示在 10%、5% 和 1% 水平上显著。

| > **中文：** 系数差异的 p 值 | 0.877 | 0.733 | 0.951 | 0.750 | 0.784 | 0.012 | 0.015 | 0.021 | 0.002 | <0.001 |

## Source Page 57

### Table 7: ISS and peer group changes

> **中文：** 表 7：ISS 与同业组变动

This table examines firms’ decisions to drop peers from (add peers to) their compensation peer groups in t+1 in response to changes in ISS recommended peers for the firm in year t.

> **中文：** 本表考察公司针对 ISS 在年份 t 为其推荐的同业公司发生的变化，于 t+1 年从薪酬同业组中剔除同业公司（或向其中新增同业公司）的决策。

The dependent variable Dropped peer in t+1 (Added peer in t+1) in models 1-4 (models 5-8) is an indicator variable equal to one if a peer is dropped by a firm from (is newly added by a firm to) its compensation peer group in year t+1, else 0.

> **中文：** 模型 1-4（模型 5-8）的因变量 Dropped peer in t+1（Added peer in t+1）为指标变量；若公司在 t+1 年将某家同业公司从其薪酬同业组中剔除（新纳入其薪酬同业组），则取值为 1，否则为 0。

Just dropped below ISS cutoff is an indicator variable that is equal to one if a firm’s potential peer was just included in its ISS recommended peer group in year t−1 (i.e., relative rank between -4 and 0) but was just excluded from its ISS recommended peer group in year t (i.e., relative rank between 1 and 5).

> **中文：** Just dropped below ISS cutoff 为指标变量；若公司的某家潜在同业公司在 t−1 年刚好被纳入 ISS 推荐同业组（即相对排名介于 -4 和 0 之间），但在年份 t 刚好被排除在 ISS 推荐同业组之外（即相对排名介于 1 和 5 之间），则取值为 1。

Just rose above ISS cutoff is an indicator variable that is equal to one if a firm’s potential peer was just excluded from its ISS recommended peer group in year t−1 (i.e., relative rank between 1 and 5) but was just included in its ISS recommended peer group in year t (i.e., relative rank between -4 and 0).

> **中文：** Just rose above ISS cutoff 为指标变量；若公司的某家潜在同业公司在 t−1 年刚好被排除在 ISS 推荐同业组之外（即相对排名介于 1 和 5 之间），但在年份 t 刚好被纳入 ISS 推荐同业组（即相对排名介于 -4 和 0 之间），则取值为 1。

Control firms in models 4 and 8 are potential peers with relative ranks between -4 and 20 in years t and t+1 that did not switch into or out of ISS’s recommended peer group.

> **中文：** 模型 4 和模型 8 中的控制公司，是在年份 t 和 t+1 的相对排名均介于 -4 和 20 之间、且未进入或退出 ISS 推荐同业组的潜在同业公司。

Further, Delisted is an indicator variable which is equal to 1 if the peer firm was delisted from the stock exchange in a year as a result of merger, bankruptcy or liquidation. Change in relative market value is the change in the relative market value of assets of the peer from year t−1 to year t. Change in relative sales is the change in the relative sales of the peer from year t−1 to year t.

> **中文：** 此外，Delisted 为指标变量；若同业公司在某一年因合并、破产或清算而从证券交易所退市，则取值为 1。Change in relative market value 是同业公司资产相对市场价值从年份 t−1 到年份 t 的变化。Change in relative sales 是同业公司相对销售额从年份 t−1 到年份 t 的变化。

Firm controls are identical to those in Table 2B. All variable definitions are described in the variable appendix. All models include a constant term. t-statistics in parentheses are based on standard errors clustered at the firm level. *, **, and *** denote significance at the 10%, 5%, and 1% levels, respectively.

> **中文：** 公司控制变量与表 2B 中的控制变量相同。所有变量的定义见变量附录。所有模型均包含常数项。括号内为基于公司层面聚类标准误计算的 t 统计量。*、** 和 *** 分别表示在 10%、5% 和 1% 水平上显著。

### Table 8: Passive investing

> **中文：** 表 8：被动投资

This table shows cross-sectional associations between measures of industry-size benchmarking and measures of passive investing.

> **中文：** 本表展示行业-规模基准比较指标与被动投资指标之间的横截面关联。

Fraction shares owned by institutional investors is the fraction of shares owned by institutional investors in a given firm-year. Fraction shares owned by quasi-indexers is the fraction of shares in a firm-year owned by quasi-indexers, as classified by Bushee and Noe (2000) and Bushee (2001).

> **中文：** Fraction shares owned by institutional investors 是特定公司—年份中由机构投资者持有的股份比例。Fraction shares owned by quasi-indexers 是公司—年份中由准指数投资者持有的股份比例；准指数投资者依据 Bushee and Noe（2000）和 Bushee（2001）的分类确定。

Fraction shares owned by index mutual funds is the fraction of shares owned by mutual funds that follow index investing. Propensity to vote with ISS is, as defined in Appel, Gormley, and Keim (2016), the fraction of shares owned by mutual funds that voted with ISS’s advice in prior years when ISS and the firm’s management gave conflicting voting advice.

> **中文：** Fraction shares owned by index mutual funds 是遵循指数投资策略的共同基金所持股份的比例。Propensity to vote with ISS 按照 Appel、Gormley 和 Keim（2016）的定义，是在以往 ISS 与公司管理层提出相互冲突的投票建议时，由选择遵循 ISS 建议投票的共同基金所持有的股份比例。

The latter measure is only available until 2017 as ISS has stopped selling vote recommendation data to academics. Firm controls are identical to those in Table 2B. Industry-by-year fixed effects are based on GICS4 industries. All variable definitions are described in the variable appendix. All models include a constant term. t-statistics in parentheses are based on standard errors clustered at the firm level. *, **, and *** denote significance at the 10%, 5%, and 1% levels, respectively.

> **中文：** 后一指标仅可获得至 2017 年，因为 ISS 已停止向学术研究者出售投票建议数据。公司控制变量与表 2B 中的控制变量相同。行业—年份固定效应以 GICS4 行业为基础。所有变量的定义见变量附录。所有模型均包含常数项。括号内为基于公司层面聚类标准误计算的 t 统计量。*、** 和 *** 分别表示在 10%、5% 和 1% 水平上显著。

## Source Page 59

### Table 9: Say on pay

> **中文：** 表 9：薪酬话语权投票（Say on Pay）

This table shows the impact of weak say on pay votes on the composition of compensation peer groups.

> **中文：** 本表展示较低的薪酬话语权投票支持率对薪酬同业组构成的影响。

The dependent variables in models 1-4 are Dispersion in relative book values and Dispersion in relative market values, which are the standard deviations of peers’ relative book value of assets (BVA) and market value of assets (MVA), respectively.

> **中文：** 模型 1-4 的因变量为 Dispersion in relative book values 和 Dispersion in relative market values，分别表示同业公司资产相对账面价值（BVA）和资产相对市场价值（MVA）的标准差。

Deviation from industry-size benchmarking in models 5-6 is the fraction of peers with a different GICS1 code or that are much larger (>200%) or much smaller (<50%) than the focal firm in terms of BVA or MVA.

> **中文：** 模型 5-6 中的 Deviation from industry-size benchmarking，是 GICS1 代码不同于核心公司，或者按 BVA 或 MVA 衡量远大于核心公司（>200%）或远小于核心公司（<50%）的同业公司所占比例。

ISS conformity in models 7-8 refers to the fraction of peers included in a synthetic compensation peer group based on ISS’s peer selection methodology (see Appendix B for details).

> **中文：** 模型 7-8 中的 ISS conformity，是依据 ISS 同业公司选择方法构建的合成薪酬同业组中所包含的同业公司比例（详见附录 B）。

Weak SOP support is an indicator for firms that receive voting support in their say on pay votes in the bottom decile of the SOP vote distribution.

> **中文：** Weak SOP support 为指标变量，表示公司在薪酬话语权投票中获得的投票支持率处于 SOP 投票分布的最低十分位。

The analysis uses only the first instance of say on pay votes at firms relating to their pay in fiscal years 2010 or 2011 and keeps a window of [-3, +3] years around the say on pay votes.

> **中文：** 本分析仅使用公司针对 2010 或 2011 财年薪酬进行的首次薪酬话语权投票，并保留薪酬话语权投票前后 [-3, +3] 年的窗口。

Control firms are those that have above-median SOP vote support and are matched by GICS2-industry and stock performance to weak-vote firms. Firm controls are identical to those in Table 2B. All variable definitions are described in the variable appendix. All models include a constant term. t-statistics in parentheses are based on standard errors clustered at the firm level. *, **, and *** denote significance at the 10%, 5%, and 1% levels, respectively.

> **中文：** 控制公司是 SOP 投票支持率高于中位数，并按 GICS2 行业和股票表现与较低投票支持率公司相匹配的公司。公司控制变量与表 2B 中的控制变量相同。所有变量的定义见变量附录。所有模型均包含常数项。括号内为基于公司层面聚类标准误计算的 t 统计量。*、** 和 *** 分别表示在 10%、5% 和 1% 水平上显著。

[版面提取顺序待核对]

| Dependent variable | Dispersion in rel. book values | Dispersion in rel. book values | Dispersion in rel. market values | Dispersion in rel. market values | Deviation from industry-size benchmarking | Deviation from industry-size benchmarking | ISS conformity | ISS conformity |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|
