# Table 10: Close say on pay frequency votes

> **中文：** 表 10：接近临界结果的薪酬话语权投票频率表决

This table compares the changes in peer group composition among Russell 3000 firms whose shareholders voted for an annual say on pay frequency over a 3-year say on pay vote frequency by a narrow margin (±5%). The analysis uses a narrow window [−3, +3] years around the first occurrence of a SOP frequency vote in firms (which happened in calendar years 2011 to 2013). We require firms to have vote frequency data for at least 2 years in the post period.

> **中文：** 本表比较 Russell 3000 公司中，股东以较小票数差距（±5%）支持每年举行一次薪酬话语权投票、而非每三年举行一次薪酬话语权投票的公司，其同业组构成的变化。分析采用公司首次举行薪酬话语权投票频率表决前后 [−3, +3] 年的窄窗口；这些表决发生在 2011 至 2013 日历年度。我们要求公司在表决后的时期至少具有 2 年的数据。

The dependent variables in models 1–4 are Dispersion in relative book values and Dispersion in relative market values, which are the standard deviations of peers’ relative book value of assets (BVA) and market value of assets (MVA), respectively.

> **中文：** 模型 1–4 的因变量分别为相对账面价值离散度和相对市场价值离散度，即同业公司的相对资产账面价值（BVA）和相对资产市场价值（MVA）的标准差。

Deviation from industry-size benchmarking in models 5–6 is the fraction of peers with a different GICS2 code or that are much larger (>200%) or much smaller (<50%) than the focal firm (in terms of BVA or MVA).

> **中文：** 模型 5–6 中的行业-规模基准偏离，是指 GICS2 代码不同于核心公司，或者在 BVA 或 MVA 意义上远大于（>200%）或远小于（<50%）核心公司的同业公司比例。

ISS conformity in models 7–8 refers to the fraction of peers included in a synthetic compensation peer group based on ISS peer selection methodology (see Appendix B for details).

> **中文：** 模型 7–8 中的 ISS 一致性，是指根据 ISS 同业公司选择方法构建的合成薪酬同业组所包含的同业公司比例（详见附录 B）。

Post is an indicator variable equal to 1 in fiscal years that begin after the year of the first SOP frequency vote, and 0 otherwise.

> **中文：** `Post` 是一个指示变量：若某财政年度开始于首次薪酬话语权投票频率表决所在年度之后，则取值为 1；否则取值为 0。

Annual SOP vote frequency is an indicator variable that is equal to 1 if a firm’s shareholders voted for annual SOP votes.

> **中文：** `Annual SOP vote frequency` 是一个指示变量：若公司股东投票支持每年举行薪酬话语权投票，则取值为 1。

Firm controls are identical to those in Table B2. All variable definitions are described in the variable appendix. Industry-by-year fixed effects are based on GICS1 industry codes. t-statistics based on standard errors clustered at the firm level are in parentheses. *, **, and *** denote significance at the 10%, 5%, and 1% levels, respectively.

> **中文：** 公司控制变量与表 B2 中的控制变量相同。所有变量定义均见变量附录。行业×年度固定效应基于 GICS1 行业代码。括号内为基于公司层面聚类标准误计算的 t 统计量。*、** 和 *** 分别表示在 10%、5% 和 1% 水平上显著。

| Dependent variable | Dispersion in rel. book values | Dispersion in rel. book values | Dispersion in rel. market values | Dispersion in rel. market values | Deviation from industry-size benchmarking | Deviation from industry-size benchmarking | ISS conformity | ISS conformity |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|---:|

# Internet Appendix I: Anecdotal evidence of peer group revisions and consequences to reciprocal benchmarking

> **中文：** 网络附录 I：同业组调整及其对互惠基准比较影响的轶事证据

## 1. AUTODESK, INC. (GICS 45: Information Technology industry)

> **中文：** 1. AUTODESK, INC.（GICS 45：信息技术行业）

At its 2012 annual meeting, Autodesk Inc. received 54 percent shareholder support in its advisory vote for its executives’ compensation packages (the “say on pay” vote), which ranked that year in the bottom five percent of say on pay vote support in the Russell 3000. In the same year, Autodesk Inc. had also received an “against” vote recommendation by ISS for its say on pay vote.

> **中文：** 在 2012 年年度股东大会上，Autodesk Inc. 关于高管薪酬方案的咨询性投票，即“薪酬话语权”投票，仅获得 54% 的股东支持，在当年 Russell 3000 公司薪酬话语权投票支持率中位列最低的 5%。同年，ISS 还对 Autodesk Inc. 的薪酬话语权投票提出了“反对”建议。

In its research report, ISS singled out two areas of concerns about compensation: pay for performance alignment and peer group benchmarking policies. On the latter concern, ISS specifically criticized that Autodesk Inc.’s compensation peers did not fit with ISS’s relative-size criteria and compared Autodesk’s CEO pay to the median of its own peer group:

> **中文：** ISS 在研究报告中特别指出了两个薪酬方面的关切领域：薪酬与业绩的一致性，以及同业组基准比较政策。对于后一个问题，ISS 特别批评 Autodesk Inc. 的薪酬同业公司不符合 ISS 的相对规模标准，并将 Autodesk 的 CEO 薪酬与其自行选定的同业组中位数进行了比较：

“The company’s fiscal 2012 pay review and determination group comprises mainly of companies that are larger in terms of revenues. Moreover, several peers are more than two times larger in terms of revenue, and fiscal 2012 CEO pay was 2.18 times ISS’s peer group median. Making pay determinations based on companies that are primarily larger in terms of revenue may escalate pay irrespective of company performance.” (ISS research report on Autodesk, 18 May 2012, p.13)

> **中文：** “该公司 2012 财政年度的薪酬审查与确定组主要由收入规模更大的公司组成。此外，若干同业公司的收入规模超过该公司的两倍，而 2012 财政年度的 CEO 薪酬是 ISS 同业组中位数的 2.18 倍。主要依据收入规模更大的公司确定薪酬，可能会在不考虑公司业绩的情况下推高薪酬。”（ISS 关于 Autodesk 的研究报告，2012 年 5 月 18 日，第 13 页）

In a proxy filing for a Special Meeting in January 2014, Autodesk Inc. summarized the actions it had taken in response to shareholders’ disapproval in prior say on pay votes:

> **中文：** 在为 2014 年 1 月特别股东大会提交的委托书文件中，Autodesk Inc. 总结了其为回应股东在此前薪酬话语权投票中表达的不满而采取的措施：

“Continuing with its focus on instituting best practices for executive compensation, the Committee took a number of actions during fiscal 2012 aimed at evolving and improving Autodesk’s executive compensation programs. These actions included: i) Designing a Performance Stock Unit program; ii) Revising Autodesk’s compensation peer group to more closely align with companies of Autodesk’s financial size and performance; and iii) Mandating stock ownership for all executive officers.” (Autodesk DEF14A, Dec 3, 2013, p.18)

> **中文：** “委员会继续致力于建立高管薪酬最佳实践，并在 2012 财政年度采取了多项旨在发展和改进 Autodesk 高管薪酬计划的措施。这些措施包括：i）设计绩效股票单位计划；ii）调整 Autodesk 的薪酬同业组，使其与财务规模和业绩更接近 Autodesk 的公司保持一致；以及 iii）强制所有高管持有公司股票。”（Autodesk DEF14A，2013 年 12 月 3 日，第 18 页）

Autodesk continues that after another disappointing say on pay vote in fiscal year 2013 with just 64.7 percent support, its management had contacted its largest stockholders, representing over 60% of the outstanding shares, to understand their views and concerns about Autodesk’s executive compensation policies. In response, the compensation committee decided to (among other things):

> **中文：** Autodesk 进一步表示，在 2013 财政年度再次经历令人失望的薪酬话语权投票、支持率仅为 64.7% 后，公司管理层联系了其最大股东。这些股东合计持有超过 60% 的流通股，公司希望借此了解他们对 Autodesk 高管薪酬政策的看法和关切。作为回应，薪酬委员会决定采取的措施包括：

“regularly review and identify compensation peer group companies of appropriate size and pay philosophy” and to “further refine Autodesk’s compensation peer group” so to have “companies in the compensation peer group more closely match Autodesk based on key financial criteria, such as revenue and market capitalization.” (ibid., pp.19-20).

> **中文：** “定期审查和确定在规模与薪酬理念方面适当的薪酬同业组公司”，并“进一步完善 Autodesk 的薪酬同业组”，使“薪酬同业组中的公司依据收入和市场资本总额等关键财务标准与 Autodesk 更加匹配”。（同上，第 19–20 页）

The revised compensation peer group in 2013 reduced the number of non-ISS compliant peers (i.e., peers that were not in ISS’s recommended peer group as per ISS’s methodology) from 9 to 5, in that process also increasing the fraction of reciprocal references by 16 percentage points.

> **中文：** 2013 年调整后的薪酬同业组将不符合 ISS 标准的同业公司数量，即按照 ISS 方法未被纳入 ISS 推荐同业组的公司数量，从 9 家减少至 5 家；在此过程中，互惠参照的比例也提高了 16 个百分点。

The following year, Autodesk Inc. removed an additional four peers and added six new ones to further increase the fit of the compensation peer group with its own size. Thereafter, Autodesk had only two non-ISS compliant peers remaining in its peer group with 12 of its 14 compensation peers representing ‘reciprocal references’ (i.e., the peers also referenced Autodesk in their respective compensation peer groups).

> **中文：** 次年，Autodesk Inc. 又移除了 4 家同业公司，并新增了 6 家同业公司，以进一步提高薪酬同业组与其自身规模的匹配程度。此后，Autodesk 的同业组中仅剩 2 家不符合 ISS 标准的公司，其 14 家薪酬同业公司中有 12 家构成“互惠参照”，即这些同业公司也在各自的薪酬同业组中将 Autodesk 列为参照公司。

After two consecutive “against” say on pay vote recommendations, ISS again issued a “for” vote recommendation for Autodesk’s say on pay vote in 2014 and shareholder support climbed from 64.7 percent in 2013 to 88.3 percent in 2014.

> **中文：** 在连续两年提出“反对”薪酬话语权投票的建议后，ISS 于 2014 年再次对 Autodesk 的薪酬话语权投票提出“赞成”建议，股东支持率也从 2013 年的 64.7% 上升至 2014 年的 88.3%。

Over the whole sample period, Autodesk increased reciprocal benchmarking in its peer group from a low of 18 percent in 2007 to 76 percent in 2018, with an intermediate high of 86 percent in 2015.

> **中文：** 在整个样本期间，Autodesk 同业组中的互惠基准比较比例从 2007 年最低的 18% 上升至 2018 年的 76%，其间曾于 2015 年达到 86% 的高点。

60

<!-- page:63 -->

## Source Page 63

## 2. MINERALS TECHNOLOGIES, INC. (GICS 15: Materials industry)

> **中文：** 2. MINERALS TECHNOLOGIES, INC.（GICS 15：材料行业）

In its 2012 annual meeting, Minerals Technologies Inc. received 56.4 percent shareholder vote support in its say on pay vote, thereby ranking in the Russell 3000 bottom five percent of say on pay vote outcomes in that year. In the same year, the company had also received an “against” vote recommendation by ISS for its say on pay vote.

> **中文：** 在 2012 年年度股东大会上，Minerals Technologies Inc. 的薪酬话语权投票获得了 56.4% 的股东支持，因而位列当年 Russell 3000 公司薪酬话语权投票结果最低的 5%。同年，ISS 也对该公司的薪酬话语权投票提出了“反对”建议。

In its research report, ISS pointed to two areas with a high level of concern: pay for performance evaluation and peer group benchmarking policies. In regards to the latter, it commented:

> **中文：** ISS 在研究报告中指出了两个高度关切的领域：薪酬与业绩评价，以及同业组基准比较政策。对于后一个问题，ISS 评论道：

“The proxy states that the company intends to have direct remuneration at the 75th percentile of comparators for the high levels of performance that the company targets. Shareholders should note, however, as illustrated in ‘Company Selected Peers’ [a chart on p.5 of the report that shows that only 1 of the 14 peers is smaller in revenues] the company’s competitive benchmarking peer group includes a number of companies that are significantly larger in terms of revenue. Above-median benchmarking and the inclusion of larger companies may have the effect of increasing compensation without providing a strong link to performance.” (ISS research report on Minerals Technologies, May 2, 2012, p. 13)

> **中文：** “委托书称，鉴于公司设定了较高的业绩目标，公司计划将直接薪酬设定在参照公司的第 75 百分位数。然而，股东应当注意，正如‘公司选定的同业公司’所示［报告第 5 页的一幅图表表明，14 家同业公司中仅有 1 家的收入规模较小］，公司的竞争性基准同业组包含若干收入规模显著更大的公司。采用高于中位数的基准并纳入规模更大的公司，可能会产生提高薪酬却未能使其与业绩紧密挂钩的效果。”（ISS 关于 Minerals Technologies 的研究报告，2012 年 5 月 2 日，第 13 页）

In response, Minerals Technologies writes in its subsequent proxy filing in April 2013 that it had consulted with major shareholders and with ISS and had implemented changes to its peer group so that it aligned more in firm size and industry classification:

> **中文：** 作为回应，Minerals Technologies 在随后于 2013 年 4 月提交的委托书文件中表示，公司已征询主要股东和 ISS 的意见，并调整了同业组，使其在公司规模和行业分类方面更加匹配：

“At our 2012 Annual Meeting, our shareholders approved the 2011 compensation of our named executive officers with 56.4% of the shares voting on the matter at the meeting voting in favor. While our 2012 “Say-on-Pay” proposal passed, there were a significant number of votes against the proposal, which likely resulted from a negative recommendation the proposal received from Institutional Shareholder Services (ISS).

> **中文：** “在 2012 年年度股东大会上，就该事项进行投票的股份中有 56.4% 投票赞成，股东由此批准了我们指定高管 2011 年度的薪酬。尽管我们 2012 年的‘薪酬话语权’提案获得通过，但仍有大量股份投票反对该提案，这很可能是因为该提案收到了 Institutional Shareholder Services（ISS）的负面建议。

We conducted an extensive outreach program in connection with our 2012 Say-on-Pay proposal, including contacting all of our top 25 shareholders, to explain the compensation program to our shareholder base. We were pleased that, as a result, a majority of our shareholders voted in favor of the proposal.

> **中文：** 围绕 2012 年薪酬话语权提案，我们开展了广泛的股东沟通活动，其中包括联系全部前 25 大股东，以向股东群体解释薪酬计划。令我们欣慰的是，多数股东最终投票支持该提案。

Since our 2012 annual meeting of shareholders, we have continued our extensive engagement with our shareholders, including contacting all of our top 45 shareholders, as well as with ISS to determine how our corporate governance and compensation practices can be improved. While many of our shareholders were pleased with the overall design of our compensation program, other shareholders had suggestions for improvement.

> **中文：** 自 2012 年年度股东大会以来，我们继续与股东广泛沟通，其中包括联系全部前 45 大股东；同时，我们也与 ISS 沟通，以确定如何改进公司治理和薪酬实践。许多股东对薪酬计划的整体设计表示满意，但也有一些股东提出了改进建议。

Our Board of Directors and Compensation Committee carefully reviewed these suggestions, and made the following changes to our executive compensation program during 2012:

> **中文：** 董事会和薪酬委员会认真审议了这些建议，并在 2012 年对高管薪酬计划作出以下调整：

- Most significantly, we performed a careful analysis of the peer companies we use to provide benchmarks regarding remuneration through our executive compensation program at a level appropriate for the markets we compete in. This has resulted in significant changes to the composition of our peer group to ensure that we use the most appropriate comparators for designing our program and making appropriate compensation decisions. See page 49 for further discussion of our peer group.”

> **中文：** 最重要的是，我们认真分析了用于提供薪酬基准的同业公司，以确保高管薪酬计划的薪酬水平适合我们参与竞争的市场。这促使我们大幅调整同业组构成，以确保在设计薪酬计划和作出适当薪酬决策时采用最合适的参照公司。有关同业组的进一步讨论，请参见第 49 页。”

[On page 49 then]

> **中文：** ［随后在第 49 页］

“As a result of our outreach to our shareholders in 2012, we substantially revised the comparator group used for determining our compensation program. The Company’s primary business competitors are foreign companies, privately held firms or subsidiaries of publicly-traded companies. Accordingly, compensation data for most of our primary business competitors is not publicly available.

> **中文：** “作为 2012 年股东沟通活动的结果，我们大幅调整了用于确定薪酬计划的参照公司组。本公司的主要业务竞争者是外国公司、非上市公司或上市公司的子公司。因此，我们大多数主要业务竞争者的薪酬数据无法公开获得。

Therefore, based on information and analysis provided by the Committee’s independent executive compensation consultant, Steven Hall & Partners, we identified the following group of comparator companies for reference in setting compensation.

> **中文：** 因此，根据委员会的独立高管薪酬顾问 Steven Hall & Partners 提供的信息和分析，我们确定了以下参照公司组，以供设定薪酬时参考。

We selected these companies because they are primarily in the specialty chemical industry, they provide a broad measure of compensation in the market in which we compete for talent, they are similar to the Company in the scope of their operations, and they reflect a generally accepted range of revenue and market capitalization for an appropriately-sized peer group. Our independent compensation consultant has reviewed and supports this peer group.” (DEF14A filing by Minerals Technology Inc., April 3, 2013; pp. 4, 49)

> **中文：** 我们选择这些公司，是因为它们主要属于特种化学品行业，能够广泛反映我们参与人才竞争的市场中的薪酬水平，其经营范围与本公司相似，而且其收入和市场资本总额处于规模适当的同业组通常可接受的范围内。我们的独立薪酬顾问已经审查并支持这一同业组。”（Minerals Technology Inc. 提交的 DEF14A 文件，2013 年 4 月 3 日，第 4、49 页）

For the following fiscal year, ISS again recommended a “for” vote recommendation for the company’s say on pay vote and shareholder vote support climbed to 87.0 percent. The 2012 peer group restructuring led to an increase in reciprocal benchmarking from 21 percent to 52 percent.

> **中文：** 在随后的财政年度，ISS 再次对该公司的薪酬话语权投票提出“赞成”建议，股东投票支持率上升至 87.0%。2012 年的同业组重组使互惠基准比较比例从 21% 上升至 52%。

# Figure IA.1: Pay dispersion in high- versus low-option-use industries

> **中文：** 图 IA.1：高期权使用行业与低期权使用行业的薪酬离散度

This figure shows CEO pay dispersion separately for industries that make above- versus below-median use of stock options in a given year.

> **中文：** 本图分别展示在特定年度股票期权使用程度高于和低于中位数的行业中的 CEO 薪酬离散度。

For a given firm, stock option usage is defined as the fraction of total CEO pay that is due to option-based pay. We then average stock option usage for all firms in a given industry-year group.

> **中文：** 对于给定公司，股票期权使用程度定义为期权薪酬占 CEO 总薪酬的比例。随后，我们计算给定行业-年度组内所有公司的股票期权使用程度平均值。

Industry definitions are based on GICS6 classifications. We require at least 10 firms in a GICS6-year group.

> **中文：** 行业定义基于 GICS6 分类。我们要求每个 GICS6-年度组至少包含 10 家公司。

Pay dispersion in low option-use industries

> **中文：** 低期权使用行业的薪酬离散度

Pay dispersion in high option-use industries

> **中文：** 高期权使用行业的薪酬离散度

# Figure IA.2: Pay dispersion and mega grants

> **中文：** 图 IA.2：薪酬离散度与巨额授予

Panel A plots the frequency of equity-based mega grants for CEOs between 1996 and 2023.

> **中文：** 图 A 绘制了 1996 至 2023 年 CEO 获得股权型巨额授予的频率。

Panel B plots (i) pay dispersion when excluding all stock- and option-based pay (thick solid line) and (ii) pay dispersion after excluding firm-years with mega grants.

> **中文：** 图 B 绘制了：（i）剔除全部股票薪酬和期权薪酬后的薪酬离散度（粗实线）；以及（ii）剔除存在巨额授予的公司-年度观测值后的薪酬离散度。

We define mega grants as equity grants (i.e., stock plus option grants) that are either larger than 50 million USD in nominal terms (definition 1) or that are larger than 1% of the firm’s market value of equity (definition 2).

> **中文：** 我们将巨额授予定义为名义金额超过 5,000 万美元（定义 1），或者超过公司权益市场价值 1%（定义 2）的股权授予，即股票授予与期权授予之和。

Multi-year mega grants further require no additional equity-based pay in at least the year immediately following the initial mega grant.

> **中文：** 多年度巨额授予还要求至少在首次巨额授予后的下一年度不存在额外的股权型薪酬。

Figure IA.3: Variation in firm characteristics

> **中文：** 图 IA.3：公司特征的差异

This figure shows the variation in firm characteristics and the dispersion of CEO pay for S&P 1500 firms. Variables that are measured as ratios or that are percentages (e.g., Stock return) are stationary; hence dispersion is measured via their standard deviation in a given year. For non-stationary variables (e.g., CEO pay, Log assets and Log market value of equity) that increase over time, we first divide the values by the median value in a given year before we compute the standard deviation to obtain their dispersion. All variables (except Log values) are winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles.

> **中文：** 本图展示了 S&P 1500 公司特征的差异和 CEO 薪酬的离散度。以比率或百分比衡量的变量（例如股票回报率）是平稳的；因此，其离散度以相应年份的标准差衡量。对于随时间增长的非平稳变量（例如 CEO 薪酬、资产对数和权益市场价值对数），我们先将其数值除以相应年份的中位数，再计算标准差以得到其离散度。除对数值外，所有变量均在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。

Figure IA.4: Pay dispersion within industries

> **中文：** 图 IA.4：行业内薪酬离散度

Panel A plots CEO pay dispersion separately for all GICS2 industries excluding utilities. Panel B plots the average of within-industry pay dispersions for different industry definitions. CEO pay dispersion is measured as the standard deviation of firms’ Pay, which is calculated as CEO pay (TDC1) divided by its median value in a given year and winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles. We remove utilities and require at least 10 firms in an industry in a given year to be included in the sample.

> **中文：** 面板 A 分别绘制了除公用事业以外所有 GICS2 行业的 CEO 薪酬离散度。面板 B 绘制了采用不同的行业定义时，行业内薪酬离散度的平均值。CEO 薪酬离散度以公司 `Pay` 的标准差衡量；`Pay` 的计算方法是将 CEO 薪酬（TDC1）除以其在相应年份的中位数，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。我们剔除公用事业公司，并要求相应年份的一个行业中至少有 10 家公司，方可纳入样本。

## Source Page 68

Figure IA.5: Realized pay dispersion

> **中文：** 图 IA.5：已实现薪酬的离散度

This figure shows dispersion in realized CEO pay between 2006 and 2023 for Execucomp firms (a lack of detailed pay data prevents its computation pre-2006). Realized pay v1 is defined as total CEO pay reported in the DEF14 filing to the SEC, except that grant date fair values of stock and option awards are replaced with the value of stocks vested during the year and the value realized from options exercised during the year (=Execucomp item TOTAL ALT2), winsorized at the 5th and 95th percentiles. Realized pay v2 follows the definition of the CAP2 measure (CAP=“Compensation Actually Paid”) by Carter and Pawliczek (2023). This measure makes the following changes to the reported pay: (i) recalculates the value of stock and option grants made at the start of the year by multiplying their value with the percent of stock price appreciation that occurred during the year, (ii) adds the change in the value of outstanding unvested stock and options by multiplying the number of units times the stock price appreciation during the year, and (iii) adds the change in the value of shares vested during the year (i.e., value of vested shares minus number of shares vested times price at the beginning of the year). The measure is winsorized at the 5th and 95th percentiles. Finally, to compute the dispersion of both measures, we scale each measure by its median value in a given year and take the standard deviation of the scaled measure. For further details, please see the Variable appendix.

> **中文：** 本图展示了 Execucomp 公司在 2006—2023 年间已实现 CEO 薪酬的离散度（由于缺少详细的薪酬数据，无法计算 2006 年以前的该指标）。已实现薪酬 v1 定义为公司向 SEC 提交的 DEF14 文件中报告的 CEO 薪酬总额，但将股票和期权奖励的授予日公允价值替换为年内归属股票的价值以及年内行权期权的已实现价值（=Execucomp 项目 `TOTAL ALT2`），并在第 5 和第 95 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。已实现薪酬 v2 遵循 Carter and Pawliczek (2023) 对 CAP2 指标的定义，其中 CAP 表示“实际支付的薪酬”（Compensation Actually Paid）。该指标对报告薪酬作出以下调整：(i) 将年初授予的股票和期权的价值乘以年内股票价格升值百分比，重新计算其价值；(ii) 将尚未归属的流通在外股票和期权的单位数量乘以年内股票价格升值额，并加入其价值变动；(iii) 加入年内已归属股份的价值变动，即已归属股份的价值减去已归属股份数量与年初价格的乘积。该指标在第 5 和第 95 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。最后，在计算两个指标的离散度时，我们将每个指标除以其在相应年份的中位数，并计算缩放后指标的标准差。更多详细信息请参见变量附录。

Figure IA.6: Alternative dispersion measures

> **中文：** 图 IA.6：替代性离散度指标

This figure shows the skewness of total CEO compensation (defined as TDC1) and the interquartile range of CEO pay (defined as TDC1 scaled by median TDC1 in a given year). The skewness measure is unscaled as skewness is a dimensionless measure of dispersion. The interquartile range (IQR) is the distance in a given year between the 75th and the 25th percentile of median-scaled CEO pay.

> **中文：** 本图展示了 CEO 薪酬总额（定义为 TDC1）的偏度，以及 CEO 薪酬的四分位距（CEO 薪酬定义为 TDC1 除以相应年份 TDC1 的中位数）。由于偏度是一种无量纲的离散度指标，因此不对偏度指标进行缩放。四分位距（IQR）是相应年份经中位数缩放后的 CEO 薪酬第 75 百分位数与第 25 百分位数之间的距离。

## Source Page 70

Figure IA.7: Extended simulation results

> **中文：** 图 IA.7：扩展模拟结果

This figure shows simulated CEO pay dispersion in the economy if firms were to follow ISS’s industry- and size-based compensation peer selection methodology and firms set their CEO pay to a given pay target percentile of such selected peers. Panel A shows the trajectory of pay dispersion for various pay target percentiles. Panel B shows the trajectory of median pay in the simulation for various target percentiles. The figures show that higher target percentiles lead to an escalation of average CEO pay (also known as the “pay ratcheting” effect) while pay dispersion declines in all scenarios.

> **中文：** 本图展示了如下情形下模拟得到的整体经济中的 CEO 薪酬离散度：公司遵循 ISS 基于行业和规模的薪酬同业公司选择方法，并将其 CEO 薪酬设定为由此选定的同业公司薪酬分布中的特定目标百分位数。面板 A 展示了不同薪酬目标百分位数下薪酬离散度的变化轨迹。面板 B 展示了模拟中不同目标百分位数下薪酬中位数的变化轨迹。图中显示，较高的目标百分位数会导致 CEO 平均薪酬上升，这也被称为“薪酬棘轮效应”；与此同时，在所有情景下，薪酬离散度均有所下降。

0.1  
8.0  
6.0  
4.0

> **中文：** 0.1

## Source Page 71

Figure IA.8: Changes in above- vs. below-relative sized peers

> **中文：** 图 IA.8：相对规模高于与低于核心公司的同业公司的变化

This figure shows the semi-variances of compensation peers’ relative sizes in firms’ compensation peer groups. Semi-variance is the variance computed only for observations that are either above or below the average and illustrates how variation changed on either side of the average. Red (blue) lines show the semi-variance in the relative sizes for compensation peers that are larger (smaller) than the subject firm. Relative size of a peer with respect to a focal firm is its size divided by the size of the subject firm, where size is measured as book value of assets, market value of equity or sales. All semi-variances are rescaled as of 2007.

> **中文：** 本图展示了公司薪酬同业组中薪酬同业公司相对规模的半方差。半方差是仅使用高于或低于平均值的观测值计算的方差，用以说明平均值两侧的差异如何变化。红线（蓝线）表示规模大于（小于）被评估公司的薪酬同业公司相对规模的半方差。一家同业公司相对于核心公司的相对规模，是用该同业公司的规模除以被评估公司的规模计算得到的，其中规模以资产账面价值、权益市场价值或销售额衡量。所有半方差均以 2007 年为基期重新缩放。

> 09.0

## Source Page 72

Figure IA.9: Clustering of compensation peer group networks

> **中文：** 图 IA.9：薪酬同业组网络的聚类

This figure shows different clustering measures of compensation peer networks at various aggregation levels. The network of compensation peer connections for the economy (Panel A) and average across industries—for various GICS industry networks (Panels B, C, and D). Reciprocity is the fraction of existing network linkages that are bilateral (i.e., point in both directions). Triangles are groups of three nodes that are completely connected. Transitivity is the number of triangles divided by the number of triads that exist in a network graph (triads are groups of three nodes that are connected in some way, while triangles are triads that are completely connected). Clustering coefficient is the number of triangles divided by the number of possible triads (intuitively, it measures how close a network graph is to a complete graph).

> **中文：** 本图展示了不同聚合层级下薪酬同业网络的不同聚类指标，包括整体经济中的薪酬同业连接网络（面板 A），以及不同 GICS 行业网络的行业平均值（面板 B、C 和 D）。互惠性是现有网络连接中双向连接所占的比例，即连接同时指向两个方向。三角形是由三个彼此完全连接的节点组成的群组。传递性等于三角形数量除以网络图中存在的三元组数量；三元组是以某种方式相互连接的三个节点组成的群组，而三角形则是三个节点彼此完全连接的三元组。聚类系数等于三角形数量除以可能的三元组数量；直观而言，该指标衡量一个网络图与完全图的接近程度。

05.1 52.1 00.1

> **中文：** 05.1 52.1 00.1

A. Clustering of economy network

> **中文：** A. 整体经济网络的聚类

2022 2020 2018 2016 2014 2012 2010 2008

## Source Page 75

Table IA.3: Size of industries and pay dispersion

> **中文：** 表 IA.3：行业规模与薪酬离散度

This table relates trends in CEO pay dispersion to the number of firms in a given industry. Time trend is defined in Panel A (in Panel B) as the fiscal year minus 1996 (minus 2007). In Panel A, Pay dispersion and Pay dispersion (abnormal) is computed at the industry level with industry fixed effects defined accordingly (i.e., GICS6, GICS4 and GICS2). The variable Number of firms in industry is the number of Compustat firms in a given firm’s industry (i.e., its GICS6, GICS4 or GICS2 industry, respectively), winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles. In Panel B, Pay dispersion and Pay dispersion (abnormal) is computed at the firm level (i.e., within firms’ compensation peer groups). Number of firms in industry-size group is the number of Compustat firms in the same GICS6-industry and within 50% and 200% of the market value of assets of the subject firm, winsorized at the 1st and 99th percentiles. For convenience in interpreting the coefficients, the variables Number of firms in industry and Number of firms in industry-size group are divided by 100. All models include a constant term. t-statistics in parentheses are based on standard errors that are clustered at the industry level in Panel A and at the firm level in Panel B. *, **, and *** denote significance at the 10%, 5%, and 1% levels, respectively.

> **中文：** 本表考察 CEO 薪酬离散度的变化趋势与特定行业中公司数量之间的关系。在面板 A（面板 B）中，时间趋势定义为财政年度减去 1996（减去 2007）。在面板 A 中，Pay dispersion 和 Pay dispersion (abnormal) 均在行业层面计算，并据此定义行业固定效应（即 GICS6、GICS4 和 GICS2）。变量 Number of firms in industry 是特定公司所属行业（即分别为其 GICS6、GICS4 或 GICS2 行业）中的 Compustat 公司数量，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。在面板 B 中，Pay dispersion 和 Pay dispersion (abnormal) 均在公司层面计算（即在公司的薪酬同业组内部计算）。Number of firms in industry-size group 是与被评估公司处于同一 GICS6 行业，且资产市场价值介于被评估公司资产市场价值的 50% 至 200% 之间的 Compustat 公司数量，并在第 1 和第 99 百分位数处进行缩尾处理。为便于解释系数，变量 Number of firms in industry 和 Number of firms in industry-size group 均除以 100。所有模型均包含常数项。括号内的 t 统计量基于聚类标准误计算，其中面板 A 在行业层面聚类，面板 B 在公司层面聚类。*、** 和 *** 分别表示在 10%、5% 和 1% 水平上显著。
